⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ FAZILAT-E-SURAH HUD ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1505)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

الۤرۚ كِتَـٰبٌ أُحۡكِمَتۡ ءَایَـٰتُهُۥ ثُمَّ فُصِّلَتۡ مِن لَّدُنۡ حَكِیمٍ خَبِیرٍ.

"Alim Laam Raa! Ye woh Kitab hai, jiski Ayaat Mohkam banayi gayi hai. Phir Sahib e Hikmat ba khabar ki taraf se tafseel ke bayan ki gayi hain."

(Surah Hud: 1)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Baqir (as):

"Jo shakhs har Juma ke Din Surah Hud padhega to Allah baroz Qayamat use Giroh e Anbiya ke saath mab'oos farmayega aur uske Naama e Aamaal mein koi laghzish marqoom na hogi (will not be written)."

(Kitab Sawabul Aamaal, Noorus Saqlain)

📚

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jo shakhs Surah Hud padhe to Hazrat Nooh (as) ki tasdeeq o takzeeb karnewale afraad aur Hud (as), Saleh (as), Shuaib (as), Lut (as), Ibrahim (as) aur Musa (as) ki tasdeeq karnewale aur unki takzeeb karnewale afraad ki ta'daad se 10 guna zyada use ajr dega."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

"...Beshak, Nekiyaa'n buraaiyo'n ko khatm kar deti hain.."_

(Surah Hud: 114)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلٰى هُوْدٍ الْمَمْدُوْدِ مِنَ اللهِ بِمَعُونَتِهٖ،......

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aaqa! Is Jaanisar ka Salam qubool kijiye jiski Rooh par fida aur uske Ahlo Ayaal Aapke Ahl o Ayaal par tasadduq.

Maula! Mein Waqae Shahadat ke baad paida hua, apni qismat ke sabab mein Huzoor ki Nusrat se mehroom raha, Aapke saamne Maidan e Karzar mein utarne walon mein shamil na ho saka, aur na hi mein Aapke Dushmanon se nabrdaazma (no fight) ho saka. Lehaza ab mein Kamale Hasrat o ando ke saath Aap par tootne wale Masaeb o Aalaam par afsos o malaal aur tapish e ranj o gham ke sabab Subah o Shaam musalsal girya o zari karta rahunga. Nez Aapke Khoon ki jagah is qadar Khoon ke Aansu bahahunga ke anjaamkar gham o Andoh ki bhatti aur Musibaton ke lapakte hue sholon mein jal kar khaakstar ho jaon aur yun Aapke Huzoor apni Jaan ka nazrana pesh kar dun....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

♦ QUR'AN KI AYAAT MOHKAM & MUFASSAL HAIN. ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1506)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

الۤرۚ كِتَـٰبٌ أُحۡكِمَتۡ ءَایَـٰتُهُۥ ثُمَّ فُصِّلَتۡ مِن لَّدُنۡ حَكِیمٍ خَبِیرٍ.

"Alim Laam Raa! Ye woh Kitab hai, jiski Ayaat Mohkam banayi gayi hai. Phir Sahib e Hikmat ba khabar ki taraf se tafseel ke saath bayan ki gayi hain."

(Surah Hud: 1)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat mein الۤرۚ Mubtida (Subject) aur كِتَـٰبٌ iski Khabar (Predicate) hai, aur baqi Sifat (Adjective phrase) hai.

Mafhoom:

أُحۡكِمَتۡ ءَایَـٰتُهُ:

1. Quran mein Mohkam Ayaat ki tadaad zyada hai jo kabhi Mansookh (cancel) nahi hoti.

2. Iski Ayaat mein Khuda e Hakim ki taraf se Hikmat shamil hai.

3. Mohkam Ayaat Aqeeda Tauheed, Adl, Nabuwwat, Imamat aur Qayamat ke mafahim par hai to ye mansookh nahi ho sakti.

4. Qurani Ayaat mein koi Tanakhus o Tazaad (Defects & Contradictions) nahi hai aur ye Balaghat (Literature) mein akheri darje par faez hain jiski Kainaat mein misaal nahi milti.

فُصِّلَتۡ:

1. Ayaat ko Suraton aur Ayaat ko Ayaat ke tahet laya gaya hai.

2. Ayaat ko yake baad digar (one after another) bheja gaya hai.

3. Insaani zarooriyat ki tafseel hai.

4. Is mein Halaal o Haraam ko alag kar diya hai.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Main apne baad apni Ummat ke liye 3 cheezo'n se darta hun. Pehli ye ke Qur'an ki ghalat Taaweel (interpretation) karenge, Aalim ki lagzish (ghalati) ko talaash karenge, ya Daulat ki wajah se sarkash (rebellious) ho jayenge. Main tumhe unse bachne ka tariqa bhi batata hun. Qur'an se taalluq rakho, uski Aayaat e Mohkamaat (ke jinke maani waazeh (clear) hain) par Amal karo; aur uski Aayaat e Mutashabihaat (ke jinke maani waazeh nahi) par Imaan rakho. Aalim ke sahi iqdaam (actions) ki itteba (follow) karo aur uski lagzish (ghalti) ko mat dhoondo. Maal ke liye Ne'mat ka Shukr ada karo aur usme se gharibo'n ke huqooq ada karo."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p175)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aaqa! Mein Shahadat deta hun ke: 'Aapne Namaz qayem karne ka Haq ada farmaya, Zakat ada ki, Neki ka hukm diya, aur Burai aur Dushmani se roka, Dil o Jaan se Allah ki Ita'at ki. Pal bhar ke liye bhi Uski Nafarmani nahi ki. Allah aur Uski Rassi se yun wabasta rahe ke Uski Reza hasil kar li. Hamesha Uske Ahkam ki nigehdasht o paasbani karte rahe, Uski Awaaz par Labbaik kahi. Uski Sutoon (pillers) ko qayem ki......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

🤲🏻

اِلٰھِیْ وَ سَیِّدِیْ فَاَسْئَلُكَ بِالْقُدْرَۃِ الَّتِیْ قَدَّرْتَھَا وَ بِالْقَضِیَّۃِ الَّتِیْ حَتَمْتَھَا وَ حَكَمْتَھَا وَ غَلَبْتَ مَنْ عَلَیْہِ اَجْرَیْتَھَا اَنْ تَھَبَ لِیْ فِیْ ھٰذِہِ اللَّیْلَۃِ وَ فِیْ ھٰذِہِ السَّاعَۃِ كُلَّ جُرْمٍ اَجْرَمْتُہٗ وَ كُلَّ ذَنْبٍ اَذْنَبْتُہٗ وَ كُلَّ قَبِیْحٍ اَسْرَرْتُہٗ وَ كُلَّ جَھْلٍ عَمِلْتُہٗ كَتَمْتُہٗ اَوْ اَعْلَنْتُہٗ

(Dua-e-Kumail)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ ISTEGHFAR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1507)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

أَلَّا تَعۡبُدُوۤا۟ إِلَّا ٱللَّهَۚ إِنَّنِی لَكُم مِّنۡهُ نَذِیرࣱ وَبَشِیرࣱ *  وَأَنِ ٱسۡتَغۡفِرُوا۟ رَبَّكُمۡ ثُمَّ تُوبُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡهِ یُمَتِّعۡكُم مَّتَـٰعًا حَسَنًا إِلَىٰۤ أَجَلࣲ مُّسَمࣰّى وَیُؤۡتِ كُلَّ ذِی فَضۡلࣲ فَضۡلَهُۥۖ وَإِن تَوَلَّوۡا۟ فَإِنِّیۤ أَخَافُ عَلَیۡكُمۡ عَذَابَ یَوۡمࣲ كَبِیرٍ *  إِلَى ٱللَّهِ مَرۡجِعُكُمۡۖ وَهُوَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَیۡءࣲ قَدِیرٌ.

"... Ke tum Allah ke kisiki Ibaadat na karo. Mein tumhare liye Uski jaanib se Daranewala aur Khushkhabari Denewala hun. Aur ye ke tum apne Parwardigar se Maghferat talab karo. Phir Uski taraf palat aao to Woh ek khaas muddat tak ke liye tumhe achcha Samaane Zeenat faraham karega. Aur har Sahibe Fazl ko uska Fazl ata karega lekin agar tum munh pherte ho to mein tumhare mutalliq ek bade haulnak Din ke Azaab se darta hun. Tumhe Khuda ki taraf palatna hai aur Woh har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai."

(Surah Hud: 2 - 4)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ye Ayat guzishta Ayat ke zikr se paiwast hai.

Maqsad ye hai ke Kitab ko isliye Mohkam o Mufassal banaya gaya hai taake tum bas Allah ki hi Ibaadat karo. Kitab e Muqaddas ka ma hasl (outcome) hi hai ke Allah ke alawa kisiki Ibaadat na ki jaye aur Anbiya ki Be'sat (bhejna) aur unki Tableegh ka pahla maqsad bhi yehi hai. Rasool Akram (saww) Allah ki taraf se Nazir aur Bashir hai. Maqsad ye hai ke jo Kalma e Tauheed ka inkaar karte hain Rasoole Khuda (saww) unke liye Azaab ki khabar denewale hain aur jo log Tauheed e Khuda wandi ka iqraar karen aur Isteghfar aur Tauba karen to AanHazrat (saww) unke liye Bashir hain aur Aap (saww) ki Basharat ye hai ke agar tumne Isteghfar aur Tauba ke taqazon par amal kiya to Allah Ta'ala tumhe Duniya mein achha Samaane Zeenat faraham karega aur har shakhs ko uski Fazilat ke mutabiq darajat ata karega. Allah Ta'ala ne Duniyavi fayde ko lafz " *متاع*" (Mata') se tabeer kiya hai jiske maani hain thoda bahut fayda. Yani Duniyavi fayda Akherat ke muqabile mein intehai kam aur qaleel tareen hai.

🚩

Allah ka Usool ye hai ke har Sahibe Fazilat ko Fazilat ke Darajat ata karta hai.

Imam Baqir (as) se manqool hai isse murad Hazrat Ali (as) hain. Yani tamam Sahibane Fazilat mein Hazrat Ali (as) Aala o Arfa Shakhsiyat ke Malik hain.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Khuda se sawaal (Dua) karo ke Wo tumhe Duniya mein tawangari aur aafiyat (wealth & safety) aur Akherat mein Maghferat aur Jannat ata farmaye."

(Wasaail ush Shia, v12, p52)

🚩

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jo Ali (as) se Mohabbat rakhe, uske liye Farishte Dua e Maghferat karte hain aur Jannat ke aatho'n (all 8) Darwaaze uske liye khol diye jaate hain ke jis Darwaaze se chaahe be-hisaab daakhil ho jaye."

(Shiane Ahlebait (as), p17)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنَّكَ قُلْتَ وَ لَوْ اَنَّهُمْ اِذْ ظَلَمُوْا اَنْفُسَهُمْ جَاۤءُوْكَ فَاسْتَغْفَرُوْا اللهَ وَ اسْتَغْفَرَ لَهُمُ الرَّسُوْلُ لَوَجَدُوْا اللهَ تَوَّابًا رَحِيمًا اِلٰهِيْ فَقَدْ اَتَيْتُ نَبِيَّكَ مُسْتَغْفِرًا تَاۤئِبًا مِنْ ذُنُوْبِي، فَصَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِهِ وَ اغْفِرْهَا لِيْ يَا سَيِّدَنَا اَتَوَجَّهُ بِكَ وَ بِاَهْلِ بَيْتِكَ اِلٰى اللّٰهِ تَعَالٰى رَبِّكَ وَ رَبِّي لِيَغْفِرَ لِي.

(Ziyarat Rasoole Khuda (saww) on Sunday - Mafateeh)

🤲🏻

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Fitno ki bhadakti hui Aag ko bujhaya. Logon ko Haq o Hidayat ki taraf bulaya, unke liye Hidayat ke Raaston ko Roshan o Munawwar karke wazeh kiya. Nez Aapne Allah ke Raaste mein Jihad karne ka Haq ada kar diya.

Aaqa! Mein Dilo Jaan se Gawahi deta hun ke: Aap hamesha Dil se Allah ke Farmabardar rahe. Aapne hamesha apne Jadd e Amjad (saww) ki itteba aur pairavi ki, Apne Walid e Majid ke Irshadaat ko suna aur us par amal kiya. Bhai ki Wasiyyat ki tezi se takmeel ki. Deem ke Sutoon (pillers) ko buland kiya. Baghawaton ka qila qama kiya, nez Sarkashon aur Baghiyon ki sarkoobi ki....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦ MUNH CHHUPANE WALE ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1508)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

أَلَاۤ إِنَّهُمۡ یَثۡنُونَ صُدُورَهُمۡ لِیَسۡتَخۡفُوا۟ مِنۡهُۚ أَلَا حِینَ یَسۡتَغۡشُونَ ثِیَابَهُمۡ یَعۡلَمُ مَا یُسِرُّونَ وَمَا یُعۡلِنُونَۚ إِنَّهُۥ عَلِیمُۢ بِذَاتِ ٱلصُّدُورِ.

"Agah raho! Ye log apne Seeno ko modte hain taake Usse chhup jayen. Agah raho! Jab ye Kapdon se apne aap ko dhanpte hain to jise woh chipa rahe hain aur jise zahir kar rahe hain use Allah khoob kaanta hai. Woh Seeno mein chhupe hue Raazon se waqif hai."

(Surah Hud: 5)

📚📖 😷

👉 Tafseer:

 Hazrat Imam Baqir (as):

"Rasoole Khuda (saww) Khana e Ka'aba ke Sahen mein baithe hote to us waqt Mushrekin Tawafe Ka'aba ke liye aate to woh apne Munh par Kapda dal lete the taake Rasoole Khuda (saww) unhe na pahchan saken."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕋

Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Hazrat Ali (as) ki koi Fazilat bayan karte to Munafiq apne Kapde sametne lag jate the. Chunanche Allah ne is Ayat mein unki isi haalat ko bayan kiya hai.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

😷

Ayat ka mafhoom ye hai ke tum agar kisi ko sataate ho ya koi aur Gunah ka irtikaab karte ho to aisa hota hai ke to usse Munh churate hai, Munh dhak kar chalte ho. Aapne kisi ka Qarz ada nahi kar ra rahe to usse Munh chhupa kar chaloge. Lekin Allah sab kuchh dekhta hai usse Munh nahi chhupa sakte, Woh tumhare Man ki baat Jaanta hai.

😷

Dekha jaye to koi bhi Insaan Masoom nahi hai. Aajkal ye Corona ki Waba ne ham sab ko aisi haalat mein dal diya hai ke ham apna Munh chhupaye chhupaye phir rahe hain. Mumkin hai ye ham par Azaab ho ya hamara Imtihaan liya jaa raha hai. Nafsa nafsi ka Aalam hai. Har Insaan Bargah e Khuda wandi ke saamne bhooka pyasa khada hai, har Insaan is baat ka Muntazir hai kab koi Allah ko pyara ho jaye. Aaj Duniya ki badi badi taqat ne Khuda ke saamne ghutne tek diye hai. Bahut Ghuroor tha Insaan ko, Star War karna chahta tha, Nuclear Bomb par pura bharosa tha, sab chakna choor ho gaya. Ek na dikhne wale Virus se haar gaya.

Aisi haalat mein Momin siwai Khuda ke saamne tasleem (surrender) hone ke kuchh nahi kar sakte.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 😷

Imam Ali (as):

"Jab tak tumhare Naseeb achche hain, tumhare Aib dhake hue hain."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)

😷

Rasule Khuda (saww)

se ek shakhs ne arz kiya, "Main chahta hun ke Khuda mere Aibo'n ko zaahir na kare."

Aap (saww) ne farmaya, "Tum apne bhaiyo'n ke Aibo'n ko poshida rakho, Khuda Wande Aalam tumhare Aibo'n ko chhupayega."

(Adaab e Islami, v1, p238)

🤲🏻

Imam Ali (as):

"Aye mere Sardar! Ab main Tujhe Teri Izzat ka waasta de kar sawaal karta hun ke meri bad-amali aur bad-kirdaari, meri Dua ko Teri bargaah tak pahunchne se na roke. Aur Tu mujhe mere un poshida Raazo'n ke sabab se jinse Tu waaqif hai, ruswa na karna. Aur main chhup chhup kar jo buraiyaa'n aur bad-kaariyaa'n kar chuka hun aur meri daaemi kotaahi, meri jihaalat, meri khwaisho'n ki zyadati, meri gaflat ki wajah se mujhe saza dene mein jaldi na karna."

(Dua e Kumail)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"........Aap hamesha Ummat ke Naaseh ban kar rahe. Aapne Jaan sapari ki sakhtiyon ko Sabr o Tahammul aur barbadi se bardasht kiya. Fasiqon ka jam se muqabila farmaya. Allah ki Hujjaton ko qayem kiya. Islam aur Musalmano ki dastgiri ki. Haq ki madad ki. Azmayishon ke mauqe par Sabro Shakebayi se kaam liya. Deen ki Hifazat ki aur iske dayre kaar ki Nigehdasht farmayi........."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ RIZQ - SUSTENANCE ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1509)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَمَا مِن دَاۤبَّةࣲ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ إِلَّا عَلَى ٱللَّهِ رِزۡقُهَا وَیَعۡلَمُ مُسۡتَقَرَّهَا وَمُسۡتَوۡدَعَهَاۚ كُلࣱّ فِی كِتَـٰبࣲ مُّبِینࣲ.

"Zameen par chalne wala koi Jaandar aisa nahi hai jiska Rizq Allah ke zimme na ho aur uske rehne ki jagah aur uske sonpe jaane ko jagah (place of storage) ko Jaanta hai. Ye sab kuchh kuchh Kitab e Mubeen mein hai."

(Surah Hud: 6)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Duniya mein har shakhs ko apne Rizq ki fikr hoti hai aur puri Zindagi ise hi haasil karne mein guzar deta. Lekin ye uski Zindagi ka maqsad nahi hona chahiye, Rizq Allah ke zimme hai, Insaan ka kaam sirf ise halaal tareeqe se talaash karna hai. Insaan ka asl maqsad Ibaadat e Khuda Wandi hai

🐜

Kaynat mein hazaron qism ke Jaandar hain aur unki Ghaza ek doosre se judi hai. Allah Ta'ala tamam Ajnaas (types) unke nature aur aaza ke taqazon ke mutabiq Rizq faraham karta hai. Riwayat mein hai ke Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) ko Apni Shaane Razzaqiyyat dikhane ke liye farmaya ke is Chattan par Asaa par maaro. Hazrat Musa (as) ne Asaa mara to Chattan phat gayi. Andar se doosri Chattan namudar hui. Aap (as) ne us par bhi Asaa mar to wo phat gayi. Us mein se ek Chattan baramad hui. Aap (as) ne phir aisa hi kiya. Us mein se ek nannha keeda baramad hua. Uske Munh mein ek hara patta tha jise woh chaba raha tha. Hazrat Musa (as) ke Kaano se Khuda ne Hijaab hataya to Aapne suna woh Keeda keh raha tha: "Paak hai Woh (Subhanallah) Jo mujhe dekh raha hai aur mera Kalam sun raha hai aur meri maujoodgi se waaqif hai aur Woh mujhe Yaad rakhta hai aur mujhe faramosh nahi karta."

🍪🍵

Imam Mohd Baqir (as):

"Ek Baddu Arab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke khidmat mein hazir hua aur usne arz kiya: "Ya Rasoolullah! Mein ek Kasirul Ayaal (Big Family) hun aur Bhaiyyon, Behno aur Bhatijo ki kifalat bhi mere zimme hai, lekin mein intehai Ghareeb aur Muflis hun. Aap Allah Ta'ala se darkhwast karen ke Woh hamare halaat behtar banaye."

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne use tasalli di aur uske saamne ye Ayat padhi (11:6) aur uske Haq mein Dua farmayi."

"Ek shakhs ne Umar ki hukumat ke zamane mein use dekha to, us waqt woh Shaher e Madina ka Maaldar shakhs tha."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Hazrat Ali (as):

"Usne sabki Rozi baant rakhi hai. Woh sabke Amal o Kirdar aur Saanso tak ke shumar ko Jaanta hai aur Woh chori chhupi Nazron aur Seene ki makhfi hidden Niyyaton aur Sulb mein unke thikano aur Shikam mein unke sonpe jaane ki jagahon ka ahata kiye hue hai yahan tak ke unki Umren apni hadd o inteha ko pahunch jayen."

(Nahjul Balagha, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

وَ مَا مِنْ دَآبَّةٍ فِي الْاَرْضِ اِلَّا عَلَى اللّٰهِ رِزْقُهَا وَ يَعْلَمُ مُسْتَقَرَّهَا وَ مُسْتَوْدَعَهَا كُلٌّ فِيْ كِتَابٍ مُبِيْنٍ........

(Har Mahine ki pahli Tarikh ki do Rakat Namaz ke baad ki Dua - Mafateeh)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اجْعَلْ لِىْ مِنْ اَمْرِىْ فَرَجًا وَ مَخْرَجًا وَ ارْزُقْنِىْ مِنْ حَيْثُ اَحْتَسِبُ وَ مِنْ حَيْثُ لَاۤ اَحْتَسِبُ۔

(Taqibaat - Mafateeh)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aaqa! Mein Allah ke Huzoor mein Gawahi deta hun ke Aapne Minara e Hidayat ko qayem rakha, Adl ki Nashr o Isha'at ki, Deen ki madad karke use zahir kiya, Deen ka Mazaaq udane walon ko roka aur unhe qarar waqai saza di. Siflon se Sharifon ka Haq le kar unhe pahunchaya. Nez Adl o Insaaf ke maamle mein kamzor aur taqatwar mein barabari rawa rakhi....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

SHIA CHANNEL COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF IMAM SAJJAD (as)

**********************************

          25th Muharram 1442

  14th September 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦ KHILQAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1510)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهُوَ ٱلَّذِی خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ فِی سِتَّةِ أَیَّامࣲ وَكَانَ عَرۡشُهُۥ عَلَى ٱلۡمَاۤءِ لِیَبۡلُوَكُمۡ أَیُّكُمۡ أَحۡسَنُ عَمَلࣰاۗ وَلَىِٕن قُلۡتَ إِنَّكُم مَّبۡعُوثُونَ مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ٱلۡمَوۡتِ لَیَقُولَنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوۤا۟ إِنۡ هَـٰذَاۤ إِلَّا سِحۡرࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Aur Woh Wohi hai jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko 6 Ayyam (adwaar - period) mein paida kiya aur Uska Takhte Iqtedar Paani par tha taake Woh tumhe azmaye ke tum mein se behtar Amal karnewala kaun hai aur agar Aap kahen ke Maut ke baad tum uthaye jaoge to Munkarin e Haq ye zaroor kahenge ke ye to wazeh Jadu ke alawa aur kuchh bhi nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 7)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Aisi hi Ayat (Surah Yunus:3) hai jiski Tafseer ho chuki hai.

🌎

Imam Reza (as):

"Allah ne Arsh, Paani aur Malaika ko Aasmaan o Zameen ki takhleeq se pehle khalq kiya. Malaika apne wujood aur Arsh o Paani ko dekh kar Khuda ki Zaat ka istedlal karte the. Phir Allah ne Apna Arsh e Iqtedar Paani par qaem kiya, taake Malaika ko Uski Qudrat ka Ilm ho sake aur unhe maloom ho sake ke Allah har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai. Phir Allah ne Arsh ko Apni Qudrat se muntaqil kiya aur use Saat Aasmaano ke upar qarar diya."

"Phir Usne 7 Aasmaano aur Zameen ko 6 Dino (Adwaar) mein paida kiya. Khuda Chashme Zadan mein bhi paida karne ki Qudrat rakhta :tha lekin Usne 6 Ayyam (adwaar) mein isliye paida kiya taake Malaika ye jaan saken ke Aasmaan o Zameen tadreeji (gradual) taur par paida hue hain aur is darja bandi se unka Haadis (created) hona sabit kiya jabke har Haadis apne wujood ke liye apne Khaliq ka mohtaj hai. Allah ne Arsh ko Apni kisi ehtiyaj ki bena par paida nahi kiya. Woh Arsh aur Apni tamam Makhlooq se Be-Niyaaz (Needless) hai. Uske mutalliq ye kehna sahih nahi ke Woh Arsh par baitha hua hai. Allah Jism o Jismaniyyat (body) se Pakeeza hai aur Apni Makhlooq ki Sifaat se Munazzah (different) hai. Phir Allah ne Takhleeq e Insaan ka maqsad bayan karte hue farmaya: "Taake tumhe Azmayen....."

"Khuda ne ye nahi kaha ke Woh maloom karna chata hai ke tum mein se behtar Amal karnewala kaun hai kyonki Khuda to har cheez ka pehle se Aalim hai."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ne Mahine 12 muqarrar farmaye aur unke Dino ki tadaad usooli taur par 360 Din banti thi lekin is mein se Takhleequl Arz o Samaa (Creation of Heaven & Earth) ke 6 Din nafi (minus) kiye gaye. Isiliye Qamari Saal (Lunar Year) ke Din 360 se kam hain." (354 Days)

(Ehtejaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aaqa! Mein is baat ki Gawahi deta hun ke Aap: Yateemon ke Sarparast aur unke Dilon ki Bahaar, Khalq e Khuda ke liye behtareen Panahgah, Islam ki Izzat, Ahkam e Ilahi ka Makhzan (treasure) aur Inaamo Ikraam ka Ma'adan (Mines), apne Jadde Amjad aur Waalid e Maajid ke Raaston par chalne wale, nez Wasiyyat o Nasihat mein apne bhai jaise the......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

  15th September 2020, Tuesday

                ♦ KHILQAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1511)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهُوَ ٱلَّذِی خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ فِی سِتَّةِ أَیَّامࣲ وَكَانَ عَرۡشُهُۥ عَلَى ٱلۡمَاۤءِ لِیَبۡلُوَكُمۡ أَیُّكُمۡ أَحۡسَنُ عَمَلࣰاۗ وَلَىِٕن قُلۡتَ إِنَّكُم مَّبۡعُوثُونَ مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ٱلۡمَوۡتِ لَیَقُولَنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوۤا۟ إِنۡ هَـٰذَاۤ إِلَّا سِحۡرࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Aur Woh Wohi hai jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko 6 Ayyam (adwaar - period) mein paida kiya aur Uska Takhte Iqtedar Paani par tha taake Woh tumhe azmaye ke tum mein se behtar Amal karnewala kaun hai aur agar Aap kahen ke Maut ke baad tum uthaye jaoge to Munkarin e Haq ye zaroor kahenge ke ye to wazeh Jadu ke alawa aur kuchh bhi nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 7)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

"Ibtedai Takhleeq ke waqt Arsh Paani par tha. Allah Ta'ala ne Hawa ko paida kiya. Phir Qalam ko paida kiya aur use Hukm diya ke wo likhe. Qalam ne arz kiya ke kya likhun?"

Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:

"Jo kuchh Kainaat mein zahur pazir hota hai wo sab kuchh likho. Phir Allah ne Hawa se Tareeki, Roshni, Paani, Arsh aur Aag ko paida kiya. Usne Hawa ki qism ko" *ريح عقيم*" (Sakht Hawa) ko banaya. Phir tamam Makhlooqat ko Hawa se paida hone wali 6 cheezon se paida kiya. Allah Sakht Hawa ko Paani par Paani par musallat kiya, jisse badi badi Maujen wujood mein aayi aur Jhaag paida hui aur uska Dhuwan Hawa mein phailne laga."

"Allah ne Jhaag aur Mauj ko jam jaane ka Hukm diya. Allah ne Jhaag se Zameen banayi aur Mauj se mazboot Pahad banaye. Phir Allah ne Rooh o Qudrat se Aasman par Arsh sajane ka Hukm diya. Phir Allah ne Dhuwe ko jamne aur lambi saans lene ka Hukm diya. Phir Allah ne 2 Dino mein Aasman aur unke barabar 7 Zameenen paida ki. Jab Usne Makhlooq ka Rizq paida kar liya to Usne Aasmaan, Jinan aur Malaika ko Jumerat ke Din paida kiya. Zameen ko Itwaar ke Din paida kiya, Barri (Land) aur Bahri (Ocean) Makhlooqat ko Somwar ke Din paida kiya aur inhi do Dino ke bare mein Allah ne farmaya:"

"To kya tum Us Hasti ka inkaar karte ho Jisne Zameen ko do Dino mein paida kiya." (41:9)

"Allah Ta'ala ne Darakht (Tree), Darya aur Daryai Makhlooq aur Charind (Janwar) Mangal ke Din paida kiye. Aur Jinnat ke Jadd e Aala" Jaann" ko Hafte (Saturday) ke Din paida kiya. Parindo ko Budh ke Din aur Adam (as) ko Roze Juma ki chhe ghadiyon mein paida kiya. Al gharz 6 Dino mein Aasmaano Zameen aur un mein rehne wali Makhlooq ko paida kiya."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌎

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ne Itwaar ke Din "Khair *خير*" ko paida kiya. Allah "Khair" se pahle "Shar *شر*" ko paida nahi kar sakta tha aur Itwaar Somwar ke Dino mein Zameenen paida ki aur Zameeni Ghazaon ko Budh, Aasmano ko Budh aur Jumerat ke Dino mein aur Aasmaani Ghazaon ko Jume Din paida kiya. Ayat (11:7)"

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Rasoole Khuda (saww) se 2 Jumeraato'n aur darmiyaani Budh ke Roze ke mutalliq sawaal kiya gaya to Aap (saww) ne farmaya, "Jahaa'n tak Jumeraat ke talluq hai to us din Aamaal pesh hote hain aur Budh is lihaaz se ke is Din Jahannum khalq ki gayi, is din ka Roza Jahannum ki dhaal hai."

(Sawaabul Aamaal, p173)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻 Imam Husain (as) ke Sifaat:

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Maula! Aapki Shaan o Sifaat ye hain ke: Zimmedariyon ko poora karnewale, Sahebe Ausaaf e Hameeda, Jood o Karam mein mashoor, Shab ki Tareekiyon mein Tahajjud guzar, Mazboot tareeqon ko ikhtiyar karnewale, Khalqe Khuda mein sab se zyada Khoobiyon ke Malik, Azeem Maazi ke haamil, Aala Hasab o Nasab wale, Buland martabon aur be panaah Manaqib ka Markaz, Pasandeeda Namuna e Amal ke khaaliq, Misaali Zindagi basar karnewale, Bawaqar, Burdbar, Buland Martaba, Daryadil, Dana wa Beena, Sahebe Azm o Jazm, Khuda Shanaas Rehbar, Khauf o Khashiyyat aur Soz o Tapish rakhne wale, Khuda ke chahne aur nez Uski Bargah mein Sar newdanewale....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

         27th Muharram 1441

  16th September 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦ KHILQAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1512)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهُوَ ٱلَّذِی خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ فِی سِتَّةِ أَیَّامࣲ وَكَانَ عَرۡشُهُۥ عَلَى ٱلۡمَاۤءِ لِیَبۡلُوَكُمۡ أَیُّكُمۡ أَحۡسَنُ عَمَلࣰاۗ وَلَىِٕن قُلۡتَ إِنَّكُم مَّبۡعُوثُونَ مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ٱلۡمَوۡتِ لَیَقُولَنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوۤا۟ إِنۡ هَـٰذَاۤ إِلَّا سِحۡرࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Aur Woh Wohi hai jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko 6 Ayyam (adwaar - period) mein paida kiya aur Uska Takhte Iqtedar Paani par tha taake Woh tumhe azmaye ke tum mein se behtar Amal karnewala kaun hai aur agar Aap kahen ke Maut ke baad tum uthaye jaoge to Munkarin e Haq ye zaroor kahenge ke ye to wazeh Jadu ke alawa aur kuchh bhi nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 7)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

Raavi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya ke log kehte hain ke Arsh Paani par tha aur Khuda Arsh par baitha hua tha?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Woh Jhoot bolte hain. Agar is nazariye ko maan liya jaye to Khuda "Mehmool" (Uthaya jaanewala) qarar payega. Ye Sifat Makhlooq (creature) ki hai Khaaliq (Creator) ki nahi. Aur is baat se ye baat sabit hoti hai ke jis ne Khuda uthaya tha us mein zyada taqat thi aur Khuda mein thodi taqat thi, jabhi to uthaya tha."

Phir Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Allah ne Apne Ilm aur Apne Deen ko Paani par sawar kiya. Us waqt na to Aasmaan tha aur na hi Zameen bani thi aur us waqt na Insaan the aur na hi Jin the aur us waqt Shamso Qamar ka wujood nahi tha. Phir jab Allah ne Makhlooq ko paida kiya to unhe Apne saamne phaila diya aur unse kaha ke tumhara Rab kaun hai?"

"Sabse pehle Rasoole Akram (saww) aur Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ne jawab diya aur kaha ke Tu hi hamara Rab hai. Allah ne Apne Ilm aur Apna Deen unke sipurd kar diya. Phir Khuda ne Malaika se farmaya:" Ye Hastiyan Mere Ilm aur Mere Deen ki haamil (Carrier) hain aur Meri Makhlooq mein Mere Ameen hain aur ye Mas'ool (Jawabdeh - Responsible) honge. Iske baad Allah ne Aulade Adam (as) se farmaya ke tum Meri Ruboobiyat aur inki ita'at ka iqraar karo." Bani Adam ne kaha:" Hamne Tere Farman ko tasleem kiya aur hamne iqrar kiya."

"Us waqt Allah ne Malaika se farmaya ke tum inke Iqraar ke Gawah ban jao taake kal Roze Mehshar mein in mein se koi ye na kah paye ke aakhir ham kiya karte, hamare Aaba o Ajdaad ne Shirk kiya tha. Ham to unke naqshe qadam par chalne wale log the."

Phir Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Roze Misaaq (Day of Covenant) hamari Wilayat ki takeed ki gayi thi."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as) ke Ausaaf:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aap! Rasoole Akram (saww) ke Farzand, Qur'an ko Bachanewale, Ummat ke Madadgar, Ita'at e Ilahi mein Jafakash, Ahd o Misaaq ke Paband o Muhafiz, Fasiqon ke Raaston se door rehne wale, Husool e Maqsad ke liye Dilo Jaan ki baazi lagane wale, aur Toolani Ruku o Sujood ada karnewale hain....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

  17th September 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                 ♦ KHILQAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1513)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهُوَ ٱلَّذِی خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ فِی سِتَّةِ أَیَّامࣲ وَكَانَ عَرۡشُهُۥ عَلَى ٱلۡمَاۤءِ لِیَبۡلُوَكُمۡ أَیُّكُمۡ أَحۡسَنُ عَمَلࣰاۗ وَلَىِٕن قُلۡتَ إِنَّكُم مَّبۡعُوثُونَ مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ٱلۡمَوۡتِ لَیَقُولَنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوۤا۟ إِنۡ هَـٰذَاۤ إِلَّا سِحۡرࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.

"Aur Woh Wohi hai jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko 6 Ayyam (adwaar - period) mein paida kiya aur Uska Takhte Iqtedar Paani par tha taake Woh tumhe azmaye ke tum mein se behtar Amal karnewala kaun hai aur agar Aap kahen ke Maut ke baad tum uthaye jaoge to Munkarin e Haq ye zaroor kahenge ke ye to wazeh Jadu ke alawa aur kuchh bhi nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 7)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

Hazrat Ali (as):

"Phir ye ke Usne kushaada Fiza, wasee atraaf o aknaaf (suroundings) aur Khala (Space) ki wus'aten paida ki aur in mein aisa Paani banaya jiski Darya ki Maujon ki lehren toofani aur Behre Zakhar (Ocean of treasures) ki Maujen teh ba teh thin. Use tez Hawa aur tund Aandhi ki pusht (back) par lada. Phir use Paani ke palatne ka Hukm diya aur isse paband rakhne par qabu kar diya aur use Paani ki sarhad se mila diya. Uske neeche Hawa door tak phaili hui thi aur upar Paani thathe maar raha tha. Phir Allah Subhanah ne us Paani ke andar ek Hawa khalq ki, jis ka chalna banjh (fruitless) tha aur isse uske markaz par qarar rakha. Iske jhonke tez kar diye aur iske chalne ki jagah door daraaz tak phaila di. Phir is Hawa ko mamoor kiya ke wo Paani ke zakheere ko thapede de aur Behre Be-Karan (Sea of Beacon) ki Maujon ko uchhale. Is Hawa ne Paani ko yun math diya jis tarah Dahi ke mashkize ko matha jata hai aur ise dhakelti hui tezi se chali jis tarah khali Fiza mein chalti hai aur Paani ke ibtidayi hisse ko aakheri hisse par aur thehre hue ko mutlatam (turbulent) par palatne lagi yahan tak ke is mutalatam Paani ki satah buland ho gayi aur wo teh ba teh Jhaag dene laga. Allah ne wo Jhaag khuli hui aur kushada Fiza ki taraf uthayi aur isse Saaton Aasmaan paida kiye. Neeche wale Aasmaan ko ruki hui Mauj ki tarah banaya aur upar wale Aasmaan ko mehfooz chhat banaya....."

(Nahjul Balagha, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as) & Duniya:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aapne Duniya se is tarah Munh moda aur yun be etenai dikhayi jaise Duniya se hamesha ke liye kooch karnewale karte hain, Duniya se khaufzada log ise dekhte hain. Aapki Tamannayen aur Arzuen Duniya se hati hui thi. Aapki Himmat o koshish iski zeenaton se beniyaz thi aur aur Aapne to Duniya ke chehre ki taraf kabhi uchatti hui nigah bhi na dali. Albatta, Akherat mein Aapki dilchaspi Shohra e Afaq (famous) hai....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

                 ♦ KHILQAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1514)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهُوَ ٱلَّذِی خَلَقَ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضَ فِی سِتَّةِ أَیَّامࣲ وَكَانَ عَرۡشُهُۥ عَلَى ٱلۡمَاۤءِ *لِیَبۡلُوَكُمۡ أَیُّكُمۡ أَحۡسَنُ عَمَلࣰاۗ وَلَىِٕن قُلۡتَ إِنَّكُم مَّبۡعُوثُونَ مِنۢ بَعۡدِ ٱلۡمَوۡتِ لَیَقُولَنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوۤا۟ إِنۡ هَـٰذَاۤ إِلَّا سِحۡرࣱ مُّبِینࣱ.*

"Aur Woh Wohi hai jisne Aasmaano aur Zameen ko 6 Ayyam (adwaar - period) mein paida kiya aur Uska Takhte Iqtedar Paani par tha taake Woh tumhe azmaye ke tum mein se behtar Amal karnewala kaun hai aur agar Aap kahen ke Maut ke baad tum uthaye jaoge to Munkarin e Haq ye zaroor kahenge ke ye to wazeh Jadu ke alawa aur kuchh bhi nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 7)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

Hazrat Ali (as):

"Allah Subhanah ne apne Rasoolon ko Wahy ke imtiyazat ke saath bheja aur unhe Makhlooq par apni Hujjat thehraya, taake woh ye ye uzr (excuse) na kar saken ke un par Hujjat tamam nahi hui. Chunanche Allah ne unhe sachchi Zabanon se Raahe Haq ki dawat di. (Yun to) Khuda Makhlooqat ko achhi tarah jaanta boojhta hai aur jin Raazon aur Bhedon ko woh chhupa kar rakhte hain, Khuda inse be khabar nahi hai. (Phir ye Ahkam is liye diye hain) ke Woh un logon ko Azma kar zahir kar de ke in mein se Aamaal ke lehaaz se kaun achha hai taake Sawaab unki Jaza aur Eqaab unki Bad Amaaliyon ki Padaash (Punishment) ho."

(Nahjul Balagha, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Hazrat Imam Musa Kazim (as):

"Allah ne Makhlooq ko paida kiya aur Woh unke anjaam se bhi Ba-Khabar tha. Allah ne unhe chand cheezon ko baja laane ka Hukm diya aur chand cheezon se Parhez karne ka Hukm diya. Jin umoor ko Usne baja laane ka Hukm diya hai logon mein uske baja laane ki isteta'at (ability) bhi rakhi hai aur jin cheezon se Khuda ne mana kiya hai usse door rehne ki bhi logon mein qudrat rakhi hai. Albatta jab log iske Awamir (Commands) baja laate hain aur iski Nawahi (Prohibitions) se baaz rehte hain to is mein Khuda ka Izn shamil hota hai. Allah ne kisi ko Apni Nafarmani par majboor nahi kiya albatta Khuda Bandon ki Azmaish zaroor karta hai. Isse Woh ye dekhta hai ke behtar Amal karne wala kaun hai?"

(Kitab Ehtejaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi:

"Yahan tak ke wo waqt aa gaya jab Jor o Sitam ne lambe lambe dig bhar kar Sarkashi shuru kar di. Zulm tamam tar Hathyar jama kar ke sakht Jang ke liye amada ho gaya. Aur Baghiyon ne apne tamam saathiyon ko bula bheja. Us waqt Aap apne Jadd ke Haram mein panah gazen, Zalimon se alag thalag, Masjid o Mehrab ke saaye mein Lazzat o Khwahishat se bezaar baithe the. Aap apni taqat aur imkanat ke mutabiq Dilo Zaban ke zariye Buraiyyon se nafrat ka izhar karte aur logon ko Buraiyyon se rokte the. Magar, phir Aapke Ilm ka taqaza hua ke Aap khullam khulla Bai'at se inkar karen aur Fujjar ke khilaf Jihad ke liye uth khade hon......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

♦ UMMATE MA'DOODAH (313) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1514)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَىِٕنۡ أَخَّرۡنَا عَنۡهُمُ ٱلۡعَذَابَ إِلَىٰۤ أُمَّةࣲ مَّعۡدُودَةࣲ لَّیَقُولُنَّ مَا یَحۡبِسُهُۥۤۗ أَلَا یَوۡمَ یَأۡتِیهِمۡ لَیۡسَ مَصۡرُوفًا عَنۡهُمۡ وَحَاقَ بِهِم مَّا كَانُوا۟ بِهِۦ یَسۡتَهۡزِءُونَ.

"Aur Agar Hamne unse kuchh *makhsoos aur muqarrar kardah Giroh* ke aane tak Azaab ko taal dete hain to kehne lagte hain ke ise kis cheez ne rok rakha hai? Jab us Saza ka waqt aayega to ise unse hataya nahi ja sakega aur jis Azaab ka woh Mazaaq uda rahe hain, wohi Azaab unko gher lega."

(Surah Hud: 8)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ayat ka Sabhi Qur'an mein aam Tarjuma is tarah hai:

"Aur agar Ham ek khas muddat tak unse Azaab ko mu'akhkhar (delay) kar dete hain to woh kehne lag jate hain ke aakhir kis cheez ne ise roke rakha hai? Jab us Saza ka waqt aayega to ise unse hataya nahi ja sakega aur jis Azaab ka woh Mazaaq uda rahe hain, wohi Azaab unko gher lega."

📝

Jo Arabic ki knowledge rakhta hai woh samajh sakta hai ke jo hamne Tarjuma pesh kiya hai wo zyada sahih hai. Aam Tarjuma mein Ummat e Ma'doodah ka Tarjuma sahih nahi kiya hai balke Ummat Tarjuma mein hai hi nahi

👥

Tafasir mein Ummat se murad ek khas Giroh se liya gaya hai. Allah ne Azaab ko ek fixed numbered group ke aane tak taal diya hai.

👥

Riwayaat e Ahle Bait (as) mein "Ummat e Ma'doodah - *امت معدودہ*" se Ashaab e Qaem (atfs) murad hain. Jab ham Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Riwayat Imam Mahdi (atfs) mutalliq sunate hain ke jab unka Zahoor hoga woh Kuffar o Mushrekin, Ahle Bait (as) ke Dushmano se Inteqam be-Iznillah lenge, to woh mazaaq udate hain. Kehte hain Imam hote to zahir ho jaate aur Inteqam lete. Allah ne farmaya jab ek makhsoos ta'daad ka giroh aa jayega tab Imam zahir honge aur Zalimon par Azaab toot padega jise koi nahi rok payega.

🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ummat e Ma'doodah yani gine hue group ke afraad ki ta'daad Mujahedin e Badr ki ta'daad ke barabar hogi."

🚩

Imam Baqir (as):

"Asaab e Qaem ki ta'daad Teen So se kuchh upar hogi. Khuda ki Qasam woh Ummat e Ma'doodah hain aur unhi ke mutalliq ye is Ayat (11:8) mein ishara kiya gaya hai. Aur jab Khuda ka Hukm hoga to woh Kharif ke Badal ke mutafarriq tukdon ki tarah se ek doosre se mil jayenge."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ummat e Ma'doodah se Hazrat Qaem (atfs) aur unke Ashaab murad hain."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Imam Baqir (as):

"Jab Hazrat Qaem (atfs) ka Zahoor hoga to Allah Ta'ala Aapke 313 saathiyon ko Aapke liye jama kar dega aur woh Kharif ke Badal ke tukdon ki tarah se ek doosre se aa kar milenge."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Taqi (as):

"Hum mein se har ek Qaim hai, lekin woh Qaim (atfs) jiski ba-daulat Khuda Zameen ko Kufr o Ilhaad se paak karega aur Adl o Insaaf se poor karega. Uski Wiladat logo'n par makhfi (hidden) hogi. Woh khud ghayeb ho'nge hatta ke unka naam lena bhi durust na hoga... Ahl e Badr ki ta'daad mein unke Ashaab honge jo atraaf e zameen se unke paas jama honge aur Khuda ka qaul "Tum jahan bhi hoge, sab ko Khuda jama karega; yaqeenan Allah har cheez par Qadeer hai") (2:148) inhi par sadiq hai. Jab ye ta'daad (313) jama ho jayegi, to wo zuhoor farmayenge. Aur jab ta'daad 10000 (dus hazaar) tak pahu'nchegi, to Aap Allah ke izn (permission) se masroof e Jihad honge aur Dushmanaan e Khuda ko tahe teg karenge."

(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v2, p194)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Tabligh e Imam Husain (as):

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Chunanche Aap apne Ahlo Ayaal, apne Shiyon, chahnewalon aur Jaanisaron ko le kar rawana ho gaye. Aur apni us mukhtasar lekin ba-azm o hausla Jamaat ki madad se Haq aur Dalael o Baraheen ko achhi tarah wazeh kar diya, logon ko Hikmat aur Mauza e Hasana ke saath Allah ki taraf bulaya, Hudood e Ilahi ke Qayam aur Allah ki Ita'at ka Hukm diya nez logon ko Khabaes o Behoodgiyon aur Sarkashi se roka......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

♦ BADALTE HALAAT MEIN INSAAN KA TARZE AMAL ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1516)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَىِٕنۡ أَذَقۡنَا ٱلۡإِنسَـٰنَ مِنَّا رَحۡمَةࣰ ثُمَّ نَزَعۡنَـٰهَا مِنۡهُ إِنَّهُۥ لَیَـُٔوسࣱ كَفُورࣱ * وَلَىِٕنۡ أَذَقۡنَـٰهُ نَعۡمَاۤءَ بَعۡدَ ضَرَّاۤءَ مَسَّتۡهُ لَیَقُولَنَّ ذَهَبَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتُ عَنِّیۤۚ إِنَّهُۥ لَفَرِحࣱ فَخُورٌ *  إِلَّا ٱلَّذِینَ صَبَرُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ لَهُم مَّغۡفِرَةࣱ وَأَجۡرࣱ كَبِیرࣱ.

"Aur agar kabhi Ham Insaan ko Rehmat ka maza chakhane ke baad usse salb (Revoke) karte hain to woh mayoos ho jata hai aur Na-shukri karne lag jata hai. Aur agar use takleef pahunchne ke baad Ne'mat ka maza chakhate hain to woh kehta hai ke mujh se tamam Buraiyyan door ho gayin hain aur woh khush ho kar fakhr karne lagta hai. Magar woh log is kaifiyat se mustasna (exception) hain jo Sabr karnewale Nekokar hain. Unke liye Bakhshish aur bada Ajr hai."

(Surah Hud: 9 - 11)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

In Ayaat mein aam Insaani Nafsiyati (Psychological) kaifiyat ko bayan kiya gaya hai ke agar Insaan ko Ne'mat mil jaye to woh Na-shukri karta hai aur agar usse Ne'mat salb kar li jaye to woh Na-umeedi aur mayoosi mein chala jata hai.

In Ayaat mein Allah Ta'ala ne wazeh kiya ke yahan Ne'maat bhi intihai mehdood (limited) aur Hawa ke Jhonke ki manind hain aur Duniya ke halaat har waqt taghayyur pazeer (changing) rehte hain. Kabhi Sukh hai to kabhi Dukh hai. Kabhi mehfilen hain to kabhi Matam ki sadayen hain. Thode Dil wale Insaan Dukh ko dekh kar jaza faza' shikwe shikayat karne lag jate hain jabke Ahle Sabr aur Aamaal e Saleh ka zakhira rakhne wale afraad Sukh mein Allah ka Shukr karte hain aur Dukh ki ghadi mein Sabr karte hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Ali (as) ko Wasiyyat ki:

"Ya Ali (as)! Ek Momin mein 8 Khaslaten honi chahiyen:

(1) Dil hila dene wale halaat mein bawaqar rahe.

(2) Azmayish ke lamhaat mein Sabir rahe.

(3) Sukh ke waqt Shukr ada kare.

(4) Khuda ke diye hue Rizq par qana'at kare.

(5) Apne Dushmano par bhi Zulm na kare.

(6) Doston par apna bojh na dale._

(7) Uska Badan usse thakan mehsoos kare.

(8) Baqi log usse Rahat mehsoos karen."

(Al Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ وَ اَحْسِنْ لِيَ التَّوْفِيْقَ وَ نَفِّسْ عَنِّيْ كُلَّ هَمٍّ وَ ضِيْقٍ اَللّٰهُمَّ جَنِّبْنِيْ عِقَابَكَ وَ امْنَحْنِيْ ثَوَابَكَ وَ اَسْكِنِّيْ جِنَانَكَ وَ ارْزُقْنِيْ رِضْوَانَكَ وَ اَمَانَكَ وَ اَشْرِكْ لِيْ فِيْ صَالِحِ دُعَاۤئِيْ وَالِدَيَّ وَ وُلْدِيْ وَ جَمِيْعَ الْمُؤْمِنِيْنَ وَ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ الْاَحْيَاۤءَ مِنْهُمْ وَ الْاَمْوَاتَ اِنَّكَ وَلِيُّ الْبَاقِيَاتِ الصَّالِحَاتِ اٰمِيْنَ رَبَّ الْعَالَمِيْنَ۔

(Ziyarat Ibrahim bin Rasoollah (saww)

🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as) aur Itmaame Hujjjat

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Lekin log Zulm o Sitam ke saath Aapke muqabile par dat gaye. Aise aade waqt par bhi, Aapne pehle to unko Khuda ke Ghazab se daraya aur un par Hujjat tamam ki phir unse Jihad kiya. Tab, unhone Aapse kiya hua Ahd toda nez Aapki Bai'at se nikal kar Aapke Rab aur Aapke Jadd e Amjad ko naraaz kiya aur Aapke saath Jang shuru kar di."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

 21st September 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ AILAN E WILAYAT E ALI (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1517)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَعَلَّكَ تَارِكُۢ بَعۡضَ مَا یُوحَىٰۤ إِلَیۡكَ وَضَاۤىِٕقُۢ بِهِۦ صَدۡرُكَ أَن یَقُولُوا۟ لَوۡلَاۤ أُنزِلَ عَلَیۡهِ كَنزٌ أَوۡ جَاۤءَ مَعَهُۥ مَلَكٌۚ إِنَّمَاۤ أَنتَ نَذِیرࣱۚ وَٱللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَیۡءࣲ وَكِیلٌ.

"To shayad tum apni taraf bheji jane wali Wahy ke baaz hisson ko tark karne wale ho aur isse tumhara Seena isliye tang hua hai ke ye log ye kahenge ke is par Khazana nazil kyon nahi kiya gaya ya iske saath Farishta kyon nahi aaya. Aap to sirf Azaab e Ilahi se Daranewale hai aur Allah har cheez ka Nigran aur Zimmedar hai."

(Surah Hud: 12)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) Makkah ke qareeb maqam "Qadya" par pahunche to Aap (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) se farmaya: "Aye Ali (as)! Meine apne Rab sawal kiya ke Woh mere aur tere darmiyan Mawalaat (Continuity) qaem rakhe, Allah ne meri Dua ko qubool kiya. Meine apne Rab se Dua maangi, Woh mere aur tere darmiyan Mawakhaat (Brotherhood) qaem farmaye, Allah ne meri ye Dua bhi qubool farmayi. Meine apne Rab se Dua maangi ke Woh tujhe mera Wasi muqarrar kare, Allah ne meri ye Dua bhi qubool farmayi."

Quresh mein se Ali (as) ke Mukhalefin ne kaha: "Muhammad (saww) ki is Dua se to Teen Kilo Khajooren jo purani Mashk mein padi hui hon, hame usse zyada aziz hain. Iske bajaye Muhammad (saww) ne ye sawal kyon na kiya ke Allah uski Madad ke liye koi Farishta nazil kare aur usne Khuda se koi khazana kyon na maanga jisse use Faqr o Faqa se Najat mile. Muhammad (saww) apne Rab se Haq o Baatil ki jo bhi Dua maangte hain woh qubool zaroor hoti hai."

"Unki baten sun kar AanHazrat (saww) ko dukh hua aur Aapko Seene mein tangi mehsoos hui. AanHazrat (saww) ki is haalat ko dekh kar Allah ne Aap (saww) par ye Ayat (11:12) nazil hui."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚩

Jibrael Ameen (as) Shab e Arafa Rasoole Khuda (saww) par nazil hue aur Wilayat e Ali (as) ki Tableegh ka Hukm diya. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Munafiqeen ki Takzeeb (Denial) ke andeshe se apne Seene mein tangi mehsoos ki. Aap (saww) ne kuchh afraad ko mashware ke liye talab kiya aur un afraad mein mein bhi shamil tha (Raavi Zaid bin Arqam). Aap (saww) ne ham se mashwara talab kiya ke kya iska ailan Ayyam e Hajj mein kiya jaye? Jawab mein hamne kuchh na kaha. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Aankhon mein Aansu aaye. Jibrael (as) ne kaha: 'Muhammad (saww)! Kya Aap Hukm e Khuda pahunchane se ghabra rahe hain? Nabi Akram (saww) ne farmaya: "Mere Rab ko Ilm hai ke meine kitni aziyyaten sahi hain. In logon ne us waqt tak meri Risalat ka iqrar nahi kiya jab tak Khuda ne mujhe Izne Jihaad na diya aur meri madad ke liye Aasmaan se Lashkar na utaare. Ab ye log meri Ali (as) ki Wilayat ke iqrar par kaise amada honge?"

Jibrael (as) AanHazrat (saww) ki guftugu sun kar chale gaye. Allah ne apne Nabi ki tasalli ke liye ye Ayat (11:12) nazil farmayi.

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

(ne H. Ali (as) se farmaya) "Meri Wafaat ke baad logo'n ke Seene mein chhupe hue Keene (Dushmani) tumhare liye zaahir ho jayenge aur wo tumhe tumhare Haq se mehroom kar denge."

(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p151)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Ma'arka-e-Karbala:

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Lehaza Aap (as) bhi Maidan e Karzar mein utar aaye, Aapne Fujjar ke Laskaron ko rond dala aur Zulfiqar sont kar Jang ke gehre gubar ke Badalon mein ghus kar ghamasan ka Ran dala ke logon ko Ali (as) ki Jang yaad aa gayi. Dushmano ne Aapki Sabit Qadami, Dileri aur bebaki dekhi to unka Pitta Paani ho gaya aur unhone muqabile ke bajaye Makkari se kaam liya aur Aapke Qatl ke liye Fareb ke Jaal bichha diye....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ CHALLENGE OF QUR'AN ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1518) 📖

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

أَمۡ یَقُولُونَ ٱفۡتَرَىٰهُۖ قُلۡ فَأۡتُوا۟ بِعَشۡرِ سُوَرࣲ مِّثۡلِهِۦ مُفۡتَرَیَـٰتࣲ وَٱدۡعُوا۟ مَنِ ٱسۡتَطَعۡتُم مِّن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ إِن كُنتُمۡ صَـٰدِقِینَ *  فَإِلَّمۡ یَسۡتَجِیبُوا۟ لَكُمۡ فَٱعۡلَمُوۤا۟ أَنَّمَاۤ أُنزِلَ بِعِلۡمِ ٱللَّهِ وَأَن لَّاۤ إِلَـٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَۖ فَهَلۡ أَنتُم مُّسۡلِمُونَ.

"Kya ye log kehte hain ke us ne khud Qur'an ghad liya hai. Aap keh den ke tum is jaise 10 Sureh ghad kar le aao aur Khuda ke alawa jo bhi tumhare ma'bood hain unko madad ke liye bula sakte ho to bula lo agar tum sachche ho. Phir agar woh (tumhare ma'bood-deity) tumhari madad ko na pahunche to phir jaan lo ke ye Kitab Allah ke Ilm se nazil hui hai aur ye ke Uske alawa koi ma'bood nahi hai to kya tum Sare tasleem kham karte ho (become Muslim)?"

(Surah Hud: 13 - 14)

Same Ayaat jo guzar chuki hai:

(10: 37 - 38) (2:23-24)

قُلْ لَئِنِ اجْتَمَعَتِ الْإِنْسُ وَالْجِنُّ عَلَىٰ أَنْ يَأْتُوا بِمِثْلِ هَٰذَا الْقُرْآنِ لَا يَأْتُونَ بِمِثْلِهِ وَلَوْ كَانَ بَعْضُهُمْ لِبَعْضٍ ظَهِيرًا

وَلَقَدْ صَرَّفْنَا لِلنَّاسِ فِي هَٰذَا الْقُرْآنِ مِنْ كُلِّ مَثَلٍ فَأَبَىٰ أَكْثَرُ النَّاسِ إِلَّا كُفُورًا.

"Keh do: agar Insaan aur Jin mil kar is Qur'an ki misl (similar) laana chahen to is ki misaal nahi laa sakenge agarche is kaam mein ek doosre ki madad bhi karen."

"Is Qur'an mein Hamne logon ke saamne tarah tarah ki misaalen aur namoone (examples) pesh kiye hain lekin log inkaare Haq ke siwa kuchh nahi karte."

(Surat Al-Isra: 88 - 89)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

(Repeat Message)

Allah ne Challenge kiya hai ke is Qur'an ki ek ayat ki bhi misl koi nahi laa sakta chaahe sab Jinn o Ins ekathha hokar ek doosre ki madad karen. Ye permanent challenge har zamaane ke liye hai. Ye ek hamare Nabi e Karim (sa) ka permanent mo'jeza hai. Aur aaj tak iski misl koi laa nahi saka na laa sakega.

Detail ki yahan gunjaaish nahi hai,

Readers can read in detail in following links:

The Challenge of the Qur'an:

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/challenge-quran

The Scientific Miracle of the Qur'an:

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/scientific-miracle-quran

Some Brief Examples​ of Scientific Data in the Qur'an:

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/some-brief-examples-scientific-data-quran

Accuracy of Historical Records in the Qur'an:

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/accuracy-historical-records-quran

Predictions in Qur'an:

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/predictions-quran

Lack of Contradictions in the Qur'an:

https://www.al-islam.org/authenticity-quran-shaykh-muslim-bhanji/lack-contradictions-quran

(40 Hadith - Quran)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ بِحَقِّ هَذَا الْقُرْاٰنِ، وَبِحَقِّ مَنْ اَرْسَلْتَهُ بِهِ، وَبِحَقِّ كُلِّ مُؤْمِنٍ مَدَحْتَهُ فِيْهِ، وَبِحَقِّكَ عَلَيْهِمْ، فَلَا اَحَدَ اَعْرَفُ بِحَقِّكَ مِنْكَ.

(Shabe Qadr Aamaal e Qur'an - Mafateeh)

Bare Ilaha bawaste is ke Qur'an hamare saare Gunah Ma'af farma.

Jiske natije mein us ne Aapko Teeron aur Nezon se chhalni kar diya, aur intihai darindgi ke saath Aapko loot liya......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

        ♦ DUNIYA TALABI ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1519)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

مَن كَانَ یُرِیدُ ٱلۡحَیَوٰةَ ٱلدُّنۡیَا وَزِینَتَهَا نُوَفِّ إِلَیۡهِمۡ أَعۡمَـٰلَهُمۡ فِیهَا وَهُمۡ فِیهَا لَا یُبۡخَسُونَ *  أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ ٱلَّذِینَ لَیۡسَ لَهُمۡ فِی ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ إِلَّا ٱلنَّارُۖ وَحَبِطَ مَا صَنَعُوا۟ فِیهَا وَبَـٰطِلࣱ مَّا كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ.

"Jo log Duniyavi Zindagi aur iski khushnumai ke talib hote hain to ham unke Aamaal ka poora Badla yehin dete hain aur in se koi kami nahi ki jati. Ye woh log hain jinke liye Akhirat mein Naare Dozakh ke alawa kuchh nahi hai aur unke saare Aamaal akarat ho gaye hain aur unka sab kiya dhara Baatil ho gaya hai."

(Surah Hud: 15 - 16)

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke Wilayat e Ali (as) ke Munkarin ke Aamaal ka Badla Ham is Duniya mein hi de denge aur inse koi kami nahi ki jayegi.

🌎

Aksar Duniya mein ye bhi muzahera karte hain ke ghair-Mazhab log zyada maldar, aisho ishrat ki zindagi guzarne wale nazar aate hain. Jabke Mo'meneen Faqar o faqa, tangi, musibat o Bala mein mubtila nazar aate hain. Aisa kyon bas Ayat ka mafhoom samajh jayen.

🌎

 Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo shakhs Duniya ke husool ke liye koi Nek kaam karega to Allah Ta'ala use Duniya hi mein iska Ajr ata kar dega jabke Akherat mein uske liye Dozakh ke siwa kuchh na hoga."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌎

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Meri Ummat ko Zameen ki Hukumat o Iqtedar ki Bashaarat di ja chuki hai. Jo bhi shakhs sirf Duniya ke liye Amal karega, uska Akherat mein koi hissa nahi hoga jaisa ke Farmane Khudawandi hai: (11:14-15)"

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَاٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَاجْعَلْنِىْ لِنَعْمَاۤئِكَ مِنَ الشَّاكِرِيْنَ وَلِاٰلَاۤئِكَ مِنَ الذَّاكِرِيْنَ وَارْحَمْنِىْ بِرَحْمَتِكَ يَاۤ اَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِيْنَ۔ مَوْلَاىَ وَسَيِّدِىْ وَكَمْ مِنْ عَبْدٍ اَمْسٰى وَاَصْبَحَ فِىْ مَضَاۤئِقِ الْحُبُوْسِ وَالسُّجُوْنِ وَكُرَبِهَا وَذُلِّهَا وَحَدِيْدِهَا يَتَدَاوَلُهُ اَعْوَانُهَا وَزَبَانِيَتُهَا فَلَا يَدْرِىْ اَىُّ حَالٍ يُفْعَلُ بِهِ وَاَىُّ مُثْلَةٍ يُمَثَّلُ بِهِ فَهُوَ فِىْ ضُرٍّ مِنَ الْعَيْشِ وَضَنْكٍ مِنَ الْحَيٰوةِ يَنْظُرُ اِلٰى نَفْسِهِ حَسْرَةً لَايَسْتَطِيْعُ لَهَا ضَرًّا وَلَا نَفْعًا وَاَنَا خِلْوٌ مِنْ ذٰلِكَ كُلِّهِ بِجُوْدِكَ وَكَرَمِكَ....

"Aur hamko Apne Ibaadat guzaron mein, Apni Ne'mat ke Shakiron aur Apne Ehsanat ke yaad rakhne walon mein qarar dede aur Apni Rehmat se Meherbani farma. Aye Behtareen Rehmat nazil Karnewale. Khudaya! Kitne hi aise Bande hain jinki Subah o Shaam Qaidkhane ki tangiyon, Ranj o Gham aur lohe ki Zanjeeron mein guzarti hai. Jahan Qaidkhane ke zimmedar o nigran unhe karwaten badalwa rahe hain aur ye nahi maloom hai ke inka anjaam kiya honewala hai aur kis tarah unhe tukde tukde kar diya jayega. Woh Zindagi ki takleefon aur Hayaat ki tangiyon mein yun ji rahe hain ke apne Nafs ko hasrat se dekh rahe hain aur koi fayda ya nuqsan nahi pahuncha sakte hain, halanke mein Tere Fazl o Karam se in tamam baaton se aafiyat mein hun...."

(Dua-e-Joshane Sagheer - Mafateeh)

👆🏻

Ye Dunyavi Zindagi un logon ki hai jo Duniya ki nahi balke Akhirat ki chaah rakhte hain.

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Ma'arka-e-Karbala:

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Usne na to Aapke silsile mein kisi Ahd o Paiman ki parwa ki aur na hi Aapke Doston ke Qatl, nez Aap aur Aapke Ahle Bait (as) ka samaan ghaarat ke silsile mein kisi Gunah ki fikr ki. Aur Aapne Maidan e Jang mein sabse aage badh kar Masaeb o Mushkelat ko yun jhela ke Aasman ke Farishte bhi Aapki Sabr o Isteqamat par dang reh gaye......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ HAZRAT ALI (as): SHAAHIDE RASOOL ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1520)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

أَفَمَن كَانَ عَلَىٰ بَیِّنَةࣲ مِّن رَّبِّهِۦ وَیَتۡلُوهُ شَاهِدࣱ مِّنۡهُ وَمِن قَبۡلِهِۦ كِتَـٰبُ مُوسَىٰۤ إِمَامࣰا وَرَحۡمَةًۚ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ یُؤۡمِنُونَ بِهِۦۚ وَمَن یَكۡفُرۡ بِهِۦ مِنَ ٱلۡأَحۡزَابِ فَٱلنَّارُ مَوۡعِدُهُۥۚ فَلَا تَكُ فِی مِرۡیَةࣲ مِّنۡهُۚ إِنَّهُ ٱلۡحَقُّ مِن رَّبِّكَ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَ ٱلنَّاسِ لَا یُؤۡمِنُونَ.

"Kya woh jo apne Rab ki taraf se khuli Daleel rakhta ho aur uske peechhe uska Gawah bhi hai jo khud usi mein se hai aur isse pehle Musa (as) ki Kitab Gawahi de rahi hai jo ke Rahnuma (Imam) aur Rehmat hai. Woh is par Imaan rakhte hain as ur Insaani girohon mein se jo bhi uska inkaar kare to Dozakh uske liye Waadagah hai. Tum is mein shak na karna. Ye tumhare Rab ki taraf se Haq hai lekin logon ki aksariyat Imaan nahi rakhti."

(Surah Hud: 17)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne ne Rasool (saww) aur Imam (as) ki Alamaat (Signs) bayan ki hain. Rasool (saww) 'Sahibe Bayyana' hain yani khuli Daleel. Isliye sabhi Rasool ne apne zamane mein koi na koi Mo'jize dikhaye. Hamare Nabi ka Mo'jiza hai Qur'an e Kareem. Imam (as) ki 3 Nishaniyan hain:

1. Rasool ka *تالى* means follower ho. Nabuwwat is followed by Imamat. Jaise Chand Suraj ke ghuroob hote hi bila fasl namudar hota hai.

2. Imam Rasool ka 'Shahid', Gawah hota hai.

3. Imam Nabi ka Juz (Part) hota hai. Isliye Nabi Akram (saww) ne farmaya:

*عَلِىٌّ مِنِّى وَ اَنَا مِنهُ.*

🚩

 Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Mein Qur'an ki har Ayat ke mutalliq jaanta hun ke wo Din ke waqt nazil hui ya Raat ke waqt nazil hui aur kiske mutalliq nazil hui aur kin halaat mein nazil hui. Har Jannati aur Jahannumi ke mutalliq Allah ne Qur'an ki koi na koi Ayat nazil ki hai. Mujhe in tamam Ayaat ka Ilm hai."

Kisi ne poochha Aapke mutalliq kaunsi Ayat hai? To Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Kiya tu ne ye Ayat (11:17) nahi suni. Rasoole Khuda (saww), Allah ki taraf se Bayyanah hain, aur mein unka Shahid hun aur un mein se hun aur unke peechhe bila fasl chalne wala hun."

(Basaerud Darajat, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as): (Khutba)

"Us Zaat ki Qasam Jisne Daane ko shigafta kiya (Sprouted) aur Insaani Jaan ko paida kiya. Quraish ke jis bhi fard par Misaaq (Covenant) jaari hua hai uske mutalliq Kitabullah ki koi Ayat nazil hui hai to mein us Ayat ko usi tarah jaanta hun jis tarah se us fard ko Jaanta hun."

Kisi ne poochha Aapke mutalliq kaunsi Ayat hai? To Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Kiya tu ne ye Ayat (11:17) nahi suni. Rasoole Khuda (saww), Allah ki taraf se Bayyanah hain, aur mein unka Shahid hun aur un mein se hun aur unke peechhe bila fasl chalne wala hun aur mein unka Juz hun."

(Amaali Shaikhut Taifa, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ وَ صَلِّ عَلٰى وَلِيِّكَ الْمُحْيِيْ سُنَّتَكَ الْقَاۤئِمِ بِاَمْرِكَ الدَّاعِيْ اِلَيْكَ الدَّلِيْلِ عَلَيْكَ حُجَّتِكَ عَلٰى خَلْقِكَ وَ خَلِيْفَتِكَ فِي اَرْضِكَ وَ شَاهِدِكَ عَلٰى عِبَادِكَ..

(Salwat Abul Hasan Zaraab Isfahani - Mafateeh)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Ma'areka-e-Karbala:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Phir Dushman har taraf se Aap (as) par toot pada, usne Aapko Zakhmo se chur chur karke nidhal kar diya aur dam lene tak ki fursat na di, yahan tak ke Aapka koi Nasir o Madadgar baqi na raha aur Aap (as) intehai Sabr o Shakebai se sab kuchh dekhte aur jhelte hue yako tanha Apni Mukhaddarao Asmat o Taharat aur Bachchon ko Dushman ke hamlon se bachane mein masroof rahe......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

25th September 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ HAZRAT ALI (as): SHAAHIDE RASOOL ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1521)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

أَفَمَن كَانَ عَلَىٰ بَیِّنَةࣲ مِّن رَّبِّهِۦ وَیَتۡلُوهُ شَاهِدࣱ مِّنۡهُ وَمِن قَبۡلِهِۦ كِتَـٰبُ مُوسَىٰۤ إِمَامࣰا وَرَحۡمَةًۚ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ یُؤۡمِنُونَ بِهِۦۚ وَمَن یَكۡفُرۡ بِهِۦ مِنَ ٱلۡأَحۡزَابِ فَٱلنَّارُ مَوۡعِدُهُۥۚ فَلَا تَكُ فِی مِرۡیَةࣲ مِّنۡهُۚ إِنَّهُ ٱلۡحَقُّ مِن رَّبِّكَ وَلَـٰكِنَّ أَكۡثَرَ ٱلنَّاسِ لَا یُؤۡمِنُونَ.

"Kya woh jo apne Rab ki taraf se khuli Daleel rakhta ho aur uske peechhe uska Gawah bhi hai jo khud usi mein se hai aur isse pehle Musa (as) ki Kitab Gawahi de rahi hai jo ke Rahnuma (Imam) aur Rehmat hai. Woh is par Imaan rakhte hain as ur Insaani girohon mein se jo bhi uska inkaar kare to Dozakh uske liye Waadagah hai. Tum is mein shak na karna. Ye tumhare Rab ki taraf se Haq hai lekin logon ki aksariyat Imaan nahi rakhti."

(Surah Hud: 17)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Ali (as) ko Rasool ka Shaahid bataya hai.

🚩

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Ayat *وَیَتۡلُوهُ شَاهِدࣱ مِّنۡهُ* se murad woh Shahid e Paighambar hain, jo Khuda ki taraf se Bandon par Hujjat hai aur Nabi (saww) ka qaem maqam sirf wohi ho sakta hai jo Nabi ki tarah se Tahir ho aur Paighambar ka Janasheen (Vicegerent) aisa koi fard nahi ho sakta jiska daman Kufr o Shirk se maloos raha ho. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) se waada kiya tha "Mera Ohda e Imamat Zalemin ko nahi pahunchega." Jabke Shirk Zulme Azeem hai. To Ibrahim (as) ne ye Dua ki: "Mujhe aur meri Aulad ko But-Parasti se mehfooz rakhna."

"Aur tumhe maloom hona chahiye ke jo shakhs Munafiqeen ko Sadeqeen par aur Kafiron ko Saleheen par tarjeeh (prefer) de to usne Badtareen iftera kiya. Jab ke Allah Haq Parast aur Baatil Parast aur Paak o Najis aur Momin o Kafir mein bada farq rakha hai. Aur Nabi (saww) ke baad uski Masnad ka Waaris wohi ho sakta hai jo Nabi ki tarah Sidq o Adl, Taharat o Fazilat ka Sarchashma ho."

(Ehtejaj Tabarsi, Kitab Sulaim bin Qaes, Tafseer Ayyashi, Majmaul Bayan, Nahjul Balagha-Khutba e Waseela, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah ne hamari Wilayat ko farz qaraar diya hai aur hamari mohabbat ko waajib kiya hai. Khuda gawaah hai ke hum apni khwaaish se kalaam nahi karte aur na apni raai se kaam karte hain. Hum wohi kehte hain jo hamare Parwardigaar ne kaha hai."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p65)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ وَ صَلِّ عَلٰى وَلِيِّكَ الْمُحْيِيْ سُنَّتَكَ الْقَاۤئِمِ بِاَمْرِكَ الدَّاعِيْ اِلَيْكَ الدَّلِيْلِ عَلَيْكَ حُجَّتِكَ عَلٰى خَلْقِكَ وَ خَلِيْفَتِكَ فِي اَرْضِكَ وَ شَاهِدِكَ عَلٰى عِبَادِكَ..

(Salwat Abul Hasan Zaraab Isfahani - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

26th September 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦JHOOTE MUDDIYAAN♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1522)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

*وَمَنۡ أَظۡلَمُ مِمَّنِ ٱفۡتَرَىٰ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ كَذِبًاۚ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ یُعۡرَضُونَ عَلَىٰ رَبِّهِمۡ وَیَقُولُ ٱلۡأَشۡهَـٰدُ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ ٱلَّذِینَ كَذَبُوا۟ عَلَىٰ رَبِّهِمۡۚ أَلَا لَعۡنَةُ ٱللَّهِ عَلَى ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.

"Aur isse badh kar bhala aur kaun Zalim ho sakta jo Khuda par Jhoot tarashe? Ye log apne Parwardigar ke huzoor pesh kiye jayenge aur Gawah ye gawahi denge ke ye woh log hain jinhone apne Rab par Jhoot bandhe the."

(Surah Hud: 18)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Jitne bhi Jhoote Muddiyaan e  (Claimant) Nabuwwat o Imamat o Mahdaviyyat guzre hain ye Ayat un tamam afraad par mushtamil hai aur Allah Ta'ala ne unhe sab se bada Zalim qarar diya hai. Aur Qayamat ke Din Gawah ye gawahi denge ke in logon ne Khuda par Jhoot tarashe the aur in par Allah in par La'anat karega.

📚

Is tarah ki same Ayat:

(3:94), (6:21), (7:37), (10:17)

ke zer zikr ho chuka hai.

👁‍🗨

Imam Baqir (as):

'Khuda par Jhoot tarashne walon mein Quraish ke woh char Salateen murad hain jinhone ek ke baad ek Saltanat ki hai aur Gawahon mein se Aimma (as) murad hai."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

👁‍🗨

 Imam Baqir (as):

"Ayat mein " *اشهاد* (Gawahi Denewale) ham hain aur yun to har Zalim par La'anat hai, lekin Aale Muhammad (as) ke Huqooq Ghasb karnewale is mein sare fehrist hain."

(Kitab Al-Manaqib, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Is baat ka faisla kar diya gaya hai ke Ahle Imaan mein ikhtilaaf nahi hona chahiye isliye ke Allah ne unhe logo'n par Gawaah muqarrar kiya hai aur Muhammad Mustafa (saww) hum par Gawaah honge aur hum apne Shiyo'n par Gawaah honge aur hamare Shia logo'n par Gawaah honge."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p266)

🤲🏻

اِلٰهِيْ قَدْ اَحْسَنْتَ اِلَيَّ‏ اِذْ لَمْ تُظْهِرْهَا لِاَحَدٍ مِنْ عِبَادِكَ الصَّالِحِيْنَ فَلَا تَفْضَحْنِيْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ عَلٰى رُؤُسِ الْاَشْهَادِ......

(Munajaat e Shabaaniya - Mafateeh)

🤲🏻

Shahadat-e-Imam Husain (as)

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Yahan tak ke Dushman ne Aapko Ghode se gira diya Aap (as) Zakhmon se pash pash Jism ke saath Zameen par gir pade. Phir woh Talwaren le kar Aap par pil pada aur usne Ghodon ki sumon ze Aapko pamaal kar diya. Ye wo waqt tha jab Aapki Jabeen e Aqdas par Maut ka Paseena aa gaya aur Rooh nikalne ke sabab Aapka Jisme Nazneen dayen bayen sukadne phailne laga......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAQ KE MUNKARIN ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1523)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

......أَلَا لَعۡنَةُ ٱللَّهِ عَلَى ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ *  ٱلَّذِینَ یَصُدُّونَ عَن سَبِیلِ ٱللَّهِ وَیَبۡغُونَهَا عِوَجࣰا وَهُم بِٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ هُمۡ كَـٰفِرُونَ *  أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ لَمۡ یَكُونُوا۟ مُعۡجِزِینَ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَمَا كَانَ لَهُم مِّن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ مِنۡ أَوۡلِیَاۤءَۘ یُضَـٰعَفُ لَهُمُ ٱلۡعَذَابُۚ مَا كَانُوا۟ یَسۡتَطِیعُونَ ٱلسَّمۡعَ وَمَا كَانُوا۟ یُبۡصِرُونَ *  أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ ٱلَّذِینَ خَسِرُوۤا۟ أَنفُسَهُمۡ وَضَلَّ عَنۡهُم مَّا كَانُوا۟ یَفۡتَرُونَ *  لَا جَرَمَ أَنَّهُمۡ فِی ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِ هُمُ ٱلۡأَخۡسَرُونَ.

"Aagah raho ke Zalimon par Allah ki La'anat hai. Jo Khuda ke Raaste se rokte hain aur Uske Raaste ko tedha (crooked) karna chahte hain aur woh Akherat ke Munkir hain. Na Ye log Zameen par Allah ko bebas kar sake aur na Allah ke siwa unka koi himayati hua. Unhe dugna (double) Azaab diya jayega. Ye log Haq baat sun nahi sakte the aur na hi Haq ko dekh sakte the."

"In logon ne apne aap ko Nuqsaan mein dala hai aur jo kuchh unhone ghad rakha tha (fabricated) wo bhi un se kho gaya. Lazmi hai ke woh Akherat mein sab se badh kar Khasaare mein rahen."

(Surah Hud: 19 - 22)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imamat Allah ka Raasta hai aur jo log Raahe Imamat se rokte hain aur Raahe Imamat ko tedha karke Aghayaar (others) ki Imamat ke daawat dete hain, ye woh log hain jo Haq baat sunne ke rawadaar nahi hain. Aur ye log Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ka Zikr-e-Khair sunne par amaada nahi hain aur ye woh hain jinhone khasaara uthaya hai aur Qayamat ke Din unke ghadhe hue Jhoot unse kho jayenge.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaapan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Aye Ma'bood! Uske (Apne Wali e Amr (atfs) ke) zariye se hamare sino'n ko shifa de aur hamare Dilo'n se Bughz Keena mita de. Jis Haq mein hamara ikhtelaf hai, Apne Hukm se uske zariye humen Hidayat ata farma. Beshak, Tu jise chaahe Seedhe Raaste ki taraf le jaata hai. Uske zariye Apne aur hamare Dushman par humen ghalba ata farma. Aye sachche Khuda, aisa hi ho!"

(Dua e Iftitaah)

🤲🏻

Shahadat Imam Husain (as):

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"........Ab Aap (as) us mod par the jahan Insaan sab kuchh bhool jata hai. Aise mein Aap (as) ne apne Khayam aur Ghar ki taraf Aakheri bar hasrat bhari nigah dali aur Aapka Asp e Bawafa (Horse - Duldul Zuljana) tezi se hinhinata aur rota hua sunani sunane ke liye Khayam ki taraf rawana ho gaya......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              10th Safar 1442

  28th September 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ TASLEEM ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1524)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

إِنَّ ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ وَعَمِلُوا۟ ٱلصَّـٰلِحَـٰتِ وَأَخۡبَتُوۤا۟ إِلَىٰ رَبِّهِمۡ أُو۟لَـٰۤىِٕكَ أَصۡحَـٰبُ ٱلۡجَنَّةِۖ هُمۡ فِیهَا خَـٰلِدُونَ.

"Beshak woh log jo Imaan laye aur Nek Amal kiye aur Rab ki Bargah mein Aajezi karte rahe, woh yaqeenan Jannati hain, woh is mein hamesha rahenge."

(Surah Hud: 23)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Lafz " اخبات" ke maani Aajezi aur Gardan jhuka dene ke hain (Humbleness). Maqsade Ayat ye hai ke jo log Imaan laaye aur Aamaal e Saleh baja laaye aur Khuda ke Huzoor Sar Tasleem kham kar diya to Jannat mein jayenge aur woh us mein hamesha rahenge.

🕌

Raavi ne Imam Sadiq (as) se arz kiya ke "hamare paas ek shakhs rehta hai jiska naam "Kaleeb" hai aur jab bhi woh Aap (as) ka koi farman sunta hai to fauran kehta hai: 'Mein ise Tasleem karta hun.', Uski is aadat e Tasleem ki wajah se hamne uska naam "Kaleeb Tasleem" rakh diya hai."

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Khuda us par rahem kare. Jaante ho "Tasleem" kiya hai?"

Hamne arz kiya aap (as) farmayen.

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Khuda ki Qasam! Tasleem hi "Akhbaat - اخبات" hai aur aise hi afraad ke liye Allah ne farmaya, Ayat (11:23)"

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Allah kisi bande ko Ne'mat ata kare aur woh banda Dil se Tasleem kare aur pehchan le ke ye Ne'mat Allah ki taraf se hai to usne jaise Shukr ka haq ada kar diya."

(Mishkaat ul Anwaar (Urdu), p63)

🕌

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ka Deen naaqis Aql se, baatil Raai se aur Faasid Khayalaat se haasil nahi hota, balke ye Tasleem se haasil hota hai. Pus, jisne humen Tasleem (accept) kiya uske liye salamati hai, jisne hamari pairavi ki uske liye Hidayat hai aur jisne Qayaas aur Raai se kaam liya wo halaak hua aur jisne hamare Qaul (hamari Hadees) aur hamare faisle par apne Nafs mein tangi mehsoos ki usne Saba' Masaani aur Qur'an naazil Karnewali Zaat (Allah Ta'ala) ka inkaar kiya."

(Falsafa e Gaibat e Mahdi (atfs) , p174)

🕌

Imam Reza (as):

"Hamare Shia hamare hukm ke saamne Sar Tasleem kham karte hain aur hamare Ahkam ko baja laate hain, hamare Dushman ke mukhaalif hain. Pus, jo in sifaat ba-kamaal ka maalik nahi hai wo hum mein se nahi hai."

(Ausaaf ush Shia - Shaikh Sadooq, p22)

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Wilayat e Ali (as) ka itteba (follow) karna aur unki Wilayat ko tasleem karna tumhare umoor (affairs) ko pareshaan na hone dega, Adl o Insaaf ko tumse qaem rakhega aur aakhir tumko Jannat mein pahuncha dega."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p81)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww)

ne Imam Ali (as) se farmaya:

"Farishte hamare Khaadim hain aur hum se Mohabbat karne waalo'n ke Khaadim hain aur Haameleen e Arsh aur uske gird rehne waale Farishte hamari Wilayat ko Tasleem karnewalo'n ke liye Astagfaar karte hain."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p379)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّي اَسْاَلُكَ اِخْبَاتَ الْمُخْبِتِيْنَ، وَاِخْلَاصَ الْمُوْقِنِيْنَ، وَمُرَافَقَةَ الْاَبْرَارِ، وَاسْتِحْقَاقَ حَقَاۤئِقِ الْاِيْمَانِ، وَالْغَنِيْمَةَ مِنْ كُلِّ بِرٍّ، وَالسَّلَامَةَ مِنْ كُلِّ اِثْمٍ، وَوُجُوْبَ رَحْمَتِكَ، وَعَزَآئِمَ مَغْفِرَتِكَ، وَالْفَوْزَ بِالْجَنَّةِ، وَالنَّجَاةَ مِنَ النَّارِ۔

(Dua Khatme Qur'an Ramazan - Mafateeh)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Karbala mein Mukhadderat e Ismat o Taharat (Bibiyan) ka haal:

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"...... Jab Mukhadderat e Ismat o Taharat ne Aapke Duldul ko khaali aur Zeen ko ulta hua dekha ek kohraam mach gaya aur woh Gham ki taab na laate hue Khemon se nikal aayen. Unhone apne Baal Chehron par bikhra liye aur apne Rukhsaron par tamache marte hue apne Buzurgon ko pukar pukar kar Nauha o Girya shuru kar diya, kyonki is sangeen sadme ke baad unko Izzat o Ehteram ki Nigahon se nahi dekha jaa raha tha aur sab ke sab gham se nidhal Aapki Shahadatgah ki taraf ja rahe the......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                11th Safar 1442

  29th September 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ ANDHE, SUN-BEHRE ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1525)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

مَثَلُ ٱلۡفَرِیقَیۡنِ كَٱلۡأَعۡمَىٰ وَٱلۡأَصَمِّ وَٱلۡبَصِیرِ وَٱلسَّمِیعِۚ هَلۡ یَسۡتَوِیَانِ مَثَلًاۚ أَفَلَا تَذَكَّرُونَ.

"In dono Firqon ki misaal Andhe, Behre aur dekhne aur sunnewale ki si hai. To kya ye dono yaksaan (equal) ho sakte hain, kya phir bhi tum Nasihat hasil nahi karte?"

(Surah Hud: 24)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Mazkoora Ayat mein Allah ne do apposite firqo (Sects) ki misaal andhe aur dekhne wale ki di hai, dono brabar nahi ho sakte. Ab jo Jume ki Namaz Budh ko padha de woh to Jume ke Pesh Imam ke bhi brabar nahi ho sakta. Jange Jamal, Siffeen mein do fareeq aamne saamne, dono sahi to nahi ho sakte ek hi sahi hoga. Ye aise waqeat hain jo aankhwalon ke saamne hain lekin unhe Haq nahi dikhayi de raha.

Is tarah ki Ayaat ka ham guzishta Ayaat mein Tafseer pesh kar chuke hain, woh Ayaat ye hain.

Haq ko na pehchanne wale:

صُمٌّ بُكْمٌ عُمْيٌ فَهُمْ لَا يَرْجِعُونَ 

"Ye Behre, Goonge aur Andhe hain. Woh palat kar nahi ayenge."

(Surah Baqarah: 18)

📚

Ye Sun-Behre log hain:

"Aye Ahle Imaan! Tum Allah aur Uske Rasool ki Ita'at karo aur Hukm sun kar Ita'at se sartabi (ignore) na karo *aur tum unki tarah se mat bano jinho ne kaha ke hamne suna hai lekin woh nahi sunte."

(Surah Anfaal: 20 - 21)

📚

Guzishta Tafseeron mein rivayat pesh kar chuke hain ke Imam bhi Allah ki Ayat hain. Allah farma raha hai:

"Woh log jinhone Hamari Ayaat (Imams) ki takzeeb ki hai woh behre (deaf) aur goonge (dumb) hain. Woh tareekyon mein pade hue hain.* Khuda jiski gumrahi chahta hai Hukm kar deta hai aur jise chahe Siraat e Mustaqeem par khada deta."

(Surah An'am: 39)

Ye Munkarin e Ayat hain jo sun ke un-suna, dekh kar un-dekhi karte hain, Haq ka inkaar karte hain, isliye itne firqon mein bat chuke hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 👀

Imam Ali (as):

"Hamare haq ki Ma'arefat Momin ka chiraag hai aur sab se zyada Andha woh hai jise hamare fazaail nazar na aayein aur bila sabab (without reason) humse adaawat rakhe. Halaa'nki, hum ne logo'n ko haq ki Daawat di aur hamare mukhalefeen ne baatil aur fitne ki Daawat di hai aur kitna bad-naseeb hai woh shakhs jisne hamare mukhalefeen ki Daawat ko qubool kiya aur hum se jung ki."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p625)

👁️

Imam Ali (as):

"Jab Aa'nkhein Nafs ki pasandida cheezein dekhne lagein to Dil anjaam se Andha ho jaata hai."

@Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p193)

🤲🏻

Shahadat-e-Imam Husain (as)

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"........Afsos! Shimr Maloom Aapke Seene par baitha hua, Aapke Gulu e Mubarak par apni Talwar rakhe hue tha. Woh Kameena Aapki Reshe Aqdas ko pakde hue apni Hindi Talwar se Aapko Zibah kar raha tha! Yahan tak ke, Aapke hosh o hawas sakin ho gaye, Aapki Saans maddham pad gayi aur Aapka Pak o Pakeeza Sar Neze par buland kar diya gaya......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

  30th September 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1526)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَقَدۡ أَرۡسَلۡنَا نُوحًا إِلَىٰ قَوۡمِهِۦۤ إِنِّی لَكُمۡ نَذِیرࣱ مُّبِینٌ *  أَن لَّا تَعۡبُدُوۤا۟ إِلَّا ٱللَّهَۖ إِنِّیۤ أَخَافُ عَلَیۡكُمۡ عَذَابَ یَوۡمٍ أَلِیمࣲ.

"Yaqeenan Hamne Nooh (as) ko uski Qaum ki taraf bheja. (Usne kaha:) "Mein tumhare liye khullam khulla Daranewala hun. Ye ke Allah ke alawa kisi ki Bandagi na karo. Mein tumhare mutalliq Dardnak Din ke Azaab ka khauf rakhta hun."

(Surah Hud: 25 - 26)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat se Hazrat Nooh (as) ka waqea shuru hota hai.

🕌

Hazrat Nooh (as) ka asl Naam "Abdul Ghaffar" tha. Woh hamesha Aap par aur logon ki Gumrahi par Nauha kuna rehte the isi wajah se unka Naam "Nooh" pad gaya.

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Mohd. Baqar (as):

"Adam (as) ne apni wafat se pehle apne Farzand Shees (as), Haibatullah, ko bahut si baaton ki Wasiyyat ki thi aur unhone apni Wasiyyat mein Hazrat Nooh (as) ki aamad ki Basharat di thi aur farmaya: 'Allah Ta'ala meri Nasl mein se Nooh (as) ko Nabi bana kar mab'oos farmayega. Woh logon ko Khuda ki Wahdaniyyat (Unity of God) ki Dawat dega.' lekin uski Qaum use jhutlayegi. Allah Ta'ala unhe Tufaan ke zariye garq kar dega."

"Hazrat Adam (as) aur Hazrat Nooh (as) ke darmiyan 10 pushton ka faasla tha aur Hazrat Nooh (as) ke tamam Abaa Nabi aur Wasi the. Hazrat Adam (as) ne Haibatullah ko Wasiyyat ki thi ke apni Aulad se keh den ke jise Nooh (as) ka zamana naseeb ho woh us par Imaan laye aur uski Pairavi kare aur tasdeeq kare."

"Adam (as) ne apne Farzand Haibatullah se farmaya tha ke woh Saal mein ek Din muqarrar karen aur us Din ko apne liye Roz e Eid qarar den aur us Din woh Nooh (as) ki aamad se logon ko ba-khabar karte rahen. Isi tarah se har jaanewala Nabi apne baad aanewale ki Wasiyyat karta raha, yahan tak ye mamla Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) par ikhtetam pazeer hua."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Shari'at Tauheed, Ikhlaas aur Tark e Shirk par mabni (based) thi aur Aqeeda e Tauheed wo Fitrat e Ilahi hai jis par usne logon ko paida kiya hai. Allah ne Hazrat Nooh (as) aur deegar Anbiya Karaam se ye Ahd liya tha ke woh Khuda ki Ibaadat karen aur kisi ko uska sharik nahi banayenge."

"Hazrat Nooh (as) logon ko Namaz, Amr Bil Ma'roof aur Nahy Anil Munkar ka Hukm diya tha aur unhe Halal o Haram se aagah kiya tha. Allah Ta'ala ne unke zamane mein Shara'ee Sazayen aur Ahkam e Miraas ko nazil nahi kiya tha."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd.......)

🙇

Hazrat Nooh (as):

"Maine Duniya ko aisa Ghar paaya jis ke 2 Darwaze hain; main ek Darwaze se daakhil hua aur doosre se nikal gaya."

[H. Nuh (as) ne 2450 saal ki umr paayi thi]

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p109)

🤲🏻

Aseeran-e-Karbala:

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aapke Ahl o Ayaal ko Ghulamo aur Kaneezon ki tarah Qaid kar liya gaya aur unko Ahna e (Iron) Zanjeeron mein jakad kar is tarah be Kajawa Oonton par sawaar kar diya gaya ke Din ki pe panah Garmi unke Chehro ko jhulsaye de rahi thi......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

  1st October 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1527)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَقَالَ ٱلۡمَلَأُ ٱلَّذِینَ كَفَرُوا۟ مِن قَوۡمِهِۦ مَا نَرَىٰكَ إِلَّا بَشَرࣰا مِّثۡلَنَا وَمَا نَرَىٰكَ ٱتَّبَعَكَ إِلَّا ٱلَّذِینَ هُمۡ أَرَاذِلُنَا بَادِیَ ٱلرَّأۡیِ وَمَا نَرَىٰ لَكُمۡ عَلَیۡنَا مِن فَضۡلِۭ بَلۡ نَظُنُّكُمۡ كَـٰذِبِینَ *  قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ أَرَءَیۡتُمۡ إِن كُنتُ عَلَىٰ بَیِّنَةࣲ مِّن رَّبِّی وَءَاتَىٰنِی رَحۡمَةࣰ مِّنۡ عِندِهِۦ فَعُمِّیَتۡ عَلَیۡكُمۡ أَنُلۡزِمُكُمُوهَا وَأَنتُمۡ لَهَا كَـٰرِهُونَ.

"Uski Qaum ke Sardar Jinhone Kufr ikhtiyar kiya tha jawab mein kaha: 'Ham to tujhe apne jaisa hi ek Insaan samajhte hain aur teri pairavi un logon ne ki hai jo hamare muashere ke ghatya tareen aur Raye se khaali afraad hain. Hamen to tumhe apne upar koi bartari dikhayi nahi deti. Sach to ye hai ke ham tumhe jhoote afraad khayaal karte hain."

"Nooh (as) ne kaha: 'Aye meri Qaum! Zara socho to sahi agar mein apne Rab ki taraf se ek khuli Shahadat par tha, phir Usne mujhe apni khaas Rehmat se bhi nawaz diya magar woh tumhe nazar na aayi to kya mein nagawari ke bawajood tumhare upar zabardasti Hidayat laad sakta hun?"

(Surah Hud: 27 - 28)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Kafiron ne 3 etraz kiye jo ke aaj kal Ibne Taimiyya ke pairov Salafi, Wahabi Hazrat bhi karte hain:

(1) Rasool wa Nabi ham jaise hai. Ham mein aur un mein koi farq nahi. Unke mutabiq Risalat ka kaam Farishton ko karna chahiye tha.

(2) Rasool ke Pairavi/follow karnewala past gire hue, ghareeb, Jahil, illiterate, ignorant jinki koi haisiyyat nahi woh log karte hain.

(3) Rasool un logon par koi bartari nahi rakhte. Ba haisiyyat afraad kam haisiyyat wale ko follow nahi kar sakte.

Hazrat Nooh (as) ne ek hi jawab diya:

"Mein bhale hi Insaan hun lekin mere saath Rehmat e Ilahi shamil e haal hai. Usne mujhe khuli wa wazeh Nishaniyan ata ki hain. Iske liye zaroori nahi ke Farishta ho. Anbiya Mojeza bhi rakhte the. Jiske saath Rehmat e Ilahi shamil ho woh bartar o afzal hai ya woh log jin se unka Khaliq naraz ho. Ye sahi hai zyadatar follower kamzor tabqe ke log the. Jab etraz karnewale Takabbur, Ghuroor, Jaah Talabi, Zulm karte the. Unka etraz ye tha ke Jahil, illiterate log followers hain, jabke jahil to woh khud the jo itni wazeh aur khuli Daleelen nahi samajh paa rahe hain.

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Nooh (as) ko Wahy ki thi ke ab teri Qaum mein koi Imaan lane wala nahi hai. Isi liye Hazrat Nooh (as) ne ye arz kiya tha: "Unki Nasl mein Fajir o Kafir ke alawa aur koi paida nahi hoga." (Nooh:27)"

(Rauza Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jo shakhs Adam (as) ko uske Akhlaq mein aur Nooh (as) ko uski Hikmat mein aur Ibrahim (as) ko Hukm mein dekhna chahta hai, woh (is) Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) ko dekh le."

(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p33)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Beghairat Dushman unko Jangalon aur Bayabano mein le ja raha tha aur unke nazuk haathon ko Gardano ke peechhe, sakhti se bandh kar Galiyon aur Bazaaron mein unki numayish kar raha tha......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

      2nd October 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1528)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ لَاۤ أَسۡـَٔلُكُمۡ عَلَیۡهِ مَالًاۖ إِنۡ أَجۡرِیَ إِلَّا عَلَى ٱللَّهِۚ وَمَاۤ أَنَا۠ بِطَارِدِ ٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوۤا۟ۚ إِنَّهُم مُّلَـٰقُوا۟ رَبِّهِمۡ وَلَـٰكِنِّیۤ أَرَىٰكُمۡ قَوۡمࣰا تَجۡهَلُونَ *  وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ مَن یَنصُرُنِی مِنَ ٱللَّهِ إِن طَرَدتُّهُمۡۚ أَفَلَا تَذَكَّرُونَ.

"Aye meri Qaum! Mein tum se is kaam ke ewaz koi Daulat to nahi maangta. Mera Ajr to Allah ke zimme hai aur na mein Imaan walon ko apne paas se nikaal sakta hun. Yaqeenan woh log apne Parwardigar ki mulaqat karnewale hain albatta mein tumhe Jahil Qaum tasawwur kar raha hun. Aye meri Qaum! Agar mein in Mo'mino ko apne paas se nikaal dun to Khuda ki taraf se meri madad kaun karega to kya tum Nasihat nahi karoge?"

(Surah Hud: 29 - 30)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Reza (as) ne Ummat aur Itrat ke 12 farq bayan farmaye. Is guftugu ke zimn mein Aapne ye farmaya: (11:29). Hazrat Hud (as) ne bhi yehi kaha tha ke mein tum se Ujrat ka talabgar nahi hun. Meri Ujrat us Khuda ke zimme hai Jisne mujhe Paida kiya hai to kya tum Aql se kaam loge. Jabke Allah ne Apne Habib Kareem (saww) se farmaya tha:  "Aap keh den ke mein tumse Tableegh e Nabuwwat par koi Ujrat nahi maangta siwae iske ke Qarabatdaron se Mawaddat rakho." (Shura:23)

"Allah Ta'ala ne Aale Muhammad (saww) ki Muwaddat ko Ajre Risaalat isliye qarar diya hai ke Khuda jaanta tha ke ye Khandaan Deen se kabhi munharif nahi hoga aur ye Khandaan kabhi Gumrah nahi hoga."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aye logo'n! Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) se Mohabbat karo, kyunki unka Gosht mera Gosht hai. Unka Khoon mera Khoon hai. Allah Ta'ala La'anat kare meri Ummat mein se un logo'n par jo Ali (as) ke bare mein mere Ahd ko zaaya kar de'n aur uske baare mein meri Wasiyyat ko bhool jaayen. Aise logo'n ke liye Khuda ke nazdeek koi Ajr o Sawaab nahi hai."

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p182)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....La'anat ho us Fasiq giroh par! Jisne Aapko Qatl karke Islam ko Qatl aur Namaz o Roze ko mo'attal kar diya. Ahkam o Sunan o Ilahi ki Nafarmani ki. Imaan ki Buniyadon ko hila diya. Ayaat e Qur'ani mein tehreef ki aur Baghawat o Dushmani ke daldal mein dhansta hi chala gaya......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)
