    3rd October 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1529)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَاۤ أَقُولُ لَكُمۡ عِندِی خَزَاۤىِٕنُ ٱللَّهِ وَلَاۤ أَعۡلَمُ ٱلۡغَیۡبَ وَلَاۤ أَقُولُ إِنِّی مَلَكࣱ وَلَاۤ أَقُولُ لِلَّذِینَ تَزۡدَرِیۤ أَعۡیُنُكُمۡ لَن یُؤۡتِیَهُمُ ٱللَّهُ خَیۡرًاۖ ٱللَّهُ أَعۡلَمُ بِمَا فِیۤ أَنفُسِهِمۡ إِنِّیۤ إِذࣰا لَّمِنَ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.

"Aur mein tumse ye to nahi kehta ke mere paas Allah ke  Khazaane hain aur na ye kehta hun ke mere paas Ilm-e-Ghaib hai aur mein ye nahi kehta ke mein Farishta hun aur mein ye bhi nahi kehta ke jin logon ko tumhari Aankhen hiqarat se dekh rahi hain, Allah unhe koi bhalai na dega, unke andar ki kaifiyat Allah behtar Jaanta hai. Agar mein aisa kahunga to mein Zalimon mein se qarar paonga."

(Surah Hud: 31)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Ummat kuchh aur soch rahi the ke ye shayad Iqtedar, Maal o Daulat ke liye kar rahe hain. Ya ye zyada shekhi baghaad rahe hain. Ya woh inko Farishte ke taur par maan rahi thi etc..

Hazrat Nooh (as) ne logon ke saamne apni inkesaari ka izhaar kiya. Jabke ek Nabi mein ye saari khususiyaat payi jati hain.

Nabi Ilm-e-Ghaib rakhta hai lekin is Ayat mein Aapne farmaya ke Ilm-e-Ghaib nahi rakhte. Is mein tazaad nahi hai. Ilm-e-Ghaib sirf aur sirf Allah rakhta hai lekin Woh jise chahta hai use deta hai. (Jinn: 27-28) Pas jo kuchh Nabi ya Imam ke Ilm-e-Ghaib rakhta hai wo Khuda ka ata kardah hai. Koi ye dawa nahi kar sakta ke mein Ilm-e-Ghaib rakhta hun. Iski wajah ye hai Nabi ya Imam har lamhe Khuda ke saamne Aajiz rehte aur Khuda ki Marzi ke saamne apna Sar kham karke Uski Ita'at mein mashghool rehte. Isliye is Ayat se ye natija nikalna ghalat hoga ke Nabi ke paas Ilm-e-Ghaib nahi hai.

Hazrat Nooh (as) ne apne Tauheedi Mission ko jari rakha aur apne maqsad ko usi raaste par qayem rakha.

(To be Cont'd.......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ka Ism e Aazam 73 Harfo'n mein hai. Hamare Ahlebait (as) ke paas uske 72 Huroof hain aur ek harf Allah Ta'ala ke paas hai jiski bina par Ilm e Gaib ko Usne Apni zaat ke liye pasand farmaya aur Apne hi paas rakha hai. Pus, har qism ki Quwwat o Taaqat bus Usi ke paas hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p916)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......Aapki Shahadat par Allah ka Rasool (saww) sarapa dard ban gaya. Kitab e Khuda ka koi poochhne wala na raha. Aap (as) par Jafa karne walon ka Haq se Rishta toot gaya. Aapke uth jaane se Takbeer o Tehleel, Haram o Halal nez Tanzeel o Taveel par Parde pad gaye......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

    4th October 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1530)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰنُوحُ قَدۡ جَـٰدَلۡتَنَا فَأَكۡثَرۡتَ جِدَ ٰ⁠لَنَا فَأۡتِنَا بِمَا تَعِدُنَاۤ إِن كُنتَ مِنَ ٱلصَّـٰدِقِینَ *  قَالَ إِنَّمَا یَأۡتِیكُم بِهِ ٱللَّهُ إِن شَاۤءَ وَمَاۤ أَنتُم بِمُعۡجِزِینَ.

"Un logon ne kaha ke, Aye Nooh (as)! Tumne hamse jhagda kiya aur bahut jhagda kiya. Ab agar tum apne Daawe mein sachche ho to jis cheez ki dhamki hame de rahe ho to ise le aao."

"Nooh (as) ne kaha: 'Agar Khuda chahega to Woh is Azaab ko layega, tum Use Aajiz karne wale nahi ho."

(Surah Hud: 32 - 33)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

Jaisa ke guzashta Ayaat mein bhi zikr ho chuka hai ke woh itne hatdharmi ho gaye the ke Azaab e Ilahi ko bhi dekhne ko tayyar the. Ab Hazrat Nooh (as) Bad-Dua na karte to kya karte, isliye Aapne Khuda se unke liye Dua ki.

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Nooh (as) ne 300 Saal tak apni Qaum ko Deen ki dawat di, lekin logon ne Aapki Tableegh ko qabool na kiya. Aap (as) ne Bad-Dua karne ka iraada kiya. Tulu e Aftaab ke waqt Aap (as) ke paas Aasmaan e Duniya se 12 Hazaar Farishte utre. Wo 500 Saal ki Masafat (distance) karke pahunche, ye kehne ke Aap Bad-Dua na karen. Aapne 300 Saal ki aur mohlat di. Isi taraf doosre Aasmaano se bhi same distance cover karke utne aur Farishte ye kehne utre ke Bad-Dua na karen."

Allah Ta'ala ne Aapko Khajoor ke Darakht kasht karne ka Hukm diya. Log unka mazaq udate rahe aur patthar bhi marte ke 900 Saal ka budha ab kasht kar raha hai. 50 Baras ke baad Hukm hua ke in Khajooron ko kaat kar inki lakdi ki Kashti banao. Kashti banate dekh Munkarin ki zabaane aur khul gayin. (11:38)"

" Allah Ta'ala ne Jibrael (as) ko bheja taake Kashti banane ki taleem den. Kashti ka Zameen ki taraf Tool (Length) 1200 Haath tha aur is Araz (Breadth) 800 Haath tha auki Bulandi (Height) 80 Haath thi.

Allah Ta'ala ne Aap (as) ke zariye Ailan karwaya ke Kashti banane mein jo koi madad karega, to Kashti se jo tukde Zameen par girenge wo Sone Chaandi mein change ho jayege, wohi unki mazdoori hogi. Log kaam par lag gaye, kaam karte jate aur hanste jate ke Khushki (dry) mein bhi Kashti banana ajeeb baat hai."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"3 cheezein Bad-tareen hain jinse mein apni Ummat ke liye darta hun: Aalim ki galati, Munafiq ka bahes o Mujadile mein Quran se istedlaal (daleel dena) aur Duniya par tawajjoh jo tumhari gardano'n ko kotaah kar deti hai. Pus, Duniya ko buri nazar se dekho (aur us se dil na lagao)."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p174)

🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as) ki Shahadat ke asarat (Effects):

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Iske alawa.... Aapke na hone se, Deen mein kya kya badla gaya! Kaise kaise taghayyurat amal mein laye gaye! Mulhedana Nazariyon ko furogh mila, Ahkam e Shari'at mu'attal kar diye gaye. Nafsani Khwahishon ki giraft mazboot hui. Gumrahiyon ne zor pakda. Fitno ne Sar uthaya, aur Baatil ki ban aayi!......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

SHIA CHANNEL COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF IMAM REZA (as)

**********************************

             *17th Safar 1442*

    *5th October 2020, Monday*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ *HAZRAT NOOH (as)*♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1531)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

**وَلَا یَنفَعُكُمۡ نُصۡحِیۤ إِنۡ أَرَدتُّ أَنۡ أَنصَحَ لَكُمۡ إِن كَانَ ٱللَّهُ یُرِیدُ أَن یُغۡوِیَكُمۡۚ هُوَ رَبُّكُمۡ وَإِلَیۡهِ تُرۡجَعُونَ *  أَمۡ یَقُولُونَ ٱفۡتَرَىٰهُۖ قُلۡ إِنِ ٱفۡتَرَیۡتُهُۥ فَعَلَیَّ إِجۡرَامِی وَأَنَا۠ بَرِیۤءࣱ مِّمَّا تُجۡرِمُونَ.*

"Agar mein tumhari khair khwahi bhi karna chahun to meri khair khwahi tumhe kuchh fayda nahi de sakegi. Jab Khuda tumhe Gumrahi mein chhod dena chahta ho. Wohi tumhara Parwardigar hai aur Usi ki  taraf tum lautaye jaoge."

"(Aye Paighambar) Kya ye log kehte hain ke usne ye sab kuchh khud ghad liya hai? Aap keh den agar meine ye sab kuchh ghada hai to iska jurm mere zimme hai aur jo Jaraim tum kar rahe ho unse mein Bezaar hun."

(Surah Hud: 34 - 35)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Hazrat Nooh (as) apni Ummat ko jata rahe hain sab kuchh Khuda ke Haath Ikhtiyar mein hai. Jab Gumrahi hi unke naseeb mein hai to koi kya kar sakta hai.

Jaisa ke Ayat mein hai ke Allah unko Gumrah rakhega. Jaisa ke pehle bhi bayan kar chuke hain ke Hidayat wa Gumrahi zaatan Allah ke Zumme mein hai lekin iska sabab khud Insaan hai. Buraiyyon ka natija hi bura hota hai. Kamre mein ham Aag jalayen to dhuan niklega aur Diwaar kaali hogi. Ab ham Diwaar ko Kaali hi kahenge. Na Aag jalate na kaali hoti. Ye nahi keh sakte kaali nahi hui. Isi tarah koi bhi Jurm karoge uska asar (effect) dikhayi dega. Unhone jab Allah ko chhod kar Gumrahi ka Raasta ikhtiyar kiya to woh iska Natija to bhugtenge, but Natural hai.

Doosri Ayat ki Tafseer Ayat (11:18) ke zel bayan kar chuke hai.

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Nooh (as) Khajooron ki kasht karte rahe. Jab Khuda ki taraf dawat di to 300 saathi munharif hue, aur hote hote last mein 70 se kuchh zyada Aapke paas reh gaye. Us waqt Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Nooh (as) ko Wahy ki ke ab har qism ka mail kuchail chhat gaya hai. Ab tareek Raat ke baat Subha namudar hone wali hai. Jis jis ki Teenat kharab thi usne tujhe chhod diya aur jo log apne Imaan par ab bhi sabit hain aur Aqeeda e Tauheed par gehre Dil se Imaan rakhte hain aur teri Nabuwwat ki Rassi ko mazbooti se thaame hue hain. Mein inhe Zameen par apna Janasheen banaonga aur unke Deen ko mazbooti ata karunga aur mein unke khauf ko Amn se badal dunga, taake woh har tarah ke shirk ke shawaib se paak ho kar meri hi Ibaadat karen. Ab agar mein Munafiqeen aur be yaqeen afraad ko unse alihda na karta to unke Nifaaq mein mazeed pukhtagi paida ho jati aur woh Mukhlis Ahle Imaan se adawat rakhte aur Zameen par Fitna o Fasaad barpa karte aur Fitna o Fasaad ki maujoodgi mein Deen ki mazbooti na-mumkin hai, lehaza tum Hamari Aankhon ke saamne Kashti banao aur Hamari Wahy ke mutabiq Kashti bano."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*

🙇

Riwayat:

Abu Hamza se riwayat hai ke Imam Baqir (as) ne farmaya, "Ibadat e Khuda woh karta hai jo Allah ki Ma'arefat rakhta hai aur jo Ma'arefat nahi rakhta woh Zalaalat (Gumrahi) ke saath Ibaadat karta hai." Abu Hamza ne puchha, "Allah ki Ma'arefat kya hai?" Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Allah ki aur uske Rasool (saww) ki tasdeeq aur Ali (as) se Dosti aur unko aur digar Aimma e Huda (as) ko Imam maanna aur unke Dushmanon se izhaar e Bara'at karna. Is tarah Ma'arefat e Allah Azz wa Jall haasil hoti hai."

(Al Kaafi, v2, p30)

----------------------------------------------

*Ahle Haram ka Nauha o Girya!:*

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

_"..... Phir hua ye ke Nauha garon ne Aapke Jadd e Amjad ke Mazaar par aah o buka aur girya o zari ke saath yun Marsiya Khwani ki: "Allah ke Rasool (saww)! Aapka Beta, Aapka Nawasa Qatl kar dala gaya, Aapka Ghar loot liya gaya, Aapki Zurriyyat Aseer hui, Aapki Itrat par badi uftaad padi...."_

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

    6th October 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1532)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَأُوحِیَ إِلَىٰ نُوحٍ أَنَّهُۥ لَن یُؤۡمِنَ مِن قَوۡمِكَ إِلَّا مَن قَدۡ ءَامَنَ فَلَا تَبۡتَىِٕسۡ بِمَا كَانُوا۟ یَفۡعَلُونَ *  وَٱصۡنَعِ ٱلۡفُلۡكَ بِأَعۡیُنِنَا وَوَحۡیِنَا وَلَا تُخَـٰطِبۡنِی فِی ٱلَّذِینَ ظَلَمُوۤا۟ إِنَّهُم مُّغۡرَقُونَ.

"Aur Nooh (as) ki taraf Wahy ki gayi ke tumhari Qaum mein se jo Imaan la chuke hain, bas woh Imaan la chuke, unke alawa aur koi Imaan nahi layega tum unke Afa'al (Actions) par gham na karo aur hamare  Nigahon ke saamne aur Hamari Wahy ki Nigraani mein Kashti banao. Aur Zalimon ke mutalliq Mujh se baat na karna, ye sab ke sab doobne wale hain."

(Surah Hud: 36 - 37)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Hazrat Nooh (as) jab poori Tabligh kar chuke tab Allah ne farmaya ke jisko Imaan lana tha la chuka, baqi sab doobenge.

Yahan par ek humanity issue bhi paida hota hai, jiska Jawab Imam (as) ne farmaya.

⛵

Imam Reza (as) se sawal hua ke Hazrat Nooh (as) ke Zamaane mein kyon poori Duniya ko gharq kiya?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Gharq honewalon mein koi Bachcha shamil nahi tha. Allah Ta'ala ne Tufaan e Nooh (as) se 40 Saal qabl Aurton ko banjh bana diya tha isiliye jab Tufaan aaya to us waqt ek bhi Bachcha maujood nahi tha aur Allah Ta'ala Aadil hai. Woh kisi Begunah ko Halaak nahi karta. Qaum e Nooh (as) ne apne Nabi ki Takzeeb (Denying) ki thi isiliye Allah ne inhe gharq kiya tha. Inke alawa baqi log woh the jo is Takzeeb par raazi the aur jo kisi Gunah par raazi ho woh bhi Gunahgar ki manind hota hai. Isiliye baqi bhi doob gaye the."

(Imam Sadiq (as) ne bhi yehi farmaya)

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Masjid e Kufa Jannat ke Baghaat mein se ek Baagh hai. Is mein padhi jaane wali ek Namaz ka Sawab 90 Namazon ke Sawab ke barabar hai. Is mein ek 1070 Anbiya ne Namaz padhi thi. Isi mein wo Tanoor tha jisse Tufaane Nooh (as) ke waqt Paani nikla tha. Aur Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kashti usi jagah banayi gayi thi aur wo Babul ki Naaf (middle part) hai aur Anbiya ke jama hone ka maqam hai."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

Gham-e-Shuhadaye Karbala:

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Ye sun kar Paighambar (saww) ko bahut sadma pahuncha, unke Qalbe Tapa'n ne Khoon ke Aansu barsaye, Malaika ne unhe Pursa diya, Anbiya (as) ne Taziyat ki. Aur Maula Aapki Madare Grami Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) par qayamat toot padi! Malaika qatar dar qatar Apke Walid e Grami ke huzoor Taziyat ke liye aaye. Aala Illiyeen mein Saf e Matam bichh gayi. Hooren apni Rukhsaron par Tamache mar mar kar nidhal ho gayi, Aasmaan aur Aasmaani Makhlooq, Jannat aur Jannat ke Dar o Diwaar, Bulandiyon aur Pastiyon, Samandaron aur Machhliyon, Jannat ke Khuddam mil kar Aapki Musibat par Khoon ke Aansu bahaye.!!!!!!!"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

 7th October 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1533)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَصۡنَعُ ٱلۡفُلۡكَ وَكُلَّمَا مَرَّ عَلَیۡهِ مَلَأࣱ مِّن قَوۡمِهِۦ سَخِرُوا۟ مِنۡهُۚ قَالَ إِن تَسۡخَرُوا۟ مِنَّا فَإِنَّا نَسۡخَرُ مِنكُمۡ كَمَا تَسۡخَرُونَ *  فَسَوۡفَ تَعۡلَمُونَ مَن یَأۡتِیهِ عَذَابࣱ یُخۡزِیهِ وَیَحِلُّ عَلَیۡهِ عَذَابࣱ مُّقِیمٌ *  حَتَّىٰۤ إِذَا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُنَا وَفَارَ ٱلتَّنُّورُ قُلۡنَا ٱحۡمِلۡ فِیهَا مِن كُلࣲّ زَوۡجَیۡنِ ٱثۡنَیۡنِ وَأَهۡلَكَ إِلَّا مَن سَبَقَ عَلَیۡهِ ٱلۡقَوۡلُ وَمَنۡ ءَامَنَۚ وَمَاۤ ءَامَنَ مَعَهُۥۤ إِلَّا قَلِیلࣱ.

"Nooh (as) Kashti bana rahe the aur jab bhi unki Qaum ke Sardaron mein se koi unke paas se guzarta to woh unka mazaq udata tha. Usne kaha ke agar tum Hamara mazaq udate ho to Ham bhi tumhara isi tarah mazaq udayenge. Anqareeb tumhe pata chal jayega ke kis par wo Azaab aata hai jo use ruswa kardega aur kis par dayemi Azaab utarta hai. Yahan tak ke jab Hamara Hukm aa gaya aur Tanoor se Paani ubalne laga to hamne kaha ke har qism ke Janwaron ka ek ek Joda (pair) Kashti mein sawar kar lo aur apne Khandaan ko bhi Kashti par sawar kar lo albatta unhe sawar na karna jinke mutalliq halakat ka faisla ho chuka hai aur jo Imaan laye hain unhe Kashti par sawar karao. Unke saath Imaan laane wale bahut hi kam log the."

(Surah Hud: 38 - 40)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kashti tayyar kar chuke to Allah Ta'ala ne Aapko Hukm diya ke Aap (as) Saryani Zabaan (Syriac) mein ye awaz den ke koi Jaanwar aur Darinda aisa na ho jo yahan na aaye. Aap (as) ne awaaz di to tamam Jaanwar Aap (as) ke paas jama ho gaye. Aap (as) ne tamam Janwaron mein se ek ek Jode ko Kashti par bithaya aur Aap (as) par Imaan laane walon ki tadaad sirf 80 afraad par mushtamil thi. Aap (as) ne unhe bhi Kashti par sawar kiya jaisa ke Farmane Ilahi hai. (11:40)."

Hazrat Nooh (as) ne wahan Kashti banayi thi jahan Aaj Masjid e Kufa hai. Jab wo Din aaya jis mein Khuda ne logon ki halakat ka iraada kiya. Nooh (as) ki Biwi apne ghar mein baithi Tanoor par Rotiya paka rahi thi ke achanak usne cheekh kar kaha ke Tanoor se Paani josh maar raha hai. Ye sun kar Nooh (as) uthe aur Tanoor par Dhakna rakha aur us Dhakkan par apni Mohr laga di. Aap (as) ne apni Kashti mein Janwaron ko Kashti mein sawar karaya. Phir Aap (as) Tanoor ke paas aaye aur Aap (as) apni Mohr todi aur Tanoor ke Munh se Dhakna hataya to Paani poore josh se nikalne laga. Suraj ko gahen laga, Aasmaan se Paani ki chadaren utarne lagi aur Zameen ke tamam Chashme phoot pade jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala farmata hai (Qamar:11-12)"

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🌊

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as)

"Khuda ki Qasam! "و فار التنور" se murad Rotiyan pakanewala Tanoor (Tandoor) murad nahi hai. Isse Suraj ka Tulu hona (Sunrise) murad hai."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Hazrat Ali (as):

Rasoole Akram (saww):

مَثَلُ اَهلُ بَيتِى فِيكُم مَثَلُ سَفِينَةُ نُوحٍ مَن رَكَبَهَا نَجٰى وَ مَن تَخَلَّف عَنهَا فِى النَّار.

"Tumhare andar mere Ahle Bait (as) ki misaal Kashti e Nooh (as) jaisi hai jo is par sawar ho gaya woh Najaat pa gaya aur jo usse peechhe reh gaya use Dozakh mein phenk diya jayega."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

           21st Safar 1442

    9th October 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1534)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ ٱرۡكَبُوا۟ فِیهَا بِسۡمِ ٱللَّهِ مَجۡرٜىٰهَا وَمُرۡسَىٰهَاۤۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی لَغَفُورࣱ رَّحِیمࣱ *  وَهِیَ تَجۡرِی بِهِمۡ فِی مَوۡجࣲ كَٱلۡجِبَالِ.....

"Nooh (as) ne kaha: Is par sawar ho jao, iska chalna aur thaherna Allah ke naam se marboot (connected) hai. Yaqeenan, mera Rab Bada Bakhshne wala, Meherban hai. Aur wo Kashti unhe le kar pahadon jaisi maujon ke darmiyan chali ja rahi thi........"

(Surah Hud: 41 - 42)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki sawari ke Jaanwar bataur miraas Hazrat Ali (as) ko mile the. AanHazrat (saww) ki sawari ke Jaanwar mein ek Gadha tha jise AanHazrat (saww) "يعفور - Ya'foor" ke naam se pukarte the. AanHazrat (saww) ki wafat ka us par gehra asar hua. Jaise hi Aapki wafat hui to usne apni Rassi todi aur daudta hua "Quba" mein aaya aur usne Bani Hateem ke Kuwen mein chhalang laga di aur woh mar gaya aur wohi Kuwan hi uski Qabr ban gaya."

"Ya'foor Gadhe ne AanHazrat (saww) se kalam bhi kiya tha aur usne kaha tha: "Mere Maa Baap Aap par Qurban ho jayen. Mujhe mere Baap ne bataya tha aur usne ye baat apne silsile Abaa se suni thi ke jab Hazrat Nooh (as) ke daur mein Tufaan aaya aur unhone Janwaron ko Kishti par sawar kiya tha to un mein hamare Jadde Aala bhi maujood the. Ek din Hazrat Nooh (as) ne uski taraf nigah e shafqat se dekha aur uske chehre par apna daste shafqat pher kar farmaya tha ke uski Nasl se woh Gadha paida hoga jis par Anbiya ka Sardar aur Khatemul Anbiya Nabi sawar hoga. Khuda ka Shukr hai Jisne mujhe ye sharaf ata kiya hai."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharay, Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⛵ 🐐

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) se chand sawal hue jin ek sawal ye tha ke Bakri ki dum upar kyon uthi rehti hai jabke Bhedh se uski Sharmgah chhupi rehti hai?

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Jab Bakri Kashti par sawar hui thi to usne Hazrat ki Nafarmani ki thi. Aap (as) ne uski Dum tod di thi, yehi wajah hai ke uski Sharmgah khuli rehti hai jabke Bhed ne Aap (as) ki awaz par jaldi se Labbaik kahi thi Aap (as) ne uski pusht par haath phera tha isi liye uski Sharmgah Dum se chhupi rehti hai."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Hazrat Ali (as):

Rasoole Akram (saww):

مَثَلُ اَهلُ بَيتِى فِيكُم مَثَلُ سَفِينَةُ نُوحٍ مَن رَكَبَهَا نَجٰى وَ مَن تَخَلَّف عَنهَا فِى النَّار.

"Tumhare andar mere Ahle Bait (as) ki misaal Kashti e Nooh (as) jaisi hai jo is par sawar ho gaya woh Najaat pa gaya aur jo usse peechhe reh gaya use Dozakh mein phenk diya jayega."

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

السلام عليك يا سفينة النجاة.

(Ziyarat-e-Yaume Juma )

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Bare Ilaha! Aye jald Hisaab Karnewale, Aye Sabse Karim Hasti, aur Aye Sabse Bade Hakim! Mein Teri Bargaj mein tamam Jahano ki taraf Tere Rasool aur Akheri Nabi Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww), unke Cousin bhai, Tawana Bazu, Danush aur Agaahi ke Markaz Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali Ibne Abi Taalib (as)...... (waasta deta hun ke un par Darood nazil farma)......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

    10th October 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1535)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقَالَ ٱرۡكَبُوا۟ فِیهَا بِسۡمِ ٱللَّهِ مَجۡرٜىٰهَا وَمُرۡسَىٰهَاۤۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی لَغَفُورࣱ رَّحِیمࣱ *  وَهِیَ تَجۡرِی بِهِمۡ فِی مَوۡجࣲ كَٱلۡجِبَالِ.....

"Nooh (as) ne kaha: Is par sawar ho jao, iska chalna aur thaherna Allah ke naam se marboot (connected) hai. Yaqeenan, mera Rab Bada Bakhshne wala, Meherban hai. Aur wo Kashti unhe le kar pahadon jaisi maujon ke darmiyan chali ja rahi thi........"

(Surah Hud: 41 - 42)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kashti ki hifazat ke liye Tera Hazaar Tera Farishte nazil kiye the aur jab Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) ka Zahoor hoga aur Aap (as) Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka Parcham lehrayenge to tamam Farishte Aap (as) ki madad ke liye Aasmaan se utrenge aur woh Aap(as) ki madad karenge.

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Tufaan e Nooh (as) ke waqt poore 40 Din tak Aasmaan se Baarish barasti rahi aur Zameen ke Chashme (Well) phootte rahe jiski wajah se Nooh (as) ki Kashti Aasmaan se ja takrati thi aur Kashti ka safar Masjid e Kufa se shuru hua tha."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🚣

Imam Reza (as): (& Imam Kazim (as):

"Jab Hazrat Nooh (as) Kashti par sawar hue aur Kashti chalne lagi to us waqt Allah Ta'ala ne Nooh (as) ko ye Wahy farmayi ke agar kisi waqt tumhe gharq hone ka khatra mehsoos ho to 1000 martaba 'لا إله إلا الله' (Kalma) ka wird karke Mujh se Najaat ki darkhwast karna, Mein tujhe aur tere saathiyon ko gharq hone se bacha lunga."

"Phir Kashti safar kar rahi thi ke shadeed Aandhi chali, Nooh (as) ne mehsoos kiya ke isse Kashti ka balance barqarar nahi reh sakega aur wo doob jayegi. Unke paas itna waqt nahi tha ke woh 1000 bar ye Kalma ka wird karen. Chunanche us waqt unhone Saryani Zabaan mein ye jumla kaha:

هيلويا الغا الغايا ماريا يا ماريا اتقن.

Ye Alfaaz kehne ki der thi ke dagmagati hui Kashti seedhi ho gayi aur har khatre se be-niyaz ho kar chalne lagi."

"Hazrat Nooh (as) ne kaha: 'Jis Kalam ki wajah se mein gharq hone se bacha hun wo Kalam har waqt mere paas rehna chahiye. Chunanche unhone apni Anguthi par ye ibarat likhi:

لا إله إلا الله الف مرّة يا ربّ اصلحنى.

(La ilaha... ek hazaar martaba. Parwardigar! Meri islah kar.)

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Al Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🚢

Imam Sadiq (as)-Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jab Hazrat Nooh (as) Kashti par baithe aur ek bar unhe garq hone ka andesha hua to unhone ye Dua padhi:"

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّى اَسئَلُكَ بِمُحَمَّدٍ وَ آلِ مُحَمَّدٍ لَمَّا اَنجَيتَنِى مِنَ الغَرقِ.

(Khudaya! Mein Tujhe Muhammad (saww) wa Aale Muhammad (as) ka waasta de kar sawal karta hun ke mujhe garq hone se najaat ata farma.)

(Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Raavi ne Imam Moosa Kazim (as) se arz kiya ke Raasta Daryai ho ya khushki dono hi khatarnak hain?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Jab tum rawangi ka iraada karo to pehle Masjid e Nabawi mein ja kar do Rakat Nafila Namaz ada karo, phir khushki ya tari ja raasta ikhtiyar karne ke liye Khuda se sau martaba Istekhara karo. Aur agar Istekhare ke baad tumhare Dil mein ye azm paida ho ke tum Daryai Raasta ka safar ikhtiyar karo to jab tum Kashti mein baitho to Hazrat Nooh (as) ke do Kalemat padho jo Qur'an mein hai: (11:41) (Khuda ne chaha to har khatre se mehfooz rahoge."

🚣🏻

Imam Reza (as):

"Jab Kashti par baitho to ye Dua padho: (11:41)"

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1536)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهِیَ تَجۡرِی بِهِمۡ فِی مَوۡجࣲ كَٱلۡجِبَالِ وَنَادَىٰ نُوحٌ ٱبۡنَهُۥ وَكَانَ فِی مَعۡزِلࣲ یَـٰبُنَیَّ ٱرۡكَب مَّعَنَا وَلَا تَكُن مَّعَ ٱلۡكَـٰفِرِینَ *  قَالَ سَـَٔاوِیۤ إِلَىٰ جَبَلࣲ یَعۡصِمُنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمَاۤءِۚ قَالَ لَا عَاصِمَ ٱلۡیَوۡمَ مِنۡ أَمۡرِ ٱللَّهِ إِلَّا مَن رَّحِمَۚ وَحَالَ بَیۡنَهُمَا ٱلۡمَوۡجُ فَكَانَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُغۡرَقِینَ

"Aur wo Kashti unhe le kar pahadon jaisi maujon ke darmiyan chali ja rahi thi ke Nooh (as) ne apne Bete ko awaz di jo ke door faasle par khada tha ke Farzand! Hamare saath Kashti par sawar ho jao aur Kafiron ke saath na raho. Usne kaha: Mein anqareeb Pahad par panah le lunga, wo mujhe Paani se bacha lega.' Nooh (as) ne kaha:' Aaj Amr e Khuda se, bachanewala koi nahi hai siwai iske jis par Woh Rahem kar de. Phir dono ke darmiyan Mauj hael ho gayi aur woh Gharq honewalon mein shamil ho gaya."

(Surah Hud: 42 - 43)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Imam Ali Naqi (as):

"Nooh (as) ki majmooyi Umr 2500 Baras thi."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

⛵

Hazrat Nooh (as) ke 3 Bete the: Saam, Haam aur Yaafis. Saam Nek wa farmabardar tha. Haam aur Yaafis ke liye unki Nafarmaniyon ki wajah se H. Nooh (as) ne Dua ki aur Parwardigar ne un dono ke Sulb ka Paani tabdeel kar diya, sab Black Haam ki Aulad hain, jabke Turk, Saqalib, Yajooj wa Majooj, Chinese sab Yafis se talluq rakhte hain. Jabke sab White Saam ki Aulad hain. H. Nooh (as) ne farmaya ke Haam aur Yafis ke Aulad Saam ki Ghulam rahegi.

Tafseer Ayyashi aur Majmaul Bayan ke mutabiq Kana'an H. Nooh (as) ka saga beta nahi tha jo Kashti mein sawar nahi hua, jabke kuchh Mufassir is baat ko nahi maante.

(Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

Najaf e Ashraf:

Imam Sadiq (as):

" 'Najaf' ek zamane mein Pahad tha. Hazrat Nooh (as) ke Farzand ne isi Pahad ke mutalliq kaha tha ke 'mein is Pahad ki panah le lunga....' Us waqt ruye Zameen par isse bada Pahad aur kahin maujood nahi tha."

"Jab Nooh (as) ke Na-Ahl Bete ne Pahad ko apni panahgah banaya to us waqt Khuda ne is Pahad se kaha: 'Aye Pahad! Kya Mujhe chhod kar log tera sahara dhoond rahe hain?' Khuda ke is Kalam se Pahad ke tukde hue aur kuchh tukde Shaam ki taraf chale gaye. Baqi Pahad ne Ret ki surat ikhtiyar kar li aur ek azeem Samandar mein tabdeel ho gaya. Us waqt use 'Behre Naye ( نَے )' kaha jata tha. Phir wo Samandar Khushk (dry) ho gaya aur khushk hone ke amal ko 'Jaf ( جف )' se tabeer kiya jata hai. Logon ne use 'Jaf' kehna shuru kar diya. Phir ahista ahista Lafz ' نَے جف ', Lafz 'Najaf نجف ' mein change ho gaya. Kyonki ye short word tha isliye common ho gaya."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Ya Ali (as)! Tumhari aur tumhari Aulaad ki misaal Safeena e Nooh (as) ki hai ke jo us Safeene par sawar ho gaya Najaat pa gaya aur jo us se alag reh gaya woh halaak ho gaya aur phir tumhari misaal Aasmaan ke Sitaron ki hai ke jab ek Sitara ghayab hota hai to doosra tulu (rise) ho jaata hai aur ye silsila Qayamat tak jaari rahega."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p168)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"(Mein Teri Bargah mein!).......... Nez unki Mazloom Itrat. Abidon ki Zeenat Hazrat Ali bin Husain (as), juyaye Haq, logon ke Markaze Tawajjah, Hazrat Mohd bin Ali (as), sabse bade Sadiqul Qaul Hazrat Jafar bin Mohd (as), Deen ke Madadgar, Hazrat Ali bin Musa (as). Pairokaron ke Rahnuma Hazrat Mohd bin Ali (as), sabse bade Parsa Hazrat Ali bin Mohd (as)....... (ka waasta deta hun ke un par Darood nazil farma)....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

    12th October 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1537)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَهِیَ تَجۡرِی بِهِمۡ فِی مَوۡجࣲ كَٱلۡجِبَالِ وَنَادَىٰ نُوحٌ ٱبۡنَهُۥ وَكَانَ فِی مَعۡزِلࣲ یَـٰبُنَیَّ ٱرۡكَب مَّعَنَا وَلَا تَكُن مَّعَ ٱلۡكَـٰفِرِینَ *  قَالَ سَـَٔاوِیۤ إِلَىٰ جَبَلࣲ یَعۡصِمُنِی مِنَ ٱلۡمَاۤءِۚ قَالَ لَا عَاصِمَ ٱلۡیَوۡمَ مِنۡ أَمۡرِ ٱللَّهِ إِلَّا مَن رَّحِمَۚ وَحَالَ بَیۡنَهُمَا ٱلۡمَوۡجُ فَكَانَ مِنَ ٱلۡمُغۡرَقِینَ

"Aur wo Kashti unhe le kar pahadon jaisi maujon ke darmiyan chali ja rahi thi ke Nooh (as) ne apne Bete ko awaz di jo ke door faasle par khada tha ke Farzand! Hamare saath Kashti par sawar ho jao aur Kafiron ke saath na raho. Usne kaha: Mein anqareeb Pahad par panah le lunga, wo mujhe Paani se bacha lega.' Nooh (as) ne kaha:' Aaj Amr e Khuda se, bachanewala koi nahi hai siwai iske jis par Woh Rahem kar de. Phir dono ke darmiyan Mauj hael ho gayi aur woh Gharq honewalon mein shamil ho gaya."

(Surah Hud: 42 - 43)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Jab Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kashti chalne lagi to Aap (as) ne Bete "Kan'an ( كنعان )" ko dekha jo Kafiron ke saath Aap (as) se door khada tha. Aap (as) ne use Kashti par chadhne ki Dawat di to usne kaha ke mein Pahad par chadh jaonga aur Paani se bach jaonga. Hazrat Nooh (as) ne farmaya ke Azaabe Khuda se koi nahi bacha sakta. Parwardigar se use bachane ki darkhwast bhi ki lekin Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya ke woh unke Ahl se nahi hai. Woh doob gaya. Tufaan e Nooh (as) mein saari Duniya doob gayi lekin Baitullah mehfooz raha. Isliye use 'Baitul Ateeq" bhi kaha jata hai. عتیق means Azaad shuda. Baitullah garq hone se Azaad tha. 40 Din Baarish hoti rahi. Tamam Chashme phoot pade aur Aap (as) ki Kashti Aasmaan se takraane lagi tab Aap (as) ne Dua ki, Aye mere Rab, bas ab Paani ko rok le.' Us waqt Baarish khatm ho gayi aur Zameen ko Hukm hua apna Paani pee le. (11:44) Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kashti' Kohe Judi' par jaa lagi. Ye Musal ke paas ek Pahad hai. (Summery)

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Momeneen mein se jo Gareeb hain wo Ameero'n se Jannat mein 40 bahaarein (yaani 40 saal) pehle daakhil honge. Phir aap ne farmaya, "Aap ke liye main ek misaal bayaan karta hoon. Iski misaal 2 kashtiyo'n (boats) ki hai jo dono ek police chowki se guzrein aur unme se ek khaali hai aur usme koi cheez police waalo'n ko nahi milti to wo usko jaane denge. Aur doosri wo hai ke jisme dekhte hain ke khilaaf e qanoon samaan maujood hai. Pus, wo usko rok lenge."

(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p234)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"(Mein Teri Bargah mein!).......... Nez Silsila e Nabuwwat o Imamat ke tamam Buzurgon ke Waaris aur Aye Allah! Teri tamam Makhlooq par Hujjat (atfs) ka waasta deta hun ke Tu Mohd o Aale Muhammad (as) un par jo Aale Taha wa Yaseen bhi hain aur Sachche aur Nekokar bhi, Darood nazil farma....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

    13th October 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1538)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقِیلَ یَـٰۤأَرۡضُ ٱبۡلَعِی مَاۤءَكِ وَیَـٰسَمَاۤءُ أَقۡلِعِی وَغِیضَ ٱلۡمَاۤءُ وَقُضِیَ ٱلۡأَمۡرُ وَٱسۡتَوَتۡ عَلَى ٱلۡجُودِیِّۖ وَقِیلَ بُعۡدࣰا لِّلۡقَوۡمِ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ.

"Hukm hua: Aye Zameen apna Paani nigal ja aur Aye Aasmaan tu ruk ja. Phir Paani Zameen mein baith gaya. Kaam pura kar diya gaya. Kashti "Judi" par tik gayi aur keh diya gaya ke Zalimon ki Qaum ke liye doori hai."

(Surah Hud: 44)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Kuffar e Quraish ne kuchh Ayaat Qur'an ke muqabile mein banane ka iraada kiya aur Adeeb Hazrat ko khoob rishwat di lekin 40 Din ke baad Adeeb Hazrat jab is Ayat par pahunche to unhone besakhta ailaan kiya ye Bashar ka Kalam nahi. Iske muqabile mein koi Kalam mushabehat nahi rakhta.

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Nooh (as) Safeene par sawar the to Khuda ne unhe Wahye farmayi ke woh Baitullah ke gird 7 Chakkar lagayen. Aap (as) ne Wahy e Ilahi ke tehet 7 Chakkar lagaye. Phir Aap (as) Kashti se Paani mein utre. Us jagah par Aap (as) ke Ghutno tak Paani mehsoos hua. Aap (as) ne us jagah se ek Sandooq baramad kiya jis mein Hazrat Adam (as) ki Haddiyan thi. Aap (as) ne wo Sandooq Kashti par rakha. Phir Kashti chakkar lagati hui Aap (as) ko Kufa ke beech mein le aayi aur jab Aap (as) yahan pahunche to us waqt Khuda ne Zameen ko Hukm diya ke tu apna Paani nigal le jis tarah se Tufaan ka aghaaz Masjid e Kufa se hua tha usi tarah se Paani nigalne ke amal ki ibtida bhi Masjid e Kufa se hui thi. Jab Paani khushk hua to Kashti par baithe hue afraad Kashti se utre aur Zameen par phail gaye."

(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

⛵🕋

Hazrat Nooh (as) kitne Din Kashti mein sawar the?

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Woh musalsal 7 Din Raat Kashti par sawar the. Kashti ne Baitullah ka Tawaf kiya phir wo 'Judi' par Langarandaz hui aur wo jagah Furaat e Kufa hai."

"Safeena e Nooh (as) ne Safa o Marwa ke darmiyan Sa'ee bhi kiya tha..."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Kashti e Nooh (as) Ashura ke Din Judi par Langarandaz hui thi. Aap (as) ne us mein sawar afraad ko hukm diya ke woh us Din Roza rakhen."

(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Aur mujhe Roze Qayamat un logon mein shamil farma le jinko us Din Amn o Itminan hasil hoga, aur woh us pareshani wale Din bhi khush o Khurram honge aur Jinhe Jannat Rizwan ki khush khabari sunayi jayegi......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1539)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَنَادَىٰ نُوحࣱ رَّبَّهُۥ فَقَالَ رَبِّ إِنَّ ٱبۡنِی مِنۡ أَهۡلِی وَإِنَّ وَعۡدَكَ ٱلۡحَقُّ وَأَنتَ أَحۡكَمُ ٱلۡحَـٰكِمِینَ *  قَالَ یَـٰنُوحُ إِنَّهُۥ لَیۡسَ مِنۡ أَهۡلِكَۖ إِنَّهُۥ عَمَلٌ غَیۡرُ صَـٰلِحࣲۖ فَلَا تَسۡـَٔلۡنِ مَا لَیۡسَ لَكَ بِهِۦ عِلۡمٌۖ إِنِّیۤ أَعِظُكَ أَن تَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡجَـٰهِلِینَ.

"Aur Nooh (as) ne apne Parwardigar ko pukara aur kaha: 'Aye mere Parwardigar! Mera Beta mere Ahl mein se hai aur Tera Waada Sachcha hai aur Tu tamam Hakimon mein sabse Bada Hakim hai. Allah ne kaha: 'Woh tere Ahl mein se nahi hai. Ye Amal Ghair Saleh hai lehaza Mujh se aisi baat ka sawal na karo jiska tujhe Ilm nahi. Mein tujh Nasihat karta hun ke Jahilon mein se na bano."

(Surah Hud: 45 - 46)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Yahoodi ne Hazrat Ali (as) se sawal kiya ke kya Anbiya bhi ghalti kar sakte hain jaise Hazrat Nooh (as) apne Na-Ahl bete ke liye shifarish ki?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Is mein Allah ki Zabardast Hikmat muzmir hai. Khuda agar Anbiya ki Bashari Kamzoriyon ka izhaar na karta to log unhe Ma'bood maan lete, jaisa ke Esaiyon ne Hazrat Esa (as) ke Mo'jezaat dekh kar unhe Ibnullah (Son of God) kehna shuru kar diya tha."

(Kitab Ehtejaaj Tabarsi, Noorus Saqlain)

⛵

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah ne Farzand e Nooh (as) ke mutalliq ye Faisla sadir farmaya ke woh Nooh (as) ke Ahl se nahi hai. Iski wajah ye hai ke woh Hazrat (as) ka mukhalif tha isiliye Allah ne use Ahl se bahar nikal diya aur jin logon ne Aap (as) ki Pairavi ki thi Khuda ne unhe Hazrat Nooh (as) ka Ahl qarar diya."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🚩

Imam Zamana (atfs) se Tauqee ke zariye kuchh sawal the us mein ek ye tha mere Khandan wale aur cousin mere khilaf kyon hain?

Imam (as) ne jawab mein farmaya:

"Suno! Khuda ki kisi Insaan se Rishtedari nahi hai aur jo mera Inkar kare woh mujh se nahi hai aur uska Raasta Farzand e Nooh (as) ke Raaste jaisa hai."

(Kitabul Ghaiba Tusi, Noorus Saqlain)

😏

Paighambar e Islam (saww):

مَن غَشَّ مُسلِمًا فَلَيسَ مِنَّا

"Jo Musalman Bhaiyyon se Dhokabazi aur Khayanat kare woh ham mein se nahi hai."

(Safeenatul Bihar, V-2, P-318)

😋

Imam Sadiq (as):

لَيسَ بِوَلِى لِى مَن اَكَلَ مَالَ مُؤمِنٍ حَرَامًا.

"Jo Momin ka Maal Najaez taur par khaaye woh mera Dost aur Mawali nahi hai."

(Wasaelus Shia, Vol-12, P-53)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Bare Ilaha! Aye Arhamur Rahemeen Apni Rehmat ke Sadqe mein mera naam Musalmano mein likh le, mujhe Saleh aur Nekokar logon mein shamil farma le, mere pasmandgan aur baad wali Naslon mein Zikre Sachhayi aur bhalayi ke saath jaari rakh, Baghiyon ke muqabile mein meri Nusrat farma, Hasad karne walon ki Chaal o Shar se meri hifazat farma, Zalimon ke haathon ko meri jaanib badhne se rok de......."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

           27th Safar 1442

    15th October 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ SADAAT KI AHLIYYAT ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1540)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَنَادَىٰ نُوحࣱ رَّبَّهُۥ فَقَالَ رَبِّ إِنَّ ٱبۡنِی مِنۡ أَهۡلِی وَإِنَّ وَعۡدَكَ ٱلۡحَقُّ وَأَنتَ أَحۡكَمُ ٱلۡحَـٰكِمِینَ *  قَالَ یَـٰنُوحُ إِنَّهُۥ لَیۡسَ مِنۡ أَهۡلِكَۖ إِنَّهُۥ عَمَلٌ غَیۡرُ صَـٰلِحࣲۖ فَلَا تَسۡـَٔلۡنِ مَا لَیۡسَ لَكَ بِهِۦ عِلۡمٌۖ إِنِّیۤ أَعِظُكَ أَن تَكُونَ مِنَ ٱلۡجَـٰهِلِینَ.

"Aur Nooh (as) ne apne Parwardigar ko pukara aur kaha: *'Aye mere Parwardigar! Mera Beta mere Ahl mein se hai* aur Tera Waada Sachcha hai aur Tu tamam Hakimon mein sabse Bada Hakim hai. Allah ne kaha: *'Woh tere Ahl mein se nahi hai. Ye Amal Ghair Saleh hai* lehaza Mujh se aisi baat ka sawal na karo jiska tujhe Ilm nahi. Mein tujh Nasihat karta hun ke Jahilon mein se na bano."

(Surah Hud: 45 - 46)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Imam Reza (as) ka bhai Zaid chand afraad ke saath Aapki mehfil mein hazir hue. Woh hazereen par apna khaandaani tafakhur (Pride) jamane lage aur kehne lage ham ye hain, ham woh hain waghaira. Imam (as), jo mehv e guftugu the, ne bhi unki baaten suni, fauran mutawajjah hue aur farmaya: "Zaid! Maloom hota hai ke Ahle Kufa ki is Riwayat ne tumhe dhoke mein dal diya hai: Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya tha:

اِنَّ فَاطِمَةَ احسَنَتَ فَرجَهَا فَحَرَّمَ اللّٰهُ تَعٰالٰى ذُرِّيَتَهَا عَلَى النَّار.

"Hazrat Fatema (sa) ne apni Ismat ki hifazat ki hai jiske natije mein Allah ne uski Aulaad par Jahannum ki Aag ko Haraam qarar diya hai."

"Achhi tarah sun lo!) ye Hadis sahih hai lekin isse Imam Hasan (as) aur Imam Husain (as) aur Hazaaron Hazrat Fatema Zehra (sa) ki bila fasl (direct) Aulaad muraad hai."

"Ajeeb baat hai tere waalid Imam Musa Kazim (as) to Khuda ki Ita'at kare, Din ko Roza rakhe, Raat ko Qayam kare, aur tu Khuda ki Nafarmani kare aur jab tum dono Khuda ke Huzoor meib aao to barabar hokar aao. Iska matlab to phir ye hai ke tum apne Waalid se bhi Khuda ko zyada aziz ho. Hazrat Imam Zainul Abedin (as) farmate the: "Ham mein se Neki karnewala ko dohra Ajr milega aur hamare Badkaar ko bhi dohra Azaab diya jayega."

Imam (as) Raavi ki taraf mutawajjah hue aur farmaya: Qur'an ki ye Ayat padhi (11:46) (Jo log ye kehte hain ke Kan'an H. Nooh (as) ka Sulbi beta nahi tha.)

"Hargiz aisa nahi. Woh unka Sulbi beta tha lekin jab usne Khuda ki Nafarmani ki to Allah ne use Hazrat (as) ke Ahl se kharij kar diya tha. Isi tarah se jo ham mein se ho kar Khuda ki Ita'at nahi karega woh ham mein se nahi hoga aur tu (Ghair Syed hokar bhi) agar Allah ki Ita'at karega to tu bhi ham Ahle Bait (as) mein se hoga."

Raavi ka bayan hai ke Imam Reza (as) ke bhai Zaid bin Musa ne Madine mein Hukumat ke khilaf khuruj kiya aur us ne Bani Abbas ke kai Makanaat ko nazar aatish kiye aur aur kuchh afraad ko qatl kiya tha. Hukumat ki fauj ne usse ladayi ki aur use giraftar kar liya. Is giraftar karke Mamoon ke paas bhej diya gaya. Mamoon ne kaha ke ise uske bhai Ali Reza (as) ke paas le jao. Chunanche jab use Imam Reza (as) ke saamne laya gaya to Aap (as) usse farmaya: Zaid! Tumhe Kufa ke Ahmaq afraad ke is qaul ne tumhe dhoka diya hai... (Same Hadis ان فاطمة....... phir same nasihat farmayi jo upar bayan ho chuki hai.)

(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

🌿

Tarikh mein bahut se waqeat hain jisse pata chalta hai Imam ka farzand ho koi Fazilat nahi balke Amal e Saleh hai. Misal ke taur Imam Mahdi (as) ke chacha Jafar e Kazzab, Imam Musa (as) ke cousins, Imam Hasan (as) ke cousins etc. Usi tarah Biwi hona bhi koi Fazilat nahi jaise Jauza Imam Hasan (as) ne hi unko zeher se Shahid kiya, Kuchh Anbiya ki Biwiyan waghaira..

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🚩

Imam Baqir (as) ne Jabir se farmaya:

"Aye Jabir! Jaan lo ke tum us waqt tak hamare dost nahi ho sakte jab tak ke tumhare saare Ahle Shaher jama ho kar tum se kahen ke tu bura shakhs hai aur tu us par ghamgeen na ho aur sab mil kar kahen ke tu achha aadmi hai aur tu khush na ho balke apne aap ko Kitab e Khuda Qur'an ke saamne pesh karo aur achhayi aur burai ke bare mein Qawaneen o zawabit usse le lo aur phir dekho tum kis giroh mein se ho."

(Safeenatul Bihar, V-2, P-491)

😏

Paighambar e Islam (saww):

لَيسَ مِنَّا مَن لَم يُحَاسِب نَفسَهٗ فِى كُلِّ يَومٍ

"Jo shakhs har roz apna Muhaseba (Account) nahi karta woh ham mein se nahi hai."

(Biharul Anwaar, Vol-15, Akhlaq)

😋

Imam Sadiq (as):

لَيسَ من شيعتنا من يظلم الناس

"Jo logon par Zulm kare woh hamara Shia nahi hai."

(Biharul Anwaar, Vol-15, P-53, Tafseer Namoona)

🤲🏻

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Mukhe Aalal Illiyeen mein Ba-Barkat Peshwaon aur Aimma e Ahlul Bait (as) ke jawar (neighbour) mein un Anbiya, Siddiqeen, Shohada aur Saleheen ke saath jama kar, jin par Tu ne Apni Ne'maten nazil farmayi hain......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

SHIA CHANNEL COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF HAZRAT RASOOLE KHUDA (saww) & IMAM HASAN (as)

**********************************

             28th Safar 1442

16th October 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1541)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ رَبِّ إِنِّیۤ أَعُوذُ بِكَ أَنۡ أَسۡـَٔلَكَ مَا لَیۡسَ لِی بِهِۦ عِلۡمࣱۖ وَإِلَّا تَغۡفِرۡ لِی وَتَرۡحَمۡنِیۤ أَكُن مِّنَ ٱلۡخَـٰسِرِینَ *  قِیلَ یَـٰنُوحُ ٱهۡبِطۡ بِسَلَـٰمࣲ مِّنَّا وَبَرَكَـٰتٍ عَلَیۡكَ وَعَلَىٰۤ أُمَمࣲ مِّمَّن مَّعَكَۚ وَأُمَمࣱ سَنُمَتِّعُهُمۡ ثُمَّ یَمَسُّهُم مِّنَّا عَذَابٌ أَلِیمࣱ.

"Nooh (as) ne arz kiya ke Aye mere Rab! Mein Tujhse Panah chahta hun ke mein Tujhse us cheez ka sawal karun jiska mujhe Ilm nahi. Agar Tu ne mujhe Ma'af na kiya aur mujh par Rahem na kiya to mein Khasara uthane walon mein se ho jaonga."

"Hukm hua Aye Nooh (as)! Utar ja, Hamari taraf se tujh par Salaamti aur Barkaten hain aur un girohon par bhi Salaamti aur Barkaten hain jo tere saath hain. Aur kuchh giroh aise bhi hain jinko Ham kuchh muddat ka liye samaane e Zindagi Bakhshenge. Phir unhe Hamari taraf se Dardnak Azaab pahunchnega."

(Surah Hud: 47 - 48)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) jaari hai:

⛵

Akhir kar Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Kishti Judi Pahad par ruki aur wahan unko utarne ka Hukm hua aur Allah ki Salamti wa Barkaton ka dilasa dilaya. Us Jagah par Hazrat Nooh (as) ne ek Masjid bhi banwayi. Tufaan ke baad poora nizaam dirham barham ho gaya tha. Ek nayi Zindagi ki phir se shuruat karni thi.

Is Waqae mein Hazrat Nooh (as) ne apne Bete ke bare mein darkhwast ki. Kyonki Aap (as) bhi ek Baap the to Bete ko Azaab mein gharq hota nahi dekh paye. Sawal uthta hai ke Paighambar hote hue bhi unhone aisa kiya aur phir Khuda se Ma'afi ke bhi talbagar hue.

Paighambar Masoom hota hai, usse koi Gunah sarzad nahi hota. Jo zikr hua hai wo Khuda ki Nafarmani mein shumar nahi hota. Isko Tark e Aula kehte hain, yani jo munasib aur behtar tha usko chhod diya. Jaisa ke pehle zikr kar chuke hain Ilm e Ghaib wa Qudrat sab Khuda ke haath mein hai. Woh jab Chaahta hai deta, jab Chaahta hai salb kar leta hai, ye Uski Maslahet hai. Isliye ye nahi keh sakte ke unko Ilm e Ghaib nahi tha. Doosri baat ye hai ke Nabi wa Imam ek namoona e Amal (Ideal) hota hai. Insaan unse seekhta hai aur unko copy karta hai. Ye sab kar ke unhone hame Tauba o Isteghfar aur ghuroor o Takabbur se door rehne aur Inkesaari ka Dars diya. Yehi wajah hai ke Allah ne Insaano mein se hi Nabi ko muntakhib kiya, warna ye kaam Farishton se bhi karwa sakta tha.

(To be Cont'd....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 😏

*Paighambar e Islam (saww):

مَن غَشَّ مُسلِمًا فَلَيسَ مِنَّا

"Jo Musalman Bhaiyyon se Dhokabazi aur Khayanat kare woh ham mein se nahi hai."

(Safeenatul Bihar, V-2, P-318)

😋

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

مَن سَمِعَ رَجُلاً يُنَادِى، يَا للمُسلِمِين فَلَم يَجِبهُ فَلَيسَ بِمُسلِم.

"Jo shakhs kisi Insaan ki awaaz sune jo pukar raha ho: Aye Musalmano! Meri madad ko pahuncho aur koi us par Labbaik na kahe, woh Musalman nahi hai."

(Usoole Kaafi, Vol-2, P-164)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Parwardigar! Tujhe Qasam hai: Tere Masoom Nabi (saww) ki, Tere Hatmi Ahkam ki, Tere muqarrarah manhiyyat ki. Aur us Pak o Pakeeza Qabr ki jiske pehlu mein Mahsoom, Maqtool aur Mazloom Imam Dafn hain, ke Tu mujhe Duniya ke Ghamon se Nijaat ata farma......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

              29th Safar 1442

  17th October 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT NOOH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1542)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

تِلۡكَ مِنۡ أَنۢبَاۤءِ ٱلۡغَیۡبِ نُوحِیهَاۤ إِلَیۡكَۖ مَا كُنتَ تَعۡلَمُهَاۤ أَنتَ وَلَا قَوۡمُكَ مِن قَبۡلِ هَـٰذَاۖ فَٱصۡبِرۡۖ إِنَّ ٱلۡعَـٰقِبَةَ لِلۡمُتَّقِینَ

 "Ye Ghaib ki khabaren hain jo Ham tumhe Wahy kar rahe hain. Isse pehle Aapko in waqeaat ka Ilm nahi tha aur na hi Aapki Qaum ko Ilm tha. Aap Sabr karen, Anjaamkar Ahle Taqwa ke liye hai."

(Surah Hud: 49)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) ka last part aapki khidmat mein pesh hai:

⛵

Qur'an mein mukhtalif maqam par Allah Ta'ala To ne hame guzishta Paighambar aur unke aur unki Qaum ke halaat pesh kiye hain taake in waqeaat se ham kuchh Ibrat hasil karen. Hazrat Nooh (as) ke waqeaat ab yahan khatm hote hain aur ainda doosre Anbiya ka tazkra hoga.

⚰️

Wafaat Hazrat Nooh (as):

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Tufaan ke baad Hazrat Nooh (as) 50 Baras mazeed  zinda rahe. Jab unki zindagi ke akheri Ayyam aye to Jibrael Amin (as) unke paas aaye aur kaha ke ab Aap (as) ki Nabuwwat ka Zamana khatm ho raha hai aur Aap (as) ki Zindagi ke Din poore hone wale hain. Aap (as) Ism e Azm, Miraas e Ilm aur Ilm e Nabuwwat ke asaar apne Farzand Saam sipurd kar den. Aap (as) ne is par amal kiya.

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🌿

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Nooh (as) ki kul Zindagi 2300 Saalon par mushtamil thi aur Aapne 850 Saal ki Umr mein Ailaan e Nabuwwat kiya aur 950 Baras tak Aap (as) ne Nabuwwat ki Tableegh ki thi aur Tufaan ke baad Aap (as) ne 500 Baras tak Zindagi basar ki. Is dauran Aapne kai Shaher abaad kiye aur apni Aulad ko Shehron mein rihaish dilai."

"Akhirkar Jaame Zindagi labrez ho gaya. Malakul Maut Aap (as) ke paas aa pahuncha. Us waqt Aap (as) Dhoop mein baithe the. Usne Aap (as) ko Salaam kiya. Aap (as) ne Salaam ka Jawab diya aur farmaya kaise aana hua? Usne kaha Aap (as) ki Rooh qabz karne ke liye aaya hun. Aap (as) ne kaha itni ijazat do ke Dhoop se Chhaon mein aa jaon. Usne ijazat de di. Aap (as) ne usse kaha: _"Mujhe apni tamam Zindagi yun mehsoos hoti hai jaise mein Dhoop se uth kar Chhaon mein aaya hun."

(Rauza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🍃

(Kuchh Riwayat mein Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Umr 2500 Saal batayi gayi hai.)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as) se jab Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) ki Qabr e Muthhar ke bare mein poochha, to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Woh apne Waalid Hazrat Nooh (as) ki Qabr mein Dafn hue the. Hazrat Nooh (as) pushte Kufa Najaf e Ashraf mein madfoon hue."

(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

(The End...Tamaam)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Momin ki Nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske chehre ka rang jitna sufaid tha us se zyada sufaid aur raushan ho jaata hai, Pehshani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski Aa'nkho’n se Aa'nsuo’n ki tarah rutubat behne lagti hai; to yehi uski Rooh nikalne ki nishaani hai…"

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (as):

"......Mere Muqaddar ki Burayi aur Sharr ko mujh se door kar de aur mujhe Zehrili Aag se bacha le. Bare Ilaha! Tu Apni Ne'mat ke tufail mujhe Izzat o Aabru marhamat farma, mujhe Apni Taqseem ki hui Rozi par raazi rakh, mujhe Apne Karam aur Jood o Sakha se dhanp le, nez mujhe Apni Nagawari aur Naraazgi se mehfooz farma de......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

   18th October 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1543)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِلَىٰ عَادٍ أَخَاهُمۡ هُودࣰاۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ ٱعۡبُدُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ مَا لَكُم مِّنۡ إِلَـٰهٍ غَیۡرُهُۥۤۖ إِنۡ أَنتُمۡ إِلَّا مُفۡتَرُونَ *  یَـٰقَوۡمِ لَاۤ أَسۡـَٔلُكُمۡ عَلَیۡهِ أَجۡرًاۖ إِنۡ أَجۡرِیَ إِلَّا عَلَى ٱلَّذِی فَطَرَنِیۤۚ أَفَلَا تَعۡقِلُونَ.

 "Aur (Qaume) Aad ki taraf Hamne unke bhai Hud (as) ko rawana kiya. Usne kaha: Aye Braderane Qaum! Allah ki Ibaadat karo. Uske alawa koi tumhara Ma'bood (Deity) nahi. Tumne to mehez Jhoot ghadh rakha hain."

"Aye meri Qaum! Is Tableegh par mein tum se koi Ujrat nahi maangta. Meri Ujrat Uske Zimme hai Jisne mujhe paida kiya hai. Kya phir bhi tum Aql se kaam nahi lete?"

(Surah Hud: 50 - 51)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Surah mein 5 Azeem Anbiya ka Tazkara hai. Sab Anbiya ki Dawat Tauheed ki jaanib thi.

Tazkara Hazrat Nooh (as) ke baad ab Hazrat Hud (as) ke waqae ki shuruat hoti hai:

🌿

Qaum e Aad ek Baadya Nashin, Khana Badosh (Nomadic tribe) Qaum thi. Unka Watan "Shaqooq - شقوق, se "Ajfar - اجفر" tak chaar manazil mein phaila hua tha. Woh Kashtkari (Farming) karte the aur bahut zyada Khajooren payi jati thin. Unki Umren bahut taweel (long Aged) aur Jism bade mazboot hote the. Woh Buton ki pooja karte the (Idol Worshippers).

🏣

Aad (Ad) bin Uz bin Aram bin Saam (Shem) bin Nooh (Noah)(as). Aad ke bete the Shadid aur Shaddad.

🏦

Allah ne unki Hidayat ke liye Hazrat Hud (as) (Eber) ko mab'oos farmaya. Aad ki Hukumat Southern Arabia, Persian Gulf Umman se Hazramaut, Yemen aur Red Sea tak phaili hui thi. Aaj bhi Hazrat Hud (as) ki Qabr Hazramaut mein ek Mazar ki surat mein hai.

Qur'an ne inke maqam ko Al-Ahqaf (The Sandy Plains) ke naam se zikr kiya hai jo ke Southern Arabia, Yemen, Western Oman ka elaqa hai.  Iram of the pillars Aad ka Capital tha.

Hazrat Hud (as) ne unhe Islam qubool karne aur But Parasti chhodne ki dawat di lekin unhone Aap (as) par Imaan laana gawara na kiya aur unhone apne Paighambar ko takleefen di.

Jaise ke pehle bhi zikr ho chuka hai Nabi kisi se Ujrat na leta hai aur na woh koi Inaam o Ikraam ka khwahish mand rehta hai. Usko Allah ki taraf se Ajr milta hai.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sajjad (as)

ne Shayar e Ahlebait (as) Kameet Asadi se mukhatib ho kar farmaya, "Aye Kameet! Hum tumhare ash'aar ka Ajr o Sawaab dene se qaasir (asamarth) hain." To Kameet ne arz ki, "Maula! Aap to mujh par bas itna Ehsaan farmayen ke apne jism e at'haar se mas-shuda libaas ba-taur e tabarruq mujhe marhamat farma de'n."

(Azadari Kyun?, p39)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Parwardigar! Laghzishon (Slips) se meri hifazat farma. Mere Qaul o Amal ko durust kar de. Meri muddat e Umr ko badha de. Mujhe Dard o Amraaz (Diseases) se aafiyat ata farma de. Aur mujhe Aimma (as) ke sadqe aur Apne Fazl o Karam ke tufail behtareen Ummeedon tak pahucha de....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

       2nd Rabiul Awwal 1442

   20th October 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) - ISTEGHFAR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1544)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ ٱسۡتَغۡفِرُوا۟ رَبَّكُمۡ ثُمَّ تُوبُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡهِ یُرۡسِلِ ٱلسَّمَاۤءَ عَلَیۡكُم مِّدۡرَارࣰا وَیَزِدۡكُمۡ قُوَّةً إِلَىٰ قُوَّتِكُمۡ وَلَا تَتَوَلَّوۡا۟ مُجۡرِمِینَ

"Aye meri Qaum! Apne Rab se Maghferat talab karo, phir Uski taraf rujoo' karo. Woh tum par moosladhar Baarish barsayega aur tumhari maujoodah Quwwat mein mazeed Quwwat ka izaafa karega aur Mujrim ban kar Munh na phero."

(Surah Hud: 52)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Hud (as) apni Qaum ko Tableegh e Deen karte rahe aur unhe Aqeeda e Tauheed apnane aur But Parasti chhodne ki dawat dete rahe aur Aap (as) ne apni Qaum ko 4 Buniyadi Nukaat ki Dawat di:

1. Allah ko Wahdahu La Sharik maano.

2. BUT PARASTI chhod do.

3. Khuda ke Huzoor Isteghfar karo.

4. Khuda ki taraf rujoo' karo.

Isteghfar aur Tauba ke Aapne do fayde bataye:

1. Agar tum Tauba o Isteghfar karoge to tumhari Khushk haali (Dryness) khatm ho jayegi, tum par moosladhar Baarish barsegi.

2. Khuda tumhari maujooda Quwwat mein mazeed izaafa karega.

Allah ne unki Hidayat ke liye Hazrat Hud (as) ko mab'oos farmaya. Aapne unhe Islam qubool karne aur But Parasti chhodne ki dawat di lekin unhone Aap (as) par Imaan laana gawara na kiya aur unhone apne Paighambar ko takleefen di. Allah Ta'ala ne unke liye Barish ka Silsila rok diya aur musalsal 7 Baras tak Baarish na barsi aur Baarish na hone ki wajah se Qahet (Famine) pad gaya.

Hazrat Hud (as) bhi ek Kashtkar the, un par bhi iska asar pada. Logon Hazrat Hud (as) ke ghar par pahunche taak unse darkhwast karen ke woh unke liye Khuda se Dua karen. Hazrat (as) ghar par nahi the to unki Budhi Biwi ne kaha ke agar unki Dua qubool hoti to unke Khet nahi murjhate.

Un logon ki Hazrat Hud (as) se bahar mulaqat hui aur Biwi ke qaul ke bare mein bataya. Hazrat Hud (as) ne ne farmaya ke mein uske liye Lambi Umr ke liye Dua karta hun. Unhe ye sun kar ajeeb laga. Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Har Momin ka koi na koi Dushman zaroor hota hai, jo use aziyyat pahunchata rehta hai aur ye bhi meri Dushman hai. Albatta woh meri aisi Dushman hai jo mere zare dast (under control) hai. Khuda ka shukr hai us ne mujhe kisi zabardast Dushman ke hawale nahi kiya."

(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

Isse pata chalta hai ke Zauja e Paighambar hona koi Fazilat nahi. Aise kai Nabiyon ki Biwiyan guzri hai jo khuda Paighambar ki khilafwarzi karti thin. Balke ek to Nabi ki qatil bhi hai. Inke naam aur Ishaare Qur'an mein maujood hain.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 Riwayat:

Raavi kehta hai ke mein Hasan ke paas tha. Ek shakhs darwaze se dakhil hua, usne apni Abaadi mein khushkhaali (dryness) ki shikayat ki. Hasan ne usse kaha: "Isteghfar karo." Doosra aaya usne Faqro Faqa ki shikayat ki. Usse bhi kaha: "Isteghfar karo." Teesra aaya, usne kaha ke Dua karen ke Khuda mujhe Beta ata kare. Usse bhi kaha: "Isteghfar karo." Raavi ko tajjub hua ke har sawal par jawab de rahe ho *"Isteghfar karo."* Hasan ne kaha ke jo kuchh meine kaha wo apni taraf se nahi balke maine ye matlab Kalaame Khuda se liya hai. Quran mein hai: _"Unse meine kaha apne Gunahon se apne Parwardigar ki Bargah mein Isteghfar karo ke Woh Bakhshne wala hai taake Woh pai dar pai tum par Aasmaan se Baarish barsaye aur Maal aur Aulad ke zariye tumhari Madad kare....." (Nooh:10-12)

----------------------------------------------

🤲🏻

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Khuda wanda! Muhammad (saww) wa Aale Muhammad (as) par Darood nazil farma, meri Tauba qubool farma le, mere Aansuon par Rahem farma, meri takleef aur ranj o gham mein mera Munis o Ghamkhwar ban ja, meri khatayen Ma'af farma de aur meri Aulad ko Saeed o Saleh bana de....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       3rd Rabiul Awwal 1442

21st October 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1545)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰهُودُ مَا جِئۡتَنَا بِبَیِّنَةࣲ وَمَا نَحۡنُ بِتَارِكِیۤ ءَالِهَتِنَا عَن قَوۡلِكَ وَمَا نَحۡنُ لَكَ بِمُؤۡمِنِینَ *  إِن نَّقُولُ إِلَّا ٱعۡتَرَىٰكَ بَعۡضُ ءَالِهَتِنَا بِسُوۤءࣲۗ قَالَ إِنِّیۤ أُشۡهِدُ ٱللَّهَ وَٱشۡهَدُوۤا۟ أَنِّی بَرِیۤءࣱ مِّمَّا تُشۡرِكُونَ

"Unhone kaha: Ay Hud (as)! Tum hamare paas koi wazeh Nishani to le kar nahi aaye aur tere kehne par ham apne Khudaon ko nahi chhod sakte aur ham tum par Imaan laane wale nahi hain. Ham to ye samajhte hain ke hamare ma'boodon mein se tum par kisi ki maar pad gayi hai."

"Hud (as) ne kaha: Mein Allah ko Gawah banata hun aur tum bhi Gawah raho ke tum jo Shirk kar rahe ho, mein usse Bezaar hun."

(Surah Hud: 53 - 54)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Unka kehna tha ke Nabi ke paas koi Daleel nahi hai. Jabke Nabi Mojeza dikhata hai. Usko bhi unhone jhutlaya aur usko keh diya ke ye to Jadu hai. Ham pehle zikr kar chuke hain ke Mojeza aur Jadu mein kya farq hai. Jabke Hazrat Hud (as) Haqeeqat Parwardigar ki taraf Dawat de rahe the aur woh log But Parasti nahi chhod rahe the. But Parasti ke liye koi zyada Daleelon ki zaroorat bhi nahi hai. Jo shakhs thoda sa bhi shaoor, Aql rakhta hai, woh But Parasti ki taraf nahi jayega. Ye sab Behoodgi hai. Unki Behoodgi ka jawab Hazrat Hud (as) in Kalamaat e Tauheed se diya. Shirk ka inkaar kiya.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Ya Allah! Main na Tere siwa kisi ko apne gunah ka bakshne waala paata hoo'n, na apne aibo'n ki koi purdah-poshi karne wala, aur na apne kisi amal ko achche amal se badalne waala. Nahi hai koi Maabud magar Tu! Main Tujhe paak samajhta hoo'n aur Teri Hamd o Sana karta hoo'n. Beshak maine apne upar zulm kiya hai, aur apni nadaani se badi himmat ki hai aur kyun ki Tu hamesha mujh par ehsaan karta raha hai aur Teri yaad mere dil mein baithhi hui hai, isi se itminaan kar liya."

(Dua e Kumail)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Rabbe Jaleel! Is Azeem Baargah aur ba-Karamat maqam par mere tamam Gunah bakhsh de, mere saare Gham door kar de, mere Rizq mein wus'at ata farma ke fursat na mile, aur mujh par itna Fazl o Karam kar ke mein tamam Makhlooqaat se beniyaaz ho jaon........"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

  22nd October 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1546)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

مِن دُونِهِۦۖ فَكِیدُونِی جَمِیعࣰا ثُمَّ لَا تُنظِرُونِ *  إِنِّی تَوَكَّلۡتُ عَلَى ٱللَّهِ رَبِّی وَرَبِّكُمۚ مَّا مِن دَاۤبَّةٍ إِلَّا هُوَ ءَاخِذُۢ بِنَاصِیَتِهَاۤۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی عَلَىٰ صِرَ ٰ⁠طࣲ مُّسۡتَقِیمࣲ.

"Tum mere khilaf mil jul kar jo bhi sazish karna chaho wo kar lo aur mujhe bilkul mohlat na do. Meine Allah par Bharosa kiya hai, jo mera aur tumhara Rab hai aur Woh har Jaandar ki Peshani ko pakde hue hai. Beshak mera Rab Seedhe Raaste par hai."

(Surah Hud: 55 - 56)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Hud (as) ne alal ailan (openly) unse Tabarrah kiya, upar se kaha ke woh unke khilaf unke Khudaon ki madad se jo karna chahe kar le, woh unka kuchh nahi bigaad sakte. Kyonki unhone ye kaha tha ke un par inke Buton ka bura asar ho gaya hai isliye aisi baaten kar rahe hain. Aap (as) ne kaha ke unhe Allah par poora Bharosa hai, phir darna kiya. *ناصية* yani Peshani ke Baal. Jab kisi ko apne control mein pakad kar rakhna hota hai to uske saamne ke Baal pakad kar khechte hain.

🕌 🛤️

إِنَّ رَبِّی عَلَىٰ صِرَ ٰ⁠طࣲ مُّسۡتَقِیمࣲ.

Hazrat Ali (as):

" Allah ka Siraate Mustaqeem par hone ka mafhoom ye hai ke Allah Ehsaan ka Badla Ehsaan aur Burai ka Badla Burai ki surat mein deta hai aur jise chahta hai Ma'af kar deta hai."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🛣️

Nihayat hi Khubsurat jumla hai. Khuda ki aisi Qudrat jo Adalat amez hai, Uske bare mein ye zebatareen taabiraat mein se hai. Kyonki aam taur par Taqatwar Jhoote aur Zalim hote hain lekin Allah apni be intiha Qudrat ke bawajood hamesha Adalat ki Siraat e Mustaqeem par hai. Uska Raasta hamesha Hikmat, Nazm aur Hisaab o Kitaab ka Saaf o Shafaaf Raasta raha hai.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Aye Khuda! Agar Tu chaahe to Apne Fazal se humko maaf kar sakta hai aur agar Tu humko azaab karna chaahe to Tere Adl ke sabab se hoga."

(Sahifa e Kaamila, Dua No.10)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".....Mere Palanhar! Mein Tujh se Nafa Bakhs Ilm, Teri jaanib jhukne wale Dil, Pukhta Imaan, Pakeeza aur Mukhlisana Amal, Misaali Sabr, aur be-panah Ajr o Sawab ka Talabgaar hun....."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

      23rd October 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1547)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَإِن تَوَلَّوۡا۟ فَقَدۡ أَبۡلَغۡتُكُم مَّاۤ أُرۡسِلۡتُ بِهِۦۤ إِلَیۡكُمۡۚ وَیَسۡتَخۡلِفُ رَبِّی قَوۡمًا غَیۡرَكُمۡ وَلَا تَضُرُّونَهُۥ شَیۡـًٔاۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَیۡءٍ حَفِیظࣱ.

"Agar tum Munh pherto ho to pher lo, mujhe jo Paigham de kar bheja gaya tha wo Paigham meine tumhe pahuncha diya hai. Mera Rab tumhari jagah aur Qaum ko le aayega aur tum Uska kuchh bhi bigad na sakoge. Beshak mera Rab har cheez ka Nigehban hai."

(Surah Hud: 57)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Hud (as) apni Qaum ko tanbi karte rahe. Yahan is Ayat mein unhone zahir kiya ke agar woh Imaan nahi laate hain jaisa ke unhone khud kaha tha to unka koi nuqsaan nahi honewala. Nabi ya Rasool ki duty hoti hai ke woh Allah ki taraf se jo Paigham laya hai apni Qaum tak pahuncha de, baaqi Allah khud unko dekh lega. Woh ek jhatke mein poori Qaum ko neest o nabood karke doosri Qaum ko unki jagah le aayega, kyonki poori Kaynaat Allah ke haath mein hai, koi Uska kuchh nahi bigad sakta.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Ambiya e Karaam (as) mein se kuchh aise the jinki Nabuwwat ka daayra aam tha aur zyada-tar aise hain jinki daawat ka daayra khaas tha. Chunaanche, Hazrat Nuh (as) ki Nabuwwat tamaam ahle zameen ke liye thi, jab ke Hazrat Hud (as) ki Nabuwwat qaum e Aad ke liye makhsoos thi…"

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p93)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"Mere Allah! Tu ne mujh par jo farawan Ne'maten nazil farmayi hain Tu hi mujhe unke bare mein Shukro sipaas ki Taufeeq ata farma aur iske natije mein mujh par Ehsaan o Karam mein izaafa farma."

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

       6th Rabiul Awwal 1442

  24th October 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1548)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُنَا نَجَّیۡنَا هُودࣰا وَٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ مَعَهُۥ بِرَحۡمَةࣲ مِّنَّا وَنَجَّیۡنَـٰهُم مِّنۡ عَذَابٍ غَلِیظࣲ.

"Phir jab Hamara Hukm aa gaya to Hamne Apni Rehmat se Hud (as) ko aur jo log us par Imaan laye the Najaat de di aur Hamne unhe Sakht Azaab se mehfooz rakha."

(Surah Hud: 58)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Jis tarah Allah Ta'ala ne Qaum Nooh (as) par Azaab se aane se pehle sab ko Kashti mein sawar karwa ke sab Ahle Imaan ko Najaat di thi, us tarah jab Hazrat Hud (as) ki Qaum par Azaab aaya to pehle Allah Ta'ala ne Apni Rehmat se Ahle Imaan ko Najaat di. Chunke Allah Adil hai, Woh sab ka khayal rakhta hai.

Is Ayat mein نجينا do bar repeat hua hai. Pehli Najaat Duniyavi Azaab se Najaat di, jabke doosri Najaat Akherat ke Azaab se hai. Akherat ke Azaab ko عذاب غليظ ka naam diya hai. Ye lafz Qur'an mein 4 jagah par aaya hai: (11:58), (14:17), (31:24), (41:50).

Beshak Duniyavi Azaab Ukhravi Azaab ke muqabile kuchh bhi nahi Qayamat ka Azaab Ghaleez qism ka Azaab hai.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Aisi Aag se daro jiski gehraayi bahut zyada hai, garmi bahut sakht hai aur Azaab har roz naya hai.."

(Tajalliyat e Hikmat)

🔥

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Qayamat ke din us shakhs ko sakht-tareen Azaab diya jayega to zabaan se Adl ki taarif kare aur apne Amal se uski mukhalefat kare."

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p137)

🔥

Imam Kazim (as):

" Jab bhi log Naye Naye qism ke gunah karte hain to Allah unhe naye naye qism ke Azaab mein daalta hai."

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p171)

Jab naye naye Gunah hote hain, nayi nayi Bimaariyan bhi paida hoti hain.

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"......(Bare Ilaha!) Logon ke darmiyan mere Qaul mein taseer ata kar, mere Amal ko Apni Bargah mein bulandi ata farma, mujhe aisa bana de ke meri Nekiyon ki pairavi ki jaane lage, aur mere Dushman ko tabah o barbad kar de..... "

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

     25th October 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ HAZRAT HUD (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1549)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَتِلۡكَ عَادࣱۖ جَحَدُوا۟ بِـَٔایَـٰتِ رَبِّهِمۡ وَعَصَوۡا۟ رُسُلَهُۥ وَٱتَّبَعُوۤا۟ أَمۡرَ كُلِّ جَبَّارٍ عَنِیدࣲ *  وَأُتۡبِعُوا۟ فِی هَـٰذِهِ ٱلدُّنۡیَا لَعۡنَةࣰ وَیَوۡمَ ٱلۡقِیَـٰمَةِۗ أَلَاۤ إِنَّ عَادࣰا كَفَرُوا۟ رَبَّهُمۡۗ أَلَا بُعۡدࣰا لِّعَادࣲ قَوۡمِ هُودࣲ.

"Ye hain Aad apne Rab ki Ayaat se unhone inkaar kiya aur uske Rasoolon ki Nafarmani ki aur unhone har Jabbar Sarkash ke hukm ki pairavi ki thi. Is Duniya aur Roze Qayamat mein unke peechhe La'anat ko lagaya gaya. Agah raho! Qaum e Aad ne apne Parwardigar ka inkaar kiya tha. Agah raho! Hud (as) ki Qaum e Aad ke liye doori hai. (door ho)"

(Surah Hud: 59 - 60)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Qaum e Aad ke log sakht buland qamat the. Unke qad ko Khajoor ke darakhton se tashbi di gayi hai. Isi munasibat se unki Imaarten mazboot, badi aur unchi rehti thi. Yahan tak ke Arab bhi buland aur mazboot Imaarton ki nisbat Qaum e Aad se dete the.

Unke 3 Gunah the:

1. Unhone Parwardigar ki Ayaat ka Inkaar kiya. Khuda ka Numainda, Rehbar khud ek Ayat hota hai.

2. Anbiya (as) ki Nafarmani aur Sarkashi ki. Yani ek Nabi ki Nafarmani sabhi Anbiya ki Nafarmani hai.

3. Hukm e Khuda chhod kar Haq ke Dushmanon ki pairavi ki.

Jabbar use kehte jo apni Taqat, zor zabardasti se sabhi ko apne followers banata hai. عنيد yani jo Haq ki mukhalifat kare.

Allah ki Sifat bhi Jabbar hai.

Lekin ek hi Sifat mansoob ke mutabiq ma'ana o mafhoom mein badalti hai.

Misaal ke taur par Insaan Takabbur karta hai, jo ke mazmoom (Condemn) lafz hai, jabke yehi Allah ke liye istemal karen to mamdooh ho jayga. Ek hi lafz ke mafhoom Khaliq o Makhlooq mein badal jate hain. Chunke Allah Khaliq hai, Bada hai, Akbar hai, Qudrat wala hai, Sara Takabbur Uske liye, Qadrat rakhta hai, isliye Jabbar o Qahar bhi hai.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Asma o Sifaat:

Ek shakhs ne Imam Ali Naqi (as) se sawal kiya:

"Kitab e Khuda mein Allah ke Sifaat mazkoor hain, kya wo Sifaat Ain e Zaat hain?

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Iske do mafhoom hain: Ham apne Rab ko "Qawi - قوى (Powerful)" kehte hain, lekin Uski Quwwat ko Makhlooq (creature) ki quwwat par qayas karna sahih nahi hai. Warna Tashbih (Similarity) lazim aayegi aur is mein izaafa (addition) ka bhi ehtemal ho to wahan kami ja bhi ehtemal ho sakta hai. Aur jab kami waaqe ho jaye to Woh "Qadeem - قديم (Everlasting)" nahi rahega aur agar Qadeem na raha to phir use Aajiz (Helpless) maanna padega."_

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

"..... Aye Jahano ke Palanhaar! Tu Apne Behtareen Bandon yani Muhammad (saww) aur Aale Muhammad (as) par Shabo Roz Apni Rehmaten aur Darood nazil farma, aur mujhe buron ke shar se mehfooz kar de, Gunahon se paak farma de. Mere bojh utar de. Mujhe Sukoon o qaraar ki jagah yani Jannat mein jagah de......"

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

       8th Rabiul Awwal 1442

   26th October 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT SALEH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1550)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِلَىٰ ثَمُودَ أَخَاهُمۡ صَـٰلِحࣰاۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ ٱعۡبُدُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ مَا لَكُم مِّنۡ إِلَـٰهٍ غَیۡرُهُۥۖ هُوَ أَنشَأَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَٱسۡتَعۡمَرَكُمۡ فِیهَا فَٱسۡتَغۡفِرُوهُ ثُمَّ تُوبُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡهِۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی قَرِیبࣱ مُّجِیبࣱ

"Aur Samood ki taraf Hamne unke Bhai Saleh ko bheja. Usne kaha Aye meri Qaum! Allah ki Ibaadat karo aur Uske alawa koi tumhara Ma'bood nahi hai. Usi ne tumhe Zameen se Paida kiya aur tumhe Zameen mein abaad kiya. Tum Usse Maghferat talab karo. Phir Uski taraf rujoo' karo. Beshak mera Rab Qareeb aur Duaon ko qubool Karnewala hai."

(Surah Hud: 61)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Hud (as) ke baad Hazrat Saleh (as) ke Zikr ka Silsila shuru hota hai:

🕌

Hazrat Saleh (as) ko Qaum-e-Samood ke darmiyan bheja gaya taake unki Hidayat karen.

Qaum-e-Samood (Thamud) Madina aur Syria ke darmiyan Wadi-ul-Qura mein rehti thi. Kuchh tarikh mein hain ke Hegra ya Madaen mein rehti thi.

Hazrat Hud (as) ki tarah Aap (as) ko bhi unki Qaum ke Bhai se mukhatib kiya hai. Ye Isliye ke yun to sabhi H. Adam (as) ki Aulad ki haisiyyat se Bhai hain, doosre ye ke Aap (as) ke apni Qaum ke saath rawayya ek bhai ki tarah aur apni beradari wala tha. Yani Qaum Hazrat Saleh (as) ko apno mein ka maane, koi ghair nahi.

Hazrat Saleh (as) ne bhi Tauheed ki Tableegh aur But Parasti ki nafi ki.

Insaan ko be qadr o qeemat Mitti se banaya aur usi mitti par abaad hone ke zarai mohayya kiye, to kis baat par Insaan Ghamand o Takabbur karta hai. Mitti se bana mitti mein mil jayega.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Aye Ali (as)! Main aur Aap dono ek Teenat (Mitti) se khalq kiye gaye hain. Aur jo Mitti us Mitti se bach gayi usse hamare Shiyo'n ko khalq kiya gaya hai aur jab Qayamat ka din hoga to logo'n ko unki Maa ke naam se pukara jaayega siwaaye Aap ke Shiyo'n ke. Pus unko unke baap ke Naam se pukara jaayega, kyunki unki wilaadat paak hai."

(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p208)

🤲🏻

Imam Mahdi (atfs):

".......Nez mujhe aur Mo'meneen o Mo'menaat mein se mere tamam Bhaiyyon aur Behnon, Aizza o Aqroba ko bakhsh de. Aye sab Rahem karnewalon se zyada Rahem karne wale Apni Rehmat ki Tasdeeq, meri ilteja ko qabool farma le." (The End)

(Ziyarat-e-Nahiya)

https://youtu.be/oyUPqfDa6e0

💕 Aqde Rasoole Khuda (saww) / Janabe Khadija (sa) Mubarak 💕

       10th Rabiul Awwal 1442

 28th October 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT SALEH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1551)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰصَـٰلِحُ قَدۡ كُنتَ فِینَا مَرۡجُوࣰّا قَبۡلَ هَـٰذَاۤۖ أَتَنۡهَىٰنَاۤ أَن نَّعۡبُدَ مَا یَعۡبُدُ ءَابَاۤؤُنَا وَإِنَّنَا لَفِی شَكࣲّ مِّمَّا تَدۡعُونَاۤ إِلَیۡهِ مُرِیبࣲ *  قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ أَرَءَیۡتُمۡ إِن كُنتُ عَلَىٰ بَیِّنَةࣲ مِّن رَّبِّی وَءَاتَىٰنِی مِنۡهُ رَحۡمَةࣰ فَمَن یَنصُرُنِی مِنَ ٱللَّهِ إِنۡ عَصَیۡتُهُۥۖ فَمَا تَزِیدُونَنِی غَیۡرَ تَخۡسِیر.

"Qaum ke afraad ne kaha: 'Isse pehlo to ham tujh se bahut kuchh Ummeeden lagaye hue the. Kya tu hame in Khudaon ki Ibaadat se rokna chahta hai jinki Ibaadat hamare Aaba o Ajdaad kiya karte the? Hame to is Deen mein hairaan kun shak hai jiski taraf tu bula raha hai."

"Hazrat Saleh (as) ne kaha: 'Aye meri Qaum! Kya tumne is baat par bhi tawajja ki hai. Agar mein apne Rab ki taraf se ek Gawahi rakhta tha, phir Usne Apni taraf se mujhe Rehmat ata ki. Iske baad mujhe Allah ki pakad se kaun bachayega? Agar meine Uski Nafarmani ki. Tum log to mere Khasare mein hi izaafa kar rahe ho."

(Surah Hud: 62 - 63)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Saleh (as) ka Zikr ka Silsila jari hai:

🕌 😏

Qaum e Saleh (as) ne Nafsiyati pehlu ka istemaal kiya. Unhone unse rookhi Muhabbat jatayi, yani woh in se bahut Ummeeden lagaye baithe the, unhe chahte the, apni mushkilaat ka hal inhi se karwate the, inhi se mashware lete the, unki Aql o Sha'oor par Imaan rakhte the, lekin unke apne Deen ki Tableegh ne sab par Paani pher diya. Woh apni Ajdaad ki wirasat mein mili But Parasti ko chhodna nahi chate the.

Yehi haal Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke saath hua, apne Nabuwwat ke ailaan ke pehle poora Jahil Arab Aap (saww) ko Ameen (Secure) aur Sadiq (Sachcha, Truthful) samajhta tha aur inhi alqaab se mashoor bhi the. Ye but Natural hai ke agar koi Ameen aur Sachcha Insaan kuchh kahe to uske qaul par etemad (bharosa) kar lena chahiye, kyonki woh Jhoot to nahi bolega. To agar aisa Insaan hame kuchh ata kare to baghair chun chara ke qabool kar lena chahiye. Yahan par koi Daleel maangne ki zaroorat hi nahi. Inkaar karne walon ke liye do baaten ho sakti hain ke woh Nabi ko Ameen aur Sachcha nahi maan rahe, jabke tarikh mein aisa nahi hai ya maante hue bhi inkaar kar rahe hain. Aap (saww) par Imaan na lana khud unke apne qaul ko jhutlana hai.

Hazrat Saleh (as) ne yehi kaha ke mein Allah ki taraf se ek Numainda ban kar aaya hun, to agar no kaam mujhe sonpa gaya hai woh na karun to Allah ko kya jawab dunga, ye to khasaare ka sauda hai.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as)

se puchha gaya ke Roze Qayamat Najaat paane waale ki pehchaan kya hai? Imam (as) ne farmaya, "Jiska fe'l (action) uske Qaul ke mutaabiq ho (he whose deeds match his words) ke ye Gawahi hogi pesh e Khuda aur jiska fe'l uske Qaul ke muwafiq nahi to uska Imaan aarzi (temporary) hoga."

(Al Kaafi, v1, p93)

🍂

Imam Hasan (as):

"Jo Kaano'n se sune aur uski Tasdeeq (accept) karein wo Imaan hai aur jo Aa'nkho'n se dekhein aur qubool karein wo Yaqeen hai."

(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p49)

🤲🏻

.....اَنْ تُصَلِّيَ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَ اَنْ تَجْعَلَنِيْ فِيْ هٰذَا الْيَوْمِ الَّذِيْ عَقَدْتَ فِيْهِ لِوَلِيِّكَ....

(Dua in Mafateeh)

       11th Rabiul Awwal 1442

   29th October 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT SALEH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1552)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ هَـٰذِهِۦ نَاقَةُ ٱللَّهِ لَكُمۡ ءَایَةࣰۖ فَذَرُوهَا تَأۡكُلۡ فِیۤ أَرۡضِ ٱللَّهِۖ وَلَا تَمَسُّوهَا بِسُوۤءࣲ فَیَأۡخُذَكُمۡ عَذَابࣱ قَرِیبࣱ *  فَعَقَرُوهَا فَقَالَ تَمَتَّعُوا۟ فِی دَارِكُمۡ ثَلَـٰثَةَ أَیَّامࣲۖ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ وَعۡدٌ غَیۡرُ مَكۡذُوبࣲ.

"Aye meri Qaum! Allah ki ye Oontni (She-Camel) tumhare liye ek Nishani hai. Ise azaad chhod do taake Allah ki Zameen par charti phirti rahe. Isse kisi tarah ki burai na karna warna bahut jald tum par Allah ka Azaab aa jayega."

"Unhone Oontni ko maar dala. Saleh (as) ne kaha: Tum apne gharon mein 3 din aur reh lo. Ye Waada hai jo Jhoota sabit na hoga."

(Surah Hud: 64 - 65)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Saleh (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Aye logo! Apne Nabi se Nishaniyan talab na karo. Dekho Qaum e Saleh ne apne Nabi se ye mutaliba kiya tha ke unke liye Pahad se Haamla Oontni baramad ho. Ek din Chashmo ka wo Paani peeti thi aur doosre din Qaum e Saleh Chashmon (Well) ka paani peeti thi. Jis Din Oontni Paani peeti thi us din Qaum-e-Saleh Oontni ka Doodh piya karti thi. Qaum e Saleh ne Sarkashi ki Raah apnayi aur Oontni ko maar dala. Hazrat Saleh (as) ne unse kaha: Ab Khuda ki taraf se 3 din baad tum par Azaab nazil hoga aur ye Khuda ka Sachcha Waada hai. Akhirkar Khuda ka Waada poora hua aur chuthe din us Qaum par Azaab nazil ho gaya. Ek shakhs ke alawa poori Mashriq o Maghrib mein us Qaum ka koi fard baaqi na bacha. Aur jo baaqi bacha tha use bhi Khuda ne isliye baaqi rakha tha ke Nuzoole Azaab ke waqt woh Haram e Khuda mein tha. Is zinda bach jaane wale Shakhs ka naam Abuza'al *ابوزعال* tha. Woh Bani Saqeef ka muris e aala tha."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🐪

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Jo shakhs kisi Momin ko sawaari de kar paidal chalne se bachayega to Allah Qayamat ke din usko Naqaa e Behisht (Jannat ke Oont) se ek aisa Oont sawaari ke liye inaayat karega jiske sabab woh Farishto'n par bhi fakhr karega."

(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p286)

🍂

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab banda koi Gunah karta hai to chaahe wo Aalim ho, magar jis waqt apne nafs ko apne Parwardigar ki na-farmani mein daalta hai, to us waqt wo jaahil ho jaata hai."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p85)

🍃

Imam Ali (as):

"Allah ki itni Ibadat karo jitni tumhe Allah ki zarurat hai, Allah ki itni na-farmani karo jitna Allah ke azaab par sabr kar sakte ho, Duniya ke liye itne aamaal karo jitna tumhe is duniya mein rehna hai, Akherat ke liye itne aamaal karo jitna tumhe wahaa'n rehna hai."

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p101)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ ۟اِلْاَئِمَّةِ الْقَادَةِ وَ الدُّعَاةِ السَّادَةِ وَ النُّجُوْمِ الزَّاهِرَةِ وَ الْاَعْلَامِ الْبَاهِرَةِ وَ سَاسَةِ الْعِبَادِ وَ اَرْكَانِ الْبِلَادِ وَ النَّاقَةِ الْمُرْسَلَةِ وَ السَّفِيْنَةِ النَّاجِيَةِ الْجَارِيَةِ......

(Dua Roze Ghadeer - Mafateeh)

◼️ YAUM-E-GHASBE KHILAFAT ◼️

🐪 Today: Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki Hijrat kar ke Madina Aamad

**********************************

      12th Rabiul Awwal 1442

     30th October 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT SALEH (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1553)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُنَا نَجَّیۡنَا صَـٰلِحࣰا وَٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ مَعَهُۥ بِرَحۡمَةࣲ مِّنَّا وَمِنۡ خِزۡیِ یَوۡمِىِٕذٍۚ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ هُوَ ٱلۡقَوِیُّ ٱلۡعَزِیزُ *  وَأَخَذَ ٱلَّذِینَ ظَلَمُوا۟ ٱلصَّیۡحَةُ فَأَصۡبَحُوا۟ فِی دِیَـٰرِهِمۡ جَـٰثِمِینَ *  كَأَن لَّمۡ یَغۡنَوۡا۟ فِیهَاۤۗ أَلَاۤ إِنَّ ثَمُودَا۟ كَفَرُوا۟ رَبَّهُمۡۗ أَلَا بُعۡدࣰا لِّثَمُودَ.

"Jab Hamare Faisle ka waqt aa gaya to Hamne Saleh (as) aur jo un par Imaan laye the Apni Rehmat se unhe Najaat di aur Hamne unhe us Din ki ruswai se mehfooz rakha. Beshak tera Rab Saheb e Quwwat aur Ghalib hai."

"Aur Zalimon ko ek bade zor ki Jhankaar ne aa dabocha. Woh apne gharon be-his o harkat aundhe pade hue reh gaye. Goya woh wahan kabhi abaad hi nahi rahe the. Aagah raho! Qaum e Samood ne apne Parwardigar ka inkaar kiya. Doori ho Qaum e Samood ke liya. (door ho)"

(Surah Hud: 66 - 68)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Saleh (as) jaari hai:

🙁😡👨🏿‍🔬🗣️ ⚡👤

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Hazrat Saleh (as) ki Oontni qatl ho gayi, to Hazrat Saleh (as) ne apni Qaum se kaha: 'Kal subah hogi to tumhare Chehre zard (yellow) ho jayenge aur doosre Din tumhare Chehre surkh (red) ho jayenge, aur teesre Din tumhare Chehre siyah (black) ho jayenge aur chauthe Din tum par Azaab aayega aur tum halaak ho jaoge.' Chunanche Subah hui to logon ke Chehre zard ho gaye. Logon ne ek doosre se kaha ke Saleh (as) ki baat sachchi sabit hui to sarkash sardaron ne kaha: 'Ham kabhi bhi Saleh (as) ki baath ko tasleem nahi karenge. Doosra Din hua to sab ke Chehre surkh ho gaye. Sarkash Sardaron ne isse bhi koi Ibrat hasil na ki aur kaha khwah ham halaak hi kyon na ho jayen phir bhi ham Saleh (as) ki baat tasleem nahi karenge. Aur jin Devi Devtaon ko hamare Baap Dada pooja karte the ham unki Ibaadat kabhi nahi chhodenge. Teesre Din unke Chehre Siyah ho gaye. Phir ek doosre se logon ne kaha Saleh (as) ki baat sach sabit ho gayi. Sarkash Sardaron ne tab bhi kaha: Thik hai Saleh (as) ham par Azaab hi bhijwa sakta hai. Ham Azaab bardasht kar lenge lekin Saleh (as) ki baat ko phir bhi nahi maanenge."

"Wo Din guzra Raat hui. Jab aadhi Raat ka waqt hua Jibrael (as) aaye, unhone ek cheekh maari aur aur wo Cheekh itni shadeed thi ke logon ke Kaan ke parde phat gaye, dil dahel gaye aur Jigar kayi hisson mein bat gaye. Qaum  e Saleh ko Maut ka yaqeen ho chuka tha, isiliye sabne Kafan pahen liye the aur Hunoot kar liye the. Jaise hi Cheekh buland hui to palak jhapatte hi tamam afraad halaak ho gaye aur ek bhi zinda na bacha. Allah ka Azaab sirf Cheekh tak hi qaem na raha. Allah ne un par Aag bheji jisne unhe jala kar khaakstar (raakh) kar diya."

Allah Apne Azaab ke pehle kaafi mohlat deta hai. Phir bhi nahi sudhre to unka anjaam aisa hi hota hai.

(The End ......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Oon't (camel) ki tarah gatt-gatt kar ke ek ghoo'nth (ek saa'ns) mein Paani na piyo balke 2 - 3 ghoo'nth kar ke piyo. Jab Paani peene lago to Bismillah padho aur peene ke baad Al Hamdulillah kaho."

(Tibb e Nabi Akram (saww), p31)

🤲🏻

يا ابا صالح ادركنى.
