🍁 Today: End of Bani Umayya Govt.

**********************************

       13th Rabiul Awwal 1442

   31st October 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ HAZRAT IBRAHIM (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1554)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَقَدۡ جَاۤءَتۡ رُسُلُنَاۤ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ بِٱلۡبُشۡرَىٰ قَالُوا۟ سَلَـٰمࣰاۖ قَالَ سَلَـٰمࣱۖ فَمَا لَبِثَ أَن جَاۤءَ بِعِجۡلٍ حَنِیذࣲ *  فَلَمَّا رَءَاۤ أَیۡدِیَهُمۡ لَا تَصِلُ إِلَیۡهِ نَكِرَهُمۡ وَأَوۡجَسَ مِنۡهُمۡ خِیفَةࣰۚ قَالُوا۟ لَا تَخَفۡ إِنَّاۤ أُرۡسِلۡنَاۤ إِلَىٰ قَوۡمِ لُوطࣲ *  وَٱمۡرَأَتُهُۥ قَاۤىِٕمَةࣱ فَضَحِكَتۡ فَبَشَّرۡنَـٰهَا بِإِسۡحَـٰقَ وَمِن وَرَاۤءِ إِسۡحَـٰقَ یَعۡقُوبَ *  قَالَتۡ یَـٰوَیۡلَتَىٰۤ ءَأَلِدُ وَأَنَا۠ عَجُوزࣱ وَهَـٰذَا بَعۡلِی شَیۡخًاۖ إِنَّ هَـٰذَا لَشَیۡءٌ عَجِیبࣱ *  قَالُوۤا۟ أَتَعۡجَبِینَ مِنۡ أَمۡرِ ٱللَّهِۖ رَحۡمَتُ ٱللَّهِ وَبَرَكَـٰتُهُۥ عَلَیۡكُمۡ أَهۡلَ ٱلۡبَیۡتِۚ إِنَّهُۥ حَمِیدࣱ مَّجِیدࣱ.

"Aur Hamare Numainde (Farishte) Ibrahim (as) ke paas Khush khabari le kar gaye, kaha: 'Tum par Salam ho' Ibrahim (as) ne un par Salam kiya. Thodi der baad Ibrahim (as) unki Mehmani ke liye bhuna hua Bachhda le kar aa gaye. Jab Ibrahim (as) ne dekha ke unke Haath khaane ki taraf nahi badh rahe hain to un se ajnabiyat mehsoos kar ke dil hi dil mein un se khauf karne lage. Unhone kaha: 'Daro nahi!, hame Qaum e Lut ki taraf bheja gaya hai."

"Ibrahim (as) ki Biwi khadi thi, woh hans di to Hamne use Ishaaq (as) ki Bashaarat di, aur Ishaaq (as) ke baad Yaqoob (as) ki Bashaarat di. Woh kehne lagi: 'Hay meri badbakhti, kya mein Bachcha janam dungi? Jabke mein Budhi hun aur ye mere Shauhar hain jo ke Budhe hain, yaqeenan ye to ajeeb cheez hai! Farishton ne kaha: 'Kya tum Allah ki Qudrat par tajjub karti ho? Aye Ahle Bait e Ibrahim (as)! Allah ki Rehmat aur Uski Barkaten tum tum par hain. Beshak Woh Qabil e Taarif aur Badi Shaan wala hai."

(Surah Hud: 69 - 73)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Saleh (as) ke Tazkare ke baad Qaum e Lut (as) ka zikr shuru hota hai:

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ne Qaume Lut ko halaak karne ke liye 4 Farishton (Jibrael (as), Mikaeel (as), Israfil (as), Karobil (as)) ko bheja. Woh Amaame bandh kar Ibrahim (as) ke paas se guzre. Unhone Aap (as) ko Salam kiya. Aap (as) ne unhe na pehchana. Aap (as) ne unki Noorani Suraten dekh kar farmaya: "Inki Ziyafat (hospitality) mein apne haathon se hi karunga."

"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) bade Sakhi aur Mehman nawaz shakha the. Aap (as) ne unke liye ek Bachhda zebah kiya aur use bhoon kar unke paas laye lekin Mehmano ke haath Khaane ki taraf na badhe. Aap (as) ko unse khatra aur khauf mehsoos hua. Jab Jibrael (as) ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki ye haalat dekhi to unhone apne Sar se Amaame utara. Aap (as) ne unhe pehchan liya aur kaha ke tum wohi ho na?"

Hazrat Jibrael (as) ne haan mein jawab diya. Itne mein Aap (as) ki Zauja Hazrat Saara (sa) wahan se guzri to Jibrael Amin (as) ne unhe Hazrat Ishaaq (as) ki Bashaarat di. Bibi ne kaha: "Kya mein budhape mein Bachcha janungi, jabke mein Banjh hun aur mera Shauhar Budha hai?"

Farishton ne kaha: Bibi! tumhe tajjub karne ki kya zaroorat hai, Allah ki Rehmat aur Barakaat Ahlebait e Ibrahim (as) ke shamil e haal hain." Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne kaha: "Tumhe bas yahin tak aana tha ya isse aage jaane ka bhi koi iraada hai?"

Unhone kaha: "Ham Qaume Lut ko halaak karne ke liye aaye hain......"

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

﻿Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) pehle insaan the jinki zabaan par Arbi zabaan (Arabic language) jaari hui thi…"

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v1, p249)

🤲🏻

....اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ اَفْضَلَ مَا صَلَّيْتَ عَلٰى اِبْرَاهِيْمَ وَ اٰلِ اِبْرَاهِيْمَ اِنَّكَ حَمِيْدٌ مَجِيْدٌ۔.....

(Salwat Rasoole Khuda (saww) - Mafateeh)

       14th Rabiul Awwal 1442

   1st November 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

  ♦ HAZRAT IBRAHIM (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1555)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا ذَهَبَ عَنۡ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ ٱلرَّوۡعُ وَجَاۤءَتۡهُ ٱلۡبُشۡرَىٰ یُجَـٰدِلُنَا فِی قَوۡمِ لُوطٍ *  إِنَّ إِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمَ لَحَلِیمٌ أَوَّ ٰ⁠هࣱ مُّنِیبࣱ *  یَـٰۤإِبۡرَ ٰ⁠هِیمُ أَعۡرِضۡ عَنۡ هَـٰذَاۤۖ إِنَّهُۥ قَدۡ جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُ رَبِّكَۖ وَإِنَّهُمۡ ءَاتِیهِمۡ عَذَابٌ غَیۡرُ مَرۡدُودࣲ.

"Jab Ibrahim (as) ka khauf door ho gaya aur uske paas Khush Khabari aa gayi to Hamse woh Qaum e Lut ke bare mein kehne sunne laga. Yaqeenan Ibrahim (as) Burdbar, Naram Dil aur Hamari taraf rujoo karnewala tha. (Farishton ne kaha): Ibrahim (as)! Isse baaz aa jao. Tumhare Rab ka Hukm pahunch chuka hai aur un par wo Azaab naazil honewala hai jise tala nahi ja sakta."

(Surah Hud: 74 - 76)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Ibrahim (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as): (Cont'd)

".........Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne kaha: "Tumhe bas yahin tak aana tha ya isse aage jaane ka bhi koi iraada hai?"

Unhone kaha: "Ham Qaume Lut ko halaak karne ke liye aaye hain."

Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne farmaya: "Agar us Qaum mein ek Sau Ahle Imaan bhi maujood hue to kya tum phir bhi unhe halaak karoge?" Jibrael (as) ne kaha: "Nahi." Hazrat (as) ne kaha:" Agar 20 Momin hue to?" Jibrael (as) ne kaha:" Nahi." Hazrat (as) ne kaha: "Agar 10 hue to?" Jibrael (as) ne kaha: "Nahi." Hazrat (as) ne kaha: "Agar 5 Momin hue to?" Jibrael (as) ne kaha: "Nahi." Hazrat (as) ne kaha: "Agar un mein se Ek Momin hua tab?" Jibrael (as): "Agar Ek bhi Momin waha raha to ham Azaab nahi denge."

Ibrahim (as) ne farmaya: "Wahan to Lut (as) bhi rehte hain?"

Farishton ne kaha:

"Ham bakhoobhi jaante hain ke wahan kaun rehta hai. Ham use aur uske Khandan ko Najaat denge magar uski Biwi ko Najaat nahi denge. Woh Peechhe reh jane walon mein se hai." (Al Ankaboot: 32)

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

😞

﻿Imam Hasan (as):

"Hazrat Ibrahim (as) logon ko bachane ke khwahisand the. Khuda ne unke mutalliq farmaya: "Woh Qaume Lut ke mutalliq jhagadne laga tha." (11:74)"

(Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Reza (as):

"Jo shakhs Sharaab aur Shatranj (Chess) ko dekhkar Imam Husain (as) ko yaad kare aur Yazeed paleed aur Ibne Ziyaad bad-nihaad par La'nat kare to Haq Ta'ala uske Gunaho'n ko baksh deta hai agarche Gunah uske shumar mein Sitaaro'n ke barabar ho."

(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v1, p131)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ خُصَّ اَنْتَ اَوَّلَ ظَالِمٍ بِاللَّعْنِ مِنِّىْ وَابْدَاْ بِهٖ اَوَّلًا ثُمَّ الثَّانِيْ وَ الثَّالِثَ وَ الرَّابِعَ اَللّٰهُمَّ الْعَنْ يَزِيْدَ خَامِسًا وَ الْعَنْ عُبَيْدَ اللهِ بْنَ زِيَادٍ وَابْنَ مَرْجَانَةَ وَ عُمَرَبْنَ سَعْدٍ وَ شِمْرًا وَ اٰلَ اَبِيْ سُفْيَانَ وَ اٰلَ زِيَادٍ وَ اٰلَ مَرْوَانَ اِلىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ۔

(Ziyarat-e-Ashura)

       16th Rabiul Awwal 1442

   3rd November 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ HOMOSEXUALITY (LAWAAT) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1556)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَمَّا جَاۤءَتۡ رُسُلُنَا لُوطࣰا سِیۤءَ بِهِمۡ وَضَاقَ بِهِمۡ ذَرۡعࣰا وَقَالَ هَـٰذَا یَوۡمٌ عَصِیبࣱ وَجَاۤءَهُۥ قَوۡمُهُۥ یُهۡرَعُونَ إِلَیۡهِ وَمِن قَبۡلُ كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ.......

"Aur jab Hamare Numainde Lut (as) ke paas pahunche to unki aamad se woh bahut ghabraya aur Dil tang hua, aur kehne laga ke aaj badi musibat ka Din hai. Jaise hi woh aaye to Lut (as) ki Qaum ke log daudte hue unke paas aaye aur *isse pehle woh Badkariyan kiya karte the.*

(Surah Hud: 77 - 78)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Lut (as) shuru hota hai, Aap (as) ke zamane mein Lawaat common ho gaya tha:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ki Ummat shuru mein to behtareen Ummat thi. Shaitan ne unhe Gumrah karne ki kai bar koshish ki lekin har bar woh nakaam hua. Un logon ki aadat thi ke jab woh kisi kam kaj ke liye jate to saare mard hi chale jate the. Gharon mein sirf Aurten reh jati thin. Iblees Laeen logon ki ghair maujoodgi mein unke gharon mein jata aur unke bartan tod deta. Usne kayi gharon ke bartan tode. Akhirkar log tang aa gaye aur kehne lage ke aaj ghaat laga kar baitho aur Bartan Todne wale ka pata chalao."

"Log apne apne gharon mein chhip kar baith gaye. Iblees Laeen ek khoobsurat ladke ki shakl mein ek shakhs ke ghar mein dakhil hua aur woh uske ghar ke bartan todne laga. Us shakhs ne use pakad liya aur use logon ke saamne le aaya aur kehne laga: 'Ye ladka rozana hamare bartan tod jata hai.

Logon ne kaha ke ab Raat hone ko hai. Us ladke ko aaj tum apne paas thehrao, kal din hoga to ham use qatl kar denge. Algharz woh ladke ko apne ghar le aaya. Aadhi Raat ke waqt ladke ne rona shuru kar diya. Us shakhs ne kaha: 'Tu kyon ro raha hai?' Ladke ne kaha: 'Mera Baap rozana Raat ke waqt mujhe apne Seene par sulaata tha aur Seene ke baghair mujhe Neend nahi aati.

Us shakhs ko ladke par rahem aaya aur kaha uth aur mere Seene par so ja. Ladka jaise hi uske Seene par aaya to usne uski Jinsi khwahish (Sexual Lust) ko tehreek di aur us shakhs se khilafe Fitrat amal karaya. Us shakhs ne jab ghair Fitri amal kiya to use badi lazzat mehsoos hui. Subah hui to ladka wahan se ja chuka tha. Log jama hue aur kaha ke us mujrim ladke ko le aao taake ham use qatl karen.

Us shakhs ne kaha ke ladke ka to mujhe Ilm nahi hai. Woh Raat ke kisi hisse mein yahan se khisak gaya, albatta usne mujhe ek nayi Jinsi Lazzat (Sex) se rushanas karaya hai. Phir usne unhe "Aghlaam bazi - *اغلام* (Homosexuality, Sodomy)" ki tarkeeb batayi. Logon ne iske baad Aghlaam bazi ikhtiyar kar li aur is mein itni munhamik (attract) hue ke unhone ne Aurton se Jinsi talluq munqata kar liye aur ladko par hi iktefa karne lage.

Phir jab Iblis ne dekha ke woh unke Mardon ko gumrah kar chuka hai to woh Aurat ke roop mein Auton ke paas aaya aur unse kaha ke meine suna hai ke tumhare Mard mardon par hi qana'at kar chuke hain aur woh tumhari taraf zarrah barabar bhi mutawajjah nahi hote. Aurton ne kaha: 'Bilkul sahih hai.' Usne kaha: 'Phir tumhe Mardon ki taraf mutawajjah hone ki kiya zaroorat hai? Phir us ne Aurton ko' Ham Jins Parasti' (Homosexuality) ki taleem di. Jiska natija ye hua ke Mard Mardon se Sexual Lust taskeen hasil karne lage aur Aurten Aurton se Jinsi Lazzat hasil karne lagi aur 'Ham Jins Parasti' (Homosexuality) ko forogh hasil hua."

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne logon ko is Bad-Fe'li se mana kiya lekin Hazrat (as) ki Nasihat ka un par koi asar na hua.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Khuda ke kuchh Bande aise bhi hain jinke Aslaab mein Aurton jaise Arhaam (Womb) maujood hain."

Raavi ne poochha ke agar yehi baat hai to unhe Hamal (pregnant) kyon nahi hota?

Imam Ali (as):

"Woh ulte hote hain, unke Dubur (Anus) mein Oont ki tarah ghada (غده) hota hai, jab woh hijaan (excited) mein aata hai to ye log bhi excited ho jate hain aur jab wo pur sukoon ho jata hai to ye bhi pur sukoon ho jate hain."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اسْتُرْ عَوْرَتِي وَ اٰمِنْ رَوْعَتِي وَ اَقِلْنِيْ عَثْرَتِيْ وَ اصْفَحْ عَنْ جُرْمِيْ وَ تَجَاوَزْ عَنْ سَيِّئَاتِيْ فِي اَصْحَابِ الْجَنَّةِ وَعْدَ الصِّدْقِ الَّذِيْ كَانُوْا يُوْعَدُوْنَ۔

(Dua Rasoole Khuda (saww) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

SHIA CHANNEL CELEBRATES WILADAT OF JANABE UMME KULSUM BINTE ALI (as)

**********************************

       18th Rabiul Awwal 1442

   5th November 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1557)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَجَاۤءَهُۥ قَوۡمُهُۥ یُهۡرَعُونَ إِلَیۡهِ وَمِن قَبۡلُ كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ بَنَاتِی هُنَّ أَطۡهَرُ لَكُمۡۖ فَٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَلَا تُخۡزُونِ فِی ضَیۡفِیۤۖ أَلَیۡسَ مِنكُمۡ رَجُلࣱ رَّشِیدࣱ. * قَالُوا۟ لَقَدۡ عَلِمۡتَ مَا لَنَا فِی بَنَاتِكَ مِنۡ حَقࣲّ وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعۡلَمُ مَا نُرِیدُ * قَالَ لَوۡ أَنَّ لِی بِكُمۡ قُوَّةً أَوۡ ءَاوِیۤ إِلَىٰ رُكۡنࣲ شَدِیدࣲ.

"Jaise hi Woh (Farishte) aaye to Lut (as) ki Qaum ke log daudte hue unke paas aaye aur isse pehle woh Badkariyan kiya karte the. Lut (as) ne kaha: "Aye meri Qaum! Ye meri Betiyan (Tumhari Biwiyan) maujood hain. Ye tumhare liye zyada Pakeeza hain. Tum Allah se Daro aur Mehmano ke mutalliq ruswa na karo. Kya tumhara andar koi basha'oor shakhs maujood nahi hai?"

"Woh kehne lage ke tu jaanta hai ke tumhari Betiyon se hamara koi talluq nahi hai aur ham jo kuchh chahte hain usse mutalliq tumhe bakhoobi ilm hai. Lut (as) ne kaha: Aye Kaash! Meri paas tumhare muqabile ke liye Quwwat maujood hoti ya mein kisi mazboot Sahare ki panah le sakta."

(Surah Hud: 77 - 80)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne logon ko is Bad-Fe'li se mana kiya lekin Hazrat (as) ki Nasihat ka un par koi asar na hua. Jab unki Behayai had se badhi to Allah ne un par Azaab bhejne ka faisla kiya. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Jibrael (as), Mikael aur Israfeel ko khoobsurat ladko ki shakl mein wahan rawana kiya. Teeno Farishte Hazrat Lut (as) ke paas aaye. Us waqt Aap (as) kheton mein kam kaj kar rahe the. Aap (as) ne unse kaha: 'Tum log kahan ja rahe ho, meine apni zindagi mein tum se zyada haseen afraad nahi dekhe?' Unhone kaha ke hamare Aaqa ne hame is shaher ke Sardar ke paas bheja hai.

Hazrat Lut (as) ne kaha: "Kya tumhare Aaqa ko ye Ilm nahi hai ke is Shaher ke log naujawan ladkon se kya sulook karte hain? Suno! Ye bade kamine log hain. Ye Mardon ko pakad kar Jinsi (Sex) taskeen hasil karte hain, yahan tak ke dubur (Anus) se Khoon nikal aata hai."

Farishton ne kaha: "Hamare Aaqa ne hamko Hidayat di hai ke ham Shaher ke Markaz (Centre) mein jayen."

Hazrat ne Farmaya:

"Phir tum meri baat maano, tum abhi yahan mere paas thehre raho, yahan tak ke tareeki chha jaye." Aap (as) ki ye baat sun kar woh Aap (as) ke paas baith gaye. Itne mein Aap (as) ki beti Aap (as) ke paas aayi. Aap (as) ne beti se farmaya: "Mehmanon ke liye khaana aur Paani lao aur sardi se mehfooz rehne ke liye kuchh chaadaren bhi yahan le aao. Hazrat (as) ki beti ghar gayi ke tez Baarish aa gayi aur waadiyan behne lagin. Hazrat Lut (as) ne ladko ko saath liya aur farmaya: "Ab meri bachchi khaana nahi la sakegi, lehaza tum mere saath mere ghar tak chalo, wahan mein tumhari Ziyafat karunga."

Hazrat Lut (as) Diwaar ke saaye mein chalne lage, jabke teeno Mehmaan raaste beech mein chalne lage. Hazrat (as) ne farmaya: "Bachcho! Darmiyan mein na chalo. Diwaar ke saath saath tareeki hai tum mere saath tareeki mein chalo. Mehmamo ne kaha: "Hamen hamare Aaqa ne Nasihat ki thi ke ham raaste ke beech mein chalen."

Hazrat Lut (as) ne Tareeki e Shab ko ghanimat jana. Aap (as) unhe saath le kar apne ghar le aaye. Aap (as) ke Darwaze ke paas ek Kuwan tha jahan se log Paani bhara karte the. Ittifaq se us waqt ek Aurat apne bachche ko uthaye hue Paani bharne ke liye wahan aayi. Iblees ne uske Bachche ko Kuwen mein dhakka diya. Aurat cheekhne lagi. Log uski madad ke liye wahan aaye. Jab woh wahan aaye to unhone Hazrat Lut (as) ke ghar 3 khubsurat ladkon ko baithe hue dekha. Jab unhone khubsurat ladke dekhe to unki ral tapakne lagi aur unhone Aap (as) se kaha: "Aap (as) hame to mana karte the, lekin Aap (as) khud hamare kaamo mein shamil hain."

Aap (as) ne farmaya: "Ye log mere Mehman hain aur Mehmano ke mutalliq mujhe ruswa na karo."

Un logon ne kaha: "Achha ham Aap (as) se musalehat kar lete hain. Aap (as) ke 3 ladke thehre hue hain, un mein se ek ladke ko apne paas rakho aur do ladke hamare sipurd kardo."

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne ان لى بكم قوة او آوى الى ركن شديد keh kar do cheezon ki khwahish ki thi: Unhone Badkaar Qaum ke muqabile mein Quwwat aur Mazboot Sahare ki khwahish ki thi. Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) jab Zahoor karenge to unhe dono cheezen hasil hongi. Khuda unhe bemisaal Quwwat ata karega aur Sahare ke liye aise saathi ata karega jinke Dil Faulad se bhi zyada Mazboot honge. Woh Lohe ke Pahad ko bhi kaatne ki quwwat rakhte honge aur us waqt tak Shasheerzani karte rahenge jab tak Khuda Raazi na ho jayega."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

یَا رُكْنَ مَنْ لَا رُكْنَ لَهٗ یَا غِیَاثَا مَنْ لَاغِیَاثَ لَهٗ........

(Dua-e-Joshane Kabir)

          ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1558)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰلُوطُ إِنَّا رُسُلُ رَبِّكَ لَن یَصِلُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡكَۖ فَأَسۡرِ بِأَهۡلِكَ بِقِطۡعࣲ مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِ وَلَا یَلۡتَفِتۡ مِنكُمۡ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا ٱمۡرَأَتَكَۖ إِنَّهُۥ مُصِیبُهَا مَاۤ أَصَابَهُمۡۚ إِنَّ مَوۡعِدَهُمُ ٱلصُّبۡحُۚ أَلَیۡسَ ٱلصُّبۡحُ بِقَرِیبࣲ.

"Unhone (Farishton) kaha: Aye Lut! Ham tere Rab ke Numainde hain. Ye log tumhara kuchh na bigad sakenge. Raat ke andar hi apne Khandan ko le kar nikal jao aur tum mein se koi peechhe palat kar na dekhe, siwai teri Biwi ke. Us par bhi wohi Azaab aanewala hai jo un par aanewala hai. Unke Azaab ke liye Subah ka waqt muqarrar ho chuka hai. Kya Subah qareeb nahi hai?"

(Surah Hud: 81)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Hasan (as):

"Algharz Farishte Hazrat Lut (as) ke paas aaye. Us waqt Aap (as) Basti ke qareeb Kheti mein masroof the. Malaika ne Aap (as) ko Salam kiya. Us waqt woh Amaama bandhe hue the. Aap (as) ne unko apne ghar qayam karne ke liye kaha. Aap (as) ne Farishton se farmaya ke tum log Khuda ki Bad-tareen paas ja rahe ho. Aisa unhone ne 3 bar kaha, yani 3 bar gawahi di.

Jo woh ghar par aaye to Hazrat Lut (as) ki Biwi ne jab in haseen o jameel ladko ko dekha to woh Chhat par gayi aur seeti bajayi. Lekin kisi ne na suna. Jab ye harba kamyab nahi hua to Aag jala kar dhuwan kiya. Log Dhuwen ko dekh kar Aap (as) ke Makan ki taraf daude. Jab log pahunchne to Biwi ne kaha aaj hamare ghar haseen o jameel ladke aaye hue hain aise haseen aaj tak nahi dekhe.

Ye sun kar logon ne mutaliba kiya ke un jawano ko hamare hawale kar do.

Hazrat Lut (as) ne farmaya:

"Aye meri Qaum! Khuda se Daro! Mehmano ke mutalliq mujhe ruswa na karo. Kya tum mein koi ba sha'oor fard maujood nahi hai? Agar tumhe Jinsi Taskeen (Sex) hi bujhani hai to apni Biwiyon se Taskeen hasil karo. Tumhari Biwiyan meri ek tarah se Betiyan hain aur woh tumhare liye Pakeeza tar hain."

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

keh kar do cheezon ki khwahish ki thi: Unhone Badkaar Qaum ke muqabile mein Quwwat aur Mazboot Sahare ki khwahish ki thi. بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰلُوطُ إِنَّا رُسُلُ رَبِّكَ لَن یَصِلُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡكَۖ فَأَسۡرِ بِأَهۡلِكَ بِقِطۡعࣲ مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِ وَلَا یَلۡتَفِتۡ مِنكُمۡ أَحَدٌ إِلَّا ٱمۡرَأَتَكَۖ إِنَّهُۥ مُصِیبُهَا مَاۤ أَصَابَهُمۡۚ إِنَّ مَوۡعِدَهُمُ ٱلصُّبۡحُۚ أَلَیۡسَ ٱلصُّبۡحُ بِقَرِیبࣲ.

"Unhone (Farishton) kaha: Aye Lut! Ham tere Rab ke Numainde hain. Ye log tumhara kuchh na bigad sakenge. Raat ke andar hi apne Khandan ko le kar nikal jao aur tum mein se koi peechhe palat kar na dekhe, siwai teri Biwi ke. Us par bhi wohi Azaab aanewala hai jo un par aanewala hai. Unke Azaab ke liye Subah ka waqt muqarrar ho chuka hai. Kya Subah qareeb nahi hai?"

(Surah Hud: 81)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ki Qaum Shaam aur Misr (Syria & Egypt) ki Tijarti Shahrao (Business Street) par rihaish pazeer the."

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne 30 Saal tak unhe Deen ki Dawat di thi. Aap un logon ko Allah ki Raah ki taraf dete rahe aur unhe Azaab e Ilahi se Khabardar karte rahe. Woh log intihai gande the. Paishab Paikhane ke baad safai nahi karte the aur woh Ghusle Janabat bhi nahi karte the.

Hazrat Lut (as) Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Khalazad bhai the aur Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki Zauja Hazrat Sarah (sa) unki Bahen thi. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aur Hazrat Lut (as) dono Allah ke Paighambar the. Lut (as) Sakhi aur Fayyaz Insaan the. Aap (as) Mehmano ki Tawazah karte the aur apni Ummat ko bhi Mehman Nawazi ki targheeb dete the.

Hazrat Lut (as) ki Qaum ne unse kaha: "Agar Mehman Nawazi se baaz na aaye to ham Aap (as) ke Mehmano ko ruswa karenge, jiski wajah se Aap (as) ko bhi ruswai uthani padegi.

Us dhamki ke baad Aap (as) chori chhupe Mehman Nawazi karte the ke kahin Aap (as) ki Qaum Aap (as) ke Mehmano ko ruswa na kare. Jis ilaqe mein Hazrat Lut (as) Tableegh e Deen karte the wahan Aap (as) ka Qabila nahi tha. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) aur Hazrat Lut (as) dono ko hi in Badbakhton ke mutalliq Azaab ka andesha tha. Dono Bagahe Ahdiyyat mein Azeem Maqam rakhte the. Allah Ta'ala Ibrahim (as) aur Lut (as) ki bahami Muhabbat ki wajah se unse Azaab ko muakhkhar (delay) karta raha....."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Khuda ko jis shakhs ki zaroorat hoti hai Woh use Aadat e Bad mein kabhi bhi mubtila nahi hone deta. Aise logon ke dubur (Anus) mein ulte Rahem hote hain aur unko bhi Aurto ki tarah se Shehwat mehsoos hoti hai. Un mein Iblis ka Beta jiska naam "Zawal" hai sharik hota hai. Woh jis Mard mein sharik ho jaye to woh Mard Maf'ool ban jata hai aur jis Aurat mein sharik ho jaye woh Badkaar ban jati hai. Aur jo shakhs 40 Saal ki umr mein Aghlambazi (Homosexuality) kare to woh usse kabhi juda nahi hota. Aise afraad "Sodom - سدوم" ki baqiyaat hain. Mein ye nahi kehta ke woh Nasli etbar se Ahle Sodom se talluq rakhte hain albatta unki Teenat Ahle Sodom ki si hai."

"Allah ne 4 Bastiyon ko ulta tha jinke naam: Sodom, Sareem - صريم, Ladma - لدما " aur Ameera - عميرا " the. Jibrael Amin (as) ne un Bastiyon ko Saatvin Zameen se kaat kar unhe apne Paron par itna buland kiya tha ke Aasmaan walon ne unke Kutton ki bhonkne ki awazen suni thi."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Bare Ilaha hame aise Badkaaron se mehfooz rakh.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    8th November 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ QAUM-E-LUT (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1560)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُنَا جَعَلۡنَا عَـٰلِیَهَا سَافِلَهَا وَأَمۡطَرۡنَا عَلَیۡهَا حِجَارَةࣰ مِّن سِجِّیلࣲ مَّنضُودࣲ *  مُّسَوَّمَةً عِندَ رَبِّكَۖ وَمَا هِیَ مِنَ ٱلظَّـٰلِمِینَ بِبَعِیدࣲ.

"Jab hamare Faisle ka waqt aaya to Hamne uske upar ke hisse ko neeche ulat diya aur us par Paki hui Mitti ke Patthar tabad tod barsai. Un mein se har Patthar tere Rab ki taraf se Nishanzadah tha aur ye Azaab Zalimon se door nahi hai."

(Surah Hud: 82 - 83)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Qaum e Lut (as) ka akheri hissa pesh hai:

🕌

Imam Baqir (as): (Cont'd)

"..... Chunanche jab aadhi Raat ka waqt hua to Hazrat Lut (as) apni Betiyon ko le kar wahan se rawana hue. Uski Biwi ne saath jaane se inkar kar diya aur woh apni Qaum ki taraf daud padi aur woh unko ye batane gayi ke Lut (as) apni Betiyon ko lekar yahan se ja rahe hain.

Subah ke waqt Arsh se mujhe ye sada sunayi di ke Aye Jibrael! Allah ki taraf se Qaum e Lut (as) par Azaab ka Faisla ho chuka hai. Lehaza tum Qaum e Lut (as) ki Basti mein jao. Us Basti ko Saatvin Zameen se kaat kar Aasmaan ki taraf le aao. Aur wahan pahunch kar thehre raho, yahan tak ke iske ulatne ke ke mutalliq tujhe Khuda ka Hukm mausool ho. Haan, us jagah par ye Ibrat ke liye Lut (as) ke Ghar ko baqi rakho. Phir waisa hi kiya. Phir Allah ne un par Pattharon ki Baarish ki aur Aap (as) ki Ummat mein se jo ye Bad-Fe'li (Un-Natural Sex) karega usse bhi ye Azaab door nahi hoga. Unka Shaher Baheera e Tabriya hai jo Syria ke Suburb mein hai. Unko Behre Shaam aur Misr ke darmiyan ulat diya tha aur jahan wo Zameen giri to usne Samandar mein Teelon ki shakl ikhtiyar kar li."

(Noorus Saqlain)

(The End ......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as)

"Jo bhi shakhs Qaum e Lut (as) ke amal (Homosexuality) ko Halal samajhta hai to Maut ke waqt us par Khuda ek Patthar bhejta hai jisse uski Maut waqe hoti hai, lekin Duniya walon ko woh Patthar dikhayi nahi deta."

👉🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jab Qaum e Lut (as) ne Bad-kaari (Homosexuality) ko rawaj diya to Zameen itna royi ke uske Aansu Arsh e Ilahi tak pahuche. Allah Ta'ala ne Aasmaan ko Hukm diya ke un par Patthar barsa aur Zameen ko Hukm diya ke un ko nigal le."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Jo shakhs apne aap se chhedkhani ki be raza o raghbat (inclined) ijazat de to Khuda us par Aurton ki si Shehwat (Lust) dal deta hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

"Khudaya! Kitne hi Bande hain ke jinki Subah o Shaam Samandaron ki Tareekiyon, Hawaon ki tez jhadokon aur haulnak Maujon ke darmiyan guzar rahi hai ke har aan ye ummeed rehti hai ke kab gharq aur halaak ho jayenge aur bachne ki koi tadbeer nahi hai ya phir Bijli ke girne, Makan ke girne, Aag lagne, Luqme ke gulugir ho jane, Zameen dhans jane, Surat ke bigad jaane aur Sangsaar (Stoning) ho jaane ke khatarat mein mubtila hain aur mein in sab ki taraf se aafiyat mein hun..... Al Hamdo lillah... Allahumma Swalle ala Muhammadin wa Aale Muhammad...."

(Dua-e-Joshan e Sagheer - Mafateeh)

       22nd Rabiul Awwal 1442

   9th November 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ MAUQA O MASLAHET ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1561)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَجَاۤءَهُۥ قَوۡمُهُۥ یُهۡرَعُونَ إِلَیۡهِ وَمِن قَبۡلُ كَانُوا۟ یَعۡمَلُونَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِ بَنَاتِی هُنَّ أَطۡهَرُ لَكُمۡۖ فَٱتَّقُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ وَلَا تُخۡزُونِ فِی ضَیۡفِیۤۖ أَلَیۡسَ مِنكُمۡ رَجُلࣱ رَّشِیدࣱ. * قَالُوا۟ لَقَدۡ عَلِمۡتَ مَا لَنَا فِی بَنَاتِكَ مِنۡ حَقࣲّ وَإِنَّكَ لَتَعۡلَمُ مَا نُرِیدُ * قَالَ لَوۡ أَنَّ لِی بِكُمۡ قُوَّةً أَوۡ ءَاوِیۤ إِلَىٰ رُكۡنࣲ شَدِیدࣲ.

"Jaise hi Woh (Farishte) aaye to Lut (as) ki Qaum ke log daudte hue unke paas aaye aur isse pehle woh Badkariyan kiya karte the. Lut (as) ne kaha: "Aye meri Qaum! Ye meri Betiyan (Tumhari Biwiyan) maujood hain. Ye tumhare liye zyada Pakeeza hain. Tum Allah se Daro aur Mehmano ke mutalliq ruswa na karo. Kya tumhara andar koi basha'oor shakhs maujood nahi hai?"

"Woh kehne lage ke tu jaanta hai ke tumhari Betiyon se hamara koi talluq nahi hai aur ham jo kuchh chahte hain usse mutalliq tumhe bakhoobi ilm hai. Lut (as) ne kaha: Aye Kaash! Meri paas tumhare muqabile ke liye Quwwat maujood hoti ya mein kisi mazboot Sahare ki panah le sakta."

(Surah Hud: 77 - 80)

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat ka Tazkara kar chuke hain, ab ise doosre pehlu se iska mafhoom samjhen.

🕌

Jo situation Hazrat Lut (as) ke Ghar par thi, waisi hi Hazrat Ali (as) wa Janabe Zehra (sa) ke Ghar par hui thi. Baad e Shahadat e Rasool (saww) Wehshi Darinde Aap (as) ke Ghar par toot pade, Janabe Zehra (sa) par jalta hua Dirwaza giraya gaya, pehlu shakista hua, Janabe Mohsin (as) ki Paidaish se pehle hi Shahadat hui. Aap (as) ke gale mein Rassi bandhi aur khechte hue Ghar se nikala.

Woh Bahadur Wasi e Rasool (saww) Jinhone itne Ma'arke Fatah kiye, Bahadur Dushmano ko pachhada. Jinke saamne Kuffar ki aane ki himmat nahi hoti thi unhone ye sab kaise bardasht kiya. 25 Saal Khamosh Zindagi kyon guzari. Iska jawab khud Imam (as) ne diya. Ek wajah to ye thi ke Rasool (saww) ki Ali (as) ko Wasiyyat thi ke mere baad agar saathi na hon to apne Dushmano se muqabila na karna.

👉🏻

Jange Jamal ke baad Hazrat Ali (as) kuchh saathiyon ne kaha ke agar Aap (as) ke Siyasi Hareefon (Opponents) ki Hukumat sahi na hoti to Aap (as) unse bhi Jang karte jis tarah Jange Jamal mein Jang ki.

Hazrat Ali (as) ne Masjid mein Khutba diya aur farmaya:

"Suno! Meine Jang na karke 6 Anbiya ki pairavi ki hai. Meine Jang na karke Hazrat Lut (as) ki pairavi ki hai, (Ye Ayat padhi 11:80) Jab Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Hazrat Lut (as) ne Mukhalefin se Jang nahi ki thi to meine agar Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Jang nahi ki to is mein kya etraz hai? Agar tum kaho ke Lut (as) ke paas Quwwat thi to Kafir ban jaoge. Agar kaho ke unhone Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Jang nahi ki thi to phir yaad rakho, Wasi ne bhi Quwwat na hone ki wajah se Jang nahi ki thi."

(Ilalus Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

----------------------------------------------

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Hazrat Lut (as) ne ان لى بكم قوة او آوى الى ركن شديد

keh kar do cheezon ki khwahish ki thi: Unhone Badkaar Qaum ke muqabile mein Quwwat aur Mazboot Sahare ki khwahish ki thi. Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) jab Zahoor karenge to unhe dono cheezen hasil hongi. Khuda unhe bemisaal Quwwat ata karega aur Sahare ke liye aise saathi ata karega jinke Dil Faulad se bhi zyada Mazboot honge. Woh Lohe ke Pahad ko bhi kaatne ki quwwat rakhte honge aur us waqt tak Shasheerzani karte rahenge jab tak Khuda Raazi na ho jayega."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

یَا رُكْنَ مَنْ لَا رُكْنَ لَهٗ یَا غِیَاثَا مَنْ لَاغِیَاثَ لَهٗ........

(Dua-e-Joshane Kabir)

        23rd Rabiul Awwal 1442

 10th November 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1562)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَإِلَىٰ مَدۡیَنَ أَخَاهُمۡ شُعَیۡبࣰاۚ قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ ٱعۡبُدُوا۟ ٱللَّهَ مَا لَكُم مِّنۡ إِلَـٰهٍ غَیۡرُهُۥۖ وَلَا تَنقُصُوا۟ ٱلۡمِكۡیَالَ وَٱلۡمِیزَانَۖ إِنِّیۤ أَرَىٰكُم بِخَیۡرࣲ وَإِنِّیۤ أَخَافُ عَلَیۡكُمۡ عَذَابَ یَوۡمࣲ مُّحِیطࣲ.

"Aur Madyan walon ki taraf Hamne unke Bhai Shu'aib ko rawana kiya. Usne kaha: Aye meri Qaum! Tum Allah ki Ibaadat karo, Uske alawa tumhara koi Ma'bood nahi hai. Aur Naap Tol mein kami na karo. Aaj mein tumhe achhe haal mein dekh raha hun magar mujhe tumhare mutalliq ye andesha hai ke tum par aisa Din aayega jiska Azaab sab ko gher lega."

(Surah Hud: 84)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Hazrat Lut (as) ke baad ab Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ka Tazkara shuru hota hai:

⚖️

Kuchh Moarrakhin ka bayan hai ke Ibrahim (as) ke ek Farzand ka Naam "Madyan" tha aur Madyan Shaher ki buniyad unhone rakhi thi.

Baqi Anbiya ki tarah Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne bhi apni Tableegh ki ibteda Dawat-e-Tauheed se ki thi.

Ahle Madyan mein do bade Aib the ke woh But-Parast the aur doosra Aib ye ke woh had darje ke Bad-Maamla the. Woh jab logon se sauda lete to zyada lete, jab khud koi cheez bechte to kam dete the. Woh ise apni Tijarati Hunarmandi (Business Tech) se tabeer karte the. Aur apni ravish se dene aur lene wale dono fareeqon ko Nuqsaan pahuchate the.

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne Tauheed ki Dawat di aur  farmaya ke Naap Tol mein kami na karo. Agar tumne Naap Tol ki kami ko chhod diya to is mein tumhari apni hi Salamti aur Khairiyat hai, warna Misr o Shaam ke darmiyan chalnewale Tijarati Qafile tumse len den band kar denge aur tum Rizq se mehroom ho jaoge aur jab Tijarati Sargarmiya (Business Transactions) khatm ho jayengi to cheezon ki qeemten badh jayengi. Agar tum apni ravish se baaz na aaye to Khair o Sa'adat ki ye ghadiyan tum se salb kar li jayengi. (Means Economic Crisis hoga) Khuda ne tumhe be-tahasha Daulat di hai. Tumhe kam Naap Tol karne ki kya zaroorat hai? (11:84)

(To be Cont'd ......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Jis shakhs ko ye manzoor ho ke uske aamaal poore naap se naape jaayen use laazim hai ke jis waqt kisi jalse se uthhne ka irada kare to in teeno Aayato'n ko padh liya kare "Subhana Rabbika Rabbil Izzati 'Amma Yasifoon, Wa Salaamun 'Alal Mursaleen, Wal Handu Lillahi Rabbil 'Aalameen." (37:180 - 182)

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p42)

🤲🏻

وَ اَطِيْعُوْا اللّٰهَ فِيْمَا نَهَاكُمْ عَنْهُ مِنْ قَذْفِ الْمُحْصَنَةِ وَ اِتْيَانِ الْفَاحِشَةِ وَ شُرْبِ الْخَمْرِ وَ بَخْسِ الْمِكْيَالِ وَ نَقْصِ الْمِيْزَانِ وَ شَهَادَةِ الزُّوْرِ وَ الْفِرَارِ مِنَ الزَّحْفِ عَصَمَنَا اللّٰهُ وَ اِيَّاكُمْ بِالتَّقْوٰى وَ جَعَلَ الْاٰخِرَةَ خَيْرًا لَنَا وَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الْاُوْلٰى.....

(Khutba Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) on Eidul Fitr, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih)

          24th Rabiul Awwal 1442

11th November 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1563)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ أَوۡفُوا۟ ٱلۡمِكۡیَالَ وَٱلۡمِیزَانَ بِٱلۡقِسۡطِۖ وَلَا تَبۡخَسُوا۟ ٱلنَّاسَ أَشۡیَاۤءَهُمۡ وَلَا تَعۡثَوۡا۟ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ مُفۡسِدِینَ ۝  بَقِیَّتُ ٱللَّهِ خَیۡرࣱ لَّكُمۡ إِن كُنتُم مُّؤۡمِنِینَۚ وَمَاۤ أَنَا۠ عَلَیۡكُم بِحَفِیظࣲ.

"Aye meri Qaum! Naap Tol Insaaf ke saath karo aur logon ko unki cheezon mein ghata na diya karo aur Zameen mein Fasaad na phailate phiro."

"Agar tum Momin ho to Allah ki Bachat tumhare liye behtar hai, aur mein tumhara Nigran nahi hun."

(Surah Hud: 85 - 86)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) jaari hai:

⚖️

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne apni Qaum se kaha:

"Aye meri Qaum! Insaaf ke Usoolon ke tahet Naap Tol karo aur chhote Baat rakh kar logon ko Nuqsaan na pahunchao aur Zameen mein Fasaad na phailate phiro, kyonki jo doosron ko Nuqsaan pahunchata hai to dar asl woh logon ko apne Nuqsaan pahunchane ki targheeb de raha hota hai. Kam Naap-Tol se tumhari Duniya o Akherat ka Nuqsaan hai aur isse Deeni Maslahaton ko bhi Nuqsaan pahunchta hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

👉🏻

(11:86) ka maqsad ye hai ke Sidq o Amanat ki ravish apnao, Naap-Tol mein kami chhod do aur Sachche Tajirana Usool (True Business Principles) apnao. Iske baad tumhe jo bhi Munafa, Profit hasil ho wo tumhare Haq mein behtar hai. Jo Tajir isse baaz na aaye aur Na-jaez Munafa khori ki rahon par amal kare to woh Momin nahi hai.

👉🏻

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne jo kaha ke mein Nigran nahi hun..

Is jumle ke do mafhoom mumkin hain. Ek ye ke mera kaam tumhe Nasihat karna tha woh kar diya albatta sab ko zabardasti chalana nahi. Doosre ye ke jaisa ke pehle bataya Naap-Tol mein kami ki wajah se Khuda ki Ne'maten Salb ho jati hain. To agar Ne'maten Salb ho gayi to Paighambar kuchh nahi kar sakta ke woh wapas le aaye.

(To be Cont'd ......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Sa'ad se Riwayat hai ke usne Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya, maine unse aise logon ke bare mein poochha jo apne maapne ke Auzaron (Tarazu) ko chhota kar ke, bikri kar rahe hain?

 قاَل َسأَْلُتُه عن َقْوٍم ُيَصغُِّروَن اْلقُْفَزاَن َيِبيُعوَن ِبَها َقاَل أُولَِئَك الَِّذيَن َيْبَخُسوَن النَّاَس أَْشَياَءُهْم

Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Ye woh log hain jo logon ki cheezon ka qeemat gira rahe hain."

(Furu e Kafi, Vol 5, Al Kafi, Hadis 72)

🤲🏻

وَ اَطِيْعُوْا اللّٰهَ فِيْمَا نَهَاكُمْ عَنْهُ مِنْ قَذْفِ الْمُحْصَنَةِ وَ اِتْيَانِ الْفَاحِشَةِ وَ شُرْبِ الْخَمْرِ وَ بَخْسِ الْمِكْيَالِ وَ نَقْصِ الْمِيْزَانِ وَ شَهَادَةِ الزُّوْرِ وَ الْفِرَارِ مِنَ الزَّحْفِ عَصَمَنَا اللّٰهُ وَ اِيَّاكُمْ بِالتَّقْوٰى وَ جَعَلَ الْاٰخِرَةَ خَيْرًا لَنَا وَ لَكُمْ مِنَ الْاُوْلٰى.....

(Khutba Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) on Eidul Fitr, Man La Yahzarahul Faqih)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          25th Rabiul Awwal 1442

  12th November 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ BAQIYYATULLAH (atfs) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1564)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

بَقِیَّتُ ٱللَّهِ خَیۡرࣱ لَّكُمۡ إِن كُنتُم مُّؤۡمِنِینَۚ وَمَاۤ أَنَا۠ عَلَیۡكُم بِحَفِیظࣲ.

"Agar tum Momin ho to Allah ki taraf ka Zakhira, Baqimaandah tumhare liye behtar hai, aur mein tumhara Nigran nahi hun."

(Surah Hud: 86)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Ayat ka Tazkara iske Zahiri maana mein kiya gaya tha aur kiya jata hai, jabke ek Ayat apne andar kayi maana wa Tafseer ki haamil hoti hai. Qur'an ki Tafseer wohi kar sakta hai jo Rasekhoona fil Ilm hain, aur woh siwai Ahlebait (as) ke koi nahi ho sakta, kyonki wohi Allah ke muntakhib shuda Numainde hain.

Jaisa ke ke ham bata chuke hain ke Dushmanane Khuda ne koshish ki ke Allah ke har Rehbar, Nabi, Imam, Hujjat, Noor ko khatm kar den, lekin iske baad Allah ne Apni Akheri Hujjat ko Baqi rakha. Isliye Imam Mahdi (as) ko "Baqiyyatullah" kaha jata hai.

🕋

Imam Baqir (as):

"Jab Qaem e Aale Muhammad (atfs) ka Zahoor hoga to woh Pushte Ka'aba se tek lagayenge aur unke paas 313 afraad jama honge. Woh apne khitab ka aghaaz is Ayat se karenge. (11:86) "Mein *Baqiyyatullah* hun aur mein tum par Khalifa e Khuda hun."

"Iske baad unhe jo bhi Salam karega woh unhe ye keh kar Salam karega:"

"ُاَلسَّلَام عَلَيكَ يَا بَقِيَّةَ اللّٰهِ فى اَرضِهِ

(Noorus Saqlain, The Promised One in Qur'an, Noorul Absaar - Syed Momin Shablanji Shafaee)

🎠

Imam Hasan Askari (as) apne Kandhe par ek Bachche ko uthaye hue aaye. Bachche ki Umr taqreeban 3 Saal thi aur uska Chehra Chaudhvi ke Chaand se bhi zyada roshan tha.

Aap (as) ne Raavi se farmaya:

"Aye Ahmed bin Ishaaq! Agar Khuda aur Hujjat haye Khuda ki Nazar mein tumhara khusoosi maqam na hota to mein apna ye Beta tujhe kabhi na dikhata. Ye Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka hamnaam hai. Us waqt Bachche ne Faseeh Arabi Zabaan mein ye Kalemaat kahe jinka tarjuma ye hai:

"Mein Khuda ki Zameen par *Baqiyyatullah* hun aur Dushmanane Khuda se Inteqaam lene wala hun. Ahmed bin Ishaaq! Asl cheez ko dekh, uske Nishaan ki talash na kar."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha ke Maula! Kya Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) ko "Ameerul Mo'meneen" keh sakte hain?

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Nahi, ye Laqab sirf Hazrat Ali (as) ke liye makhsoos hai. Aap (as) se pehle ye kisi ka Laqab nahi tha aur Aap (as) ke baad jo bhi ye Laqab ikhtiyar karega woh Kafir ho jayega. Qaem Aale Muhammad (atfs) ko "ُاَلسَّلَام عَلَيكَ يَا بَقِيَّةَ اللّٰهِ - As Salamo Alaika ya Baqiyyatullah" keh kar Salam kiya jayega."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا بَقِيَّةَ اللّٰهِ مِنَ الْبَرَرَةِ الْمَاضِيْنَ...

(Ziyarat Janabe Salman)

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا بَقِيَّةَ اللّٰهِ مِنَ الصَّفْوَةِ الْمُنْتَجَبِيْنَ....

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلٰى بَقِيَّةِ اللّٰهِ فِيْ بِلَادِهِ،....

(Ziyarat e Saheb e Amr (atfs) (Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU

**********************************

        26th Rabiul Awwal 1442

    13th November 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1565)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰشُعَیۡبُ أَصَلَوٰتُكَ تَأۡمُرُكَ أَن نَّتۡرُكَ مَا یَعۡبُدُ ءَابَاۤؤُنَاۤ أَوۡ أَن نَّفۡعَلَ فِیۤ أَمۡوَ ٰ⁠لِنَا مَا نَشَـٰۤؤُا۟ۖ إِنَّكَ لَأَنتَ ٱلۡحَلِیمُ ٱلرَّشِیدُ.

"Unhone kaha: Aye Shu'aib (as)! Kya teri Namaz tujhe yehi taleem deti hai ke ham in Ma'boodon ki Ibaadat den jinki Parastish hamare Baap Dada kiya karte the? Ya ye keh hamko apne Maal mein hasbe mansha tasarruf ka haq hi na rahe? To kya sirf tu hi ek Halim aur Raast baaz (Nek) Aadmi reh gaya hai?"

(Surah Hud: 87)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne apni Qaum ko do baaton ki khusoosi Dawat di thi. Pehle Aeeda e Tauheed aur doosre Naap-Tol mein kami ko chhodne ki. Iske jawab mein unhone aisa kaha..... to Aapki Namaz ham par lazim karti hai ke ham apne Maal o Daulat ke husool mein apni Azaadi e Kasb o Amal ko chhod den aur ham apne Amwaal mein apni hasbe mansha tasarruf (use) bhi na karen?...

Lafz *ٱلۡحَلِیمُ ٱلرَّشِیدُ* ke mutalliq kaha jata hai woh log dar haqeeqat Aapko Bewaqoof o Jahil kehna chahte the, lekin unhone mazaq mein aisa kaha. Jaise koi Kanjoos se kahe: 'Agar Hatim aapko dekh le to woh aapke saamne sarnagu ho jaye.'

Doosre ye ke Hazrat Shu'aib (as) Ailaan e Nabuwwat se pehle apni Qaum mein Halim o Rasheed ke Laqab se jaane jate the. Jaise Rasoole Khuda (saww) zamana Jahiliyyat mein Sadiq wa Ameen se mashhoor the. Aapki Qaum Aapko Aali Zarf aur Raast baaz ke Naamon se pukarta tha. Phir jab Aap (as) ne logon ko Aqeeda e Tauheed ki Dawat di aur unhe Naap-Tol mein kami se roka to unhone bataur hasrat kaha ke ham to Aapko Halim & Rasheed ke Laqab se pukarte the lekin tum hamari tawaqquat par poore nahi utre, kya koi Aali Zarf aur Nek Aadmi is tarah ko baaten karta hai jaisi Aap (as) kar rahe hain.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Har Namaz ke waqt ek Farishta logo'n ko awaaz deta hai ke "Uthho aur wo Aag jo tumhare liye raushan ki gayi hai use apni Namazo'n se bujhaao."

(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p461)

🤲🏻

.....وَاَنْتَ السَّيِّدُ وَاَنَا الْعَبْدُ، وَاَنْتَ الْغَافِرُ وَاَنَا الْمُسِيْئُ وَاَنْتَ الْعَالِمُ وَاَنَا الْجَاهِلُ، وَاَنْتَ الْحَلِيْمُ وَاَنَا الْعَجُوْلُ، وَاَنْتَ الرَّحْمٰنُ وَاَنَا الْمَرْحُوْمُ، وَاَنْتَ الْمُعَافِىْ وَاَنَا الْمُبْتَلٰى، وَاَنْتَ الْمُجِيْبُ وَاَنَا الْمُضْطَرُّ،.....

(Dua-e-Yastaseer - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1566)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ أَرَءَیۡتُمۡ إِن كُنتُ عَلَىٰ بَیِّنَةࣲ مِّن رَّبِّی وَرَزَقَنِی مِنۡهُ رِزۡقًا حَسَنࣰاۚ وَمَاۤ أُرِیدُ أَنۡ أُخَالِفَكُمۡ إِلَىٰ مَاۤ أَنۡهَىٰكُمۡ عَنۡهُۚ إِنۡ أُرِیدُ إِلَّا ٱلۡإِصۡلَـٰحَ مَا ٱسۡتَطَعۡتُۚ وَمَا تَوۡفِیقِیۤ إِلَّا بِٱللَّهِۚ عَلَیۡهِ تَوَكَّلۡتُ وَإِلَیۡهِ أُنِیبُ.

"Shu'aib (as) ne kaha: Aye meri Qaum! Tum hi socho agar mein apne Rab se ek khuli hui Roshan Daleel liye hun. Phir Usne mujhe Apni taraf se achha Rizq bhi ata kiya (to kya iske bawajood mein tumhari himayat kar sakta hun). Aur mein ye nahi chahta ke mein jin baaton se tumko rokta hun unka khud irtekab karun jahan tak mera bas chale. Mein to Islah (Reform) chahta hun. Meri Taufeeq ka Sarchashma (Source) Khuda ki hi Zaat hai. Us par meine Bharosa kiya hai aur Uski taraf mujhe rujoo' (Refer) karna hai."

(Surah Hud: 88)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ki guftugu ka matlab ye hai ke mujhe Wahy e Ilahi mein Khayanat karne ki kisi wajah se koi zaroorat nahi.

1. Khuda ne mujhe Apni taraf se Ilm-e-Deen aur Hidayat o Nabuwwat ata ki.

2. Mujhe wasee Rizq-e-Halal ata kiya.

3. Mein jo kehta hun khud bhi karta hun.

4. Asl maqsad Qaum ki Islah hai. Usise Taufeeq ka talabgar hun aur Usi par Bharosa karta hun, aur mujhe Usi ki taraf palatna hai.

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ki is tarah guftar o Khutbon se Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya tha ke 'Shu'aib (as) Khateebul Anbiya' hain.

(To be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🍴💪

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah ne Bani Adam (Aadmi) ko jumla makhluqaat par fazilat di hai aur unhe khushki aur tari mein uthaya aur har qism ke pakiza phalo'n se use Rizq diya. Har haiwaan aur parinda ye taaqat nahi rakhta ke apna khana aur paani apne haatho'n se utha-kar apne Mu'nh mein daale. Ye fazilat sirf Bani Adam (Aadmi) hi ko hai ke wo apna khana apne haatho'n se apne Mu'nh mein daalta hai aur ye bahut badi fazilat hai."

(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p92)

🍵🍪

Imam Ali (as):

"Jo Allah ke thode se Rizq pe raazi hoga, Allah bhi uske thode se Amal pe raazi hoga."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p597)

🕌🏬

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jab tumne dukaan kholi aur Maal phaila-kar baithe ho to jo tumhare zimme tha wo kar chuke, ab baaqi Khuda ke zimme hai, Uspar Tawakkul karo."

(Tehzeeb ul Islam, p394)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Agar tum Allah par Tawakkul (bharosa) karte to tumhe aise Rozi deta jaise parindo ko deta hai, Subah khaali peyt hote hain aur shaam ko peyt bharaa hota hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4)

🤲🏻

.....اِنِّيْ اَعُوْذُ بِكَ فَاَعِذْنِيْ وَ اَسْتَجِيْرُ بِكَ فَاَجِرْنِيْ وَ اَسْتَرْزِقُكَ فَارْزُقْنِيْ وَ اَتَوَكَّلُ عَلَيْكَ فَاكْفِنِيْ وَ اَسْتَنْصِرُكَ عَلٰى عَدُوِّيْ [عَدُوِّكَ‏] فَانْصُرْنِيْ وَ اَسْتَعِيْنُ بِكَ فَاَعِنِّيْ وَ اَسْتَغْفِرُكَ يَاۤ اِلٰهِيْ فَاغْفِرْ لِيْ اٰمِيْنَ اٰمِيْنَ اٰمِيْنَ،.....

(Dua-e-Shabe Juma - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1567)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ لَا یَجۡرِمَنَّكُمۡ شِقَاقِیۤ أَن یُصِیبَكُم مِّثۡلُ مَاۤ أَصَابَ قَوۡمَ نُوحٍ أَوۡ قَوۡمَ هُودٍ أَوۡ قَوۡمَ صَـٰلِحࣲۚ وَمَا قَوۡمُ لُوطࣲ مِّنكُم بِبَعِیدࣲ *  وَٱسۡتَغۡفِرُوا۟ رَبَّكُمۡ ثُمَّ تُوبُوۤا۟ إِلَیۡهِۚ إِنَّ رَبِّی رَحِیمࣱ وَدُودࣱ.

"(Hazrat Shu'aib (as)): "Aye meri Qaum! Meri Nafarmani kahin ye naubat na pahucha de ke akhirkar tum par bhi wohi Azaab nazil ho jo Qaum-e-Nooh (as) aur Qaum-e-Hud (as) ya Qaum-e-Saleh (as) par aaya tha. Aur Qaum-e-Lut (as) tumse kuchh zyada door nahi hai. Tum apne Rab se Maghferat talab karo, phir Uski taraf rujoo' karo. Yaqeenan mera Rab Meherban aur (Bandon se) Muhabbat rakhnewala hai."

(Surah Hud: 89 - 90)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne apni Qaum ko Azaab e Ilahi se khabardar karte hue farmaya: "Khayal rakho kahin meri mukhalifat o Adawat ki wajah se tum par wo Azaab na aa jaye jo Qaum-e-Nooh (as), Qaum-e-Hud (as), Qaum-e-Saleh (as) aur Qaum-e-Lut (as) par nazil hua hai.

(In Qaumon ke Azaab ka tazkara abhi guzishta Ayaat ke zel mein ho chuka hai.)

Qaum-e-Lut (as) ka ilaqa ya to qareeb tha ya is Qaum ki halakat ko zyada arsa nahi guzra tha. Anjaam sab ko pata tha.

Ab bachne ka sirf ek hi raasta tha ke ye Qaum Isteghfar kare, Allah se Ma'afi ki guhar lagaye. Beshak Allah Ma'af karnewala hai kyonki Woh apne Bando se Muhabbat karta hai. Usi tarah jaise ek Baap aur Beta. Beta koi bhi ghalti karta to use saza bhi deta hai aur Beta Maafi mangta hai to use Ma'af kar deta hai.

(To be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Khuda Rahem farmayega us Bande par jo doosro'n ke saath jama ho kar hamare Amr ke baare mein guftagu kare. Jab 2 aise afraad jama ho kar baith'te hain to us Mehfil mein teesri hasti ek Farishta hoti hai jo unke liye Isteghfar karta hai aur jab 2 shakhs ikattha ho kar baith'te hain aur hamara zikr karte hain to Khuda Wande Aalam un 2 shakhso'n ke baare mein Fakhr o Mubahaat farmata hai."

(Azadari Kyun?, p35)

🕌

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Jo Ali (as) se Mohabbat rakhe, uske liye Farishte Dua e Maghferat karte hain aur Jannat ke aatho'n (all 8) Darwaze uske liye khol diye jate hain ke jis Darwaze se chaahe be-hisaab daakhil ho jaye."

(Shiane Ahlebait (as), p17)

🤲🏻

.....اِنِّيْ اَعُوْذُ بِكَ فَاَعِذْنِيْ وَ اَسْتَجِيْرُ بِكَ فَاَجِرْنِيْ وَ اَسْتَرْزِقُكَ فَارْزُقْنِيْ وَ اَتَوَكَّلُ عَلَيْكَ فَاكْفِنِيْ وَ اَسْتَنْصِرُكَ عَلٰى عَدُوِّيْ [عَدُوِّكَ‏] فَانْصُرْنِيْ وَ اَسْتَعِيْنُ بِكَ فَاَعِنِّيْ وَ اَسْتَغْفِرُكَ يَاۤ اِلٰهِيْ فَاغْفِرْ لِيْ اٰمِيْنَ اٰمِيْنَ اٰمِيْنَ،.....

(Dua-e-Shabe Juma - Mafateeh)

   16th November 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1568)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

قَالُوا۟ یَـٰشُعَیۡبُ مَا نَفۡقَهُ كَثِیرࣰا مِّمَّا تَقُولُ وَإِنَّا لَنَرَىٰكَ فِینَا ضَعِیفࣰاۖ وَلَوۡلَا رَهۡطُكَ لَرَجَمۡنَـٰكَۖ وَمَاۤ أَنتَ عَلَیۡنَا بِعَزِیزࣲ *  قَالَ یَـٰقَوۡمِ أَرَهۡطِیۤ أَعَزُّ عَلَیۡكُم مِّنَ ٱللَّهِ وَٱتَّخَذۡتُمُوهُ وَرَاۤءَكُمۡ ظِهۡرِیًّاۖ إِنَّ رَبِّی بِمَا تَعۡمَلُونَ مُحِیطࣱ

"Unhone kaha: "Shu'aib (as)! Tumhari bahut si Baaten hamari samajh se upar hai aur ham dekhte hain ke tu hamare darmiyan kamzor shakhs ka fard hai. Agar teri Biradari na hoti to ham kabhi ka tujhe Sangsar (Stoning) kar chuke hote. Tu ham par bhari nahi hai."

"Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne kaha: Kya mera Qabila  tumhari nazar mein Khuda se bhi zyada Mohtaram hai. Tumne Allah ko to pase pusht dal diya hai (neglected). Tum jo kuchh kar rahe ho mera Rab use ghere hue hai."

(Surah Hud: 91 - 92)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) jaari hai:

🕌

Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ne apni Qaum ko unhi ki zabaan mein intihai sada alfaaz mein Tableegh ki thi, magar Aap (as) ke Munkarin ne ye kaha ke Aap (as) ki aksar baaten samajh mein nahi aati. Aap (as) ki Qaum ka ye Jawab is Haqeeqat ka mazhar hai ke un logon ko Aap (as) se sakht nafrat thi. Woh Aap (as) ki Baaton ko sunna hi nahi chahte the aur unhone az rahe Tauheen ye kaha ke pata nahi Aap kis tarah ki baaten kar rahe hain. Jab Insaan Sun-Behra ho jata hai, sunna hi nahi chahta to samajh samajh kar Nasamajh banta phirta hai, apne aap ko hoshiyaar doosron ko bewaqoof khayal karta hai. Inki Aqlon par patthar pad jate hain.

👉🏻

Is Ayat mein Fiqh ka lafz istemal hua hai jiska matlab hai "Samajh boojh".

Aur Rajm - *رجم* means 'Phekna'. Kisi ko qatl ki se Sangsar (Pathrao) karen mein bhi istemal hota hai. Zaban ke zariye kisi ko door karne ke liye bhi istemal hota hai.

Ibne Abbas se Riwayat hai ke Allah ne do Ummaton ko ek hi Azaab se halaak nahi kiya siwai Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) aur Qaum-e-Saleh (as) ke. Qaum-e-Saleh (as) ko Neeche se Cheekh ki Awaaz sunayi di thi jis se woh Qaum halaak ho gayi thi aur Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) ko upar se Cheekh ki Awaaz sunayi di thi.

(To be Cont'd.....)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 🤲🏻

الإمامُ الصّادقُ (عَلَيهِ الّسَلامُ): ما. اجتَمَعَ أربعةُ رَهطٍ قَطُّ على أمرٍ واحدٍ فَدَعَوا اللّه‏َ إلّا تَفَرَّقُوا عن إجابَةٍ.

Imam al-Sadiq (as):

"Jab 4 log group mein kisi kaam ke kiye Dua karne ke liye ikattha hote hain, to woh ek doosre se juda hone se pehle hi unki Dua mustajab ho jati hai."

(Al Kafi, Vol-2, P-487,H-2, Mizanul Hikmah, H-4090)

🤲🏻

Imam Husain (as):

"Aye Woh, Jisne Maa-Baap se meri purdah-poshi ki hai, ke Woh mujhe dhut-kaar denge. Ahl e Qabeela aur bhai-bando'n se mere purdah rakha hai ke mujhe daa'nt-dapat karein. Aur haakimo'n se mera purdah rakha hai ke woh mujhe saza denge. Aye mere Maula! Agar woh mere bare mein woh jaan lete jo Tu jaanta hai to woh mujhe kuchh bhi mohlat na dete, mujhe chhor dete aur qat e talluq kar lete."

(Dua e Arafa)

   17th November 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1569)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ ٱعۡمَلُوا۟ عَلَىٰ مَكَانَتِكُمۡ إِنِّی عَـٰمِلࣱۖ سَوۡفَ تَعۡلَمُونَ مَن یَأۡتِیهِ عَذَابࣱ یُخۡزِیهِ وَمَنۡ هُوَ كَـٰذِبࣱۖ وَٱرۡتَقِبُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُمۡ رَقِیبࣱ

"Aye meri Qaum! Tum apni jagah kaam kiye jao mein bhi amal kar raha hun tum anqareeb jaan loge ke kis par Zillat ka Azaab aata hai aur kaun jhootha hai. Tum bhi intezar karo, mein bhi tumhare saath Intezaar kar raha hun."

(Surah Hud: 93)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Jab Qaume Shu'aib (as) ne apni zor zabardasti dikhayi aur apni baat par ade rahe to Aap (as) ne bhi unko aisa hi jawab diya. Yani ab jo tumhe karna hai karo, tumhe jitni apni taqat lagani hai laga lo. Idhar ham bhi intezar mein hain, ab dekhte jao kya hota hai. Ye log muqabila kar kar rahe the Usse jo Maut o Hayat ka Malik hai. Yani ye ek tarah ka Mubahela tha ke dekhte hain Jhoota kaun hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Christian se Mubahela kiya tha ke Jhooton par Allah ki La'anat Barsegi. Lekin un logon ne Panjetan e Paak (as) ko dekh kar hi Mubahela radd kar diya aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki baat maan li.

Lekin Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) par koi asar na hua aur ye challenge qabool kiya.

Ab Aap (as) ko us waqt ka Intezaar tha ke kab ye Azaab in par aayega.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Reza (as) se Sawaal kiya ke kushaysh (Faraj) kab hogi?Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Kya tum nahi jaante ke Kushayesh ka Intezaar bhi Kushayesh ka ek hissa hai. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ.

"Sabr aur Kushayesh ka Intezaar behtareen cheez hai. Kya tu ne Allah ka ye farman nahi suna:

وَٱرۡتَقِبُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُمۡ رَقِیبࣱ (Hud: 93)

فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ. (7: 71)

"Lehaza tumhe Sabr se kaam lena chahiye. Hamesha Mayusi ke Waqt hi Kushayesh utarti hai. (Kyonki Shab e Siyah ka khatema hamesha Subah par hua karta hai.)Tumse pehle log tumse bade Sabir the."

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنْ حَالَ بَيْنِيْ وَ بَيْنَهُ الْمَوْتُ الَّذِيْ جَعَلْتَهُ عَلٰى عِبَادِكَ حَتْمًا مَقْضِيًّا، فَاَخْرِجْنِيْ مِنْ قَبْرِيْ مُؤْتَزِرًا كَفَنِيْ شَاهِرًا سَيْفِيْ مُجَرِّدًا قَنَاتِيْ

(Dua-e-Ahad)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         2nd Rabius Sani 1442

18th November 2020, Wednesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT SHU'AIB (as)♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1570)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَمَّا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُنَا نَجَّیۡنَا شُعَیۡبࣰا وَٱلَّذِینَ ءَامَنُوا۟ مَعَهُۥ بِرَحۡمَةࣲ مِّنَّا وَأَخَذَتِ ٱلَّذِینَ ظَلَمُوا۟ ٱلصَّیۡحَةُ فَأَصۡبَحُوا۟ فِی دِیَـٰرِهِمۡ جَـٰثِمِینَ * كَأَن لَّمۡ یَغۡنَوۡا۟ فِیهَاۤۗ أَلَا بُعۡدࣰا لِّمَدۡیَنَ كَمَا بَعِدَتۡ ثَمُودُ.

"Jab Hamare Faisle ka waqt aa gaya to Hamne Shu'aib (as) aur uske Momin saathiyon ko Nijaat di aur Zulm karne walon ko ek Sakht Dhamake ne pakad liya aur woh apne gharon mein pade ke pade reh gaye, goya ke woh un gharon mein base hi na the."

"Suno! Madyan wale bhi Qaum-e-Samood ki tarah door hon."

(Surah Hud: 94 - 95)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ka akheri hissa pesh e khidmat hai.

⚡💥

Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) yani Ahle Madyan par jab koi Nasihat kar asar na hua to unka bhi akhari marhala aa gaya. Jo Imaan le aaye the un par Allah ki Rehmat ne unko bacha liya. Baqi is Gumrah, Zalim, aur Hat dharm, Sitamgar Qaum ko ek Zabardast Cheekh ke Azaab ne gher liya.

Allah ka Azaab bhi kuchh hat ke hota hai. Ek awaaz hi Azaab ka sabab ban jati hai jiski wajah se sab se sab halaak ho gaye.

Ibne Abbas se Riwayat hai ke Allah ne do Ummaton ko ek hi Azaab se halaak nahi kiya siwai Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) aur Qaum-e-Saleh (as) ke. Qaum-e-Saleh (as) ko Neeche se Cheekh ki Awaaz sunayi di thi jis se woh Qaum halaak ho gayi thi aur Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) ko upar se Cheekh ki Awaaz sunayi di thi.

Itni zordar dhamakadar Awaaz hui ke sab ke sab apne ghar Mu'nh ke bal gir pade aur pade ke pade reh gaye.

Allah ne jab bhi jis Qaum ko Azaab mein mubtila kiya, use ham log ki zaban mein hi Zhidka: "Door ho ja Meri Nazron se, door ho."

Jab Allah kisi ko door kar de phir usko kaun bacha sakta hai.

Jis cheez par woh ghamand kar rahe the sab dhare dhare reh gaye, na koi Taqat, na Daulat kaam aayi. Ghar Zameen jo unhone abaad ki thi sab chhod gaye.

Qur'an ki ye sab Anbiya ki Dastaane aaj ke logon ke liye bhi sabaq amoz, lesson hain. Isi wajah se Qur'an ne in Dastaanon ko kai bar dohraya hai.

Is Dastaan mein ek hi lesson tha woh Business ke mutalliq tha. Business, dhanda, Karobar Imaandari se karo. Karobar mein apne Maamelat Saaf rakho.

Islam ne Business, Transactions ke bhi Usool wa Shari'at batayi hain jiski pabandi karni chahiye. Hota ye hai ek Tajir, Businessman apne aap ko zyada hoshiyar aur intelligent samajhta hai. Woh apna dimagh nayi nayi chalon, dhoka dhadi ki tarkeebon mein lagata hai. Islam o Insaaniyat mein kisi ko Dhoka dena buri baat /Gunah mana jata hai. Agar Dhande mein Imaandari nahi hogi to pura Business System to kharab hoga hi, Akherat mein bhi usko waisa Azaab milega, Duniya mein uski kamayi hui Rozi se Barkat uth jayegi. Insaan ye sab gadbadi tab karta hai jab woh Allah par Imaan nahi rakhta.

(The End......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jisme ye 2 Aadaten hongi wo achchha hai, warna door ho, door ho, door ho."

Aap se puchha gaya ke wo kaunsi 2 Aadatein hain? Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Namaz ko waqt par baqaida ada karna aur Mohtajo'n aur Qaidiyo'n se hamdardi karna."

(Khisaal, p48)

🤲🏻

اَوْ لَعَلَّكَ لَمْ تُحِبَّ اَنْ تَسْمَعَ دُعَاۤئِیْ فَبَاعَدْتَنِيْ، اَوْ لَعَلَّكَ بِجُرْمِيْ وَ جَرِيْرَتِيْ كَافَيْتَنِيْ،.....

(Dua-e-Abu Hamza Somali)

".... Tu kis qadar mujh se Qareeb hai aur mein kis qadar Tujh se door hun aur jab Tu is qadar Meherban hai to ab kaun darmiyan mein hayel ho sakta hai...."

(Dua-e-Imam Husain (as) Roze Arafa)

 19th November 2020, Thursday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT MOOSA (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1571)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَقَدۡ أَرۡسَلۡنَا مُوسَىٰ بِـَٔایَـٰتِنَا وَسُلۡطَـٰنࣲ مُّبِینٍ *  إِلَىٰ فِرۡعَوۡنَ وَمَلَإِی۟هِۦ فَٱتَّبَعُوۤا۟ أَمۡرَ فِرۡعَوۡنَۖ وَمَاۤ أَمۡرُ فِرۡعَوۡنَ بِرَشِیدࣲ.

"Aur Hamne Firaun aur uske Sardaron (establishment) ki taraf Moosa (as) ko Apni Nishaniyon aur wazeh Sanad ke saath bheja. Unhone Firaun ke hukm ki pairavi ki, halanke Firaun ka Hukm Bhalayi par mabne (based) nahi tha."

(Surah Hud: 96 - 97)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Tazkara Hazrat Shu'aib (as) khatm hone ke baad Hazrat Moosa (as) ka Tazkara shuru karte hai.

👑

Wazeh rahe ke ye Surah Hud ka Satwaan (7th) Qissah hai aur is Surah ka aakheri. Yahan " آيات - Ayaat" se Taurat aur Shari'at o Ahkam hain aur " سلطان مبين - Sultan Mobin" se Hazrat Moosa (as) ke Mo'jezaat (Miracles) murad hain. Maqsad ye hai ke Hazrat Moosa (as) ko Ahkam o Shari'at ke saath uske support mein Daleel ke taur par Mo'jezaat ke saath bheja.

Hazrat Moosa (as) ka waqeat bhi tafseel se guzishta Ayaat wa Surahon mein guzar chuke hain aur ham pesh kar chuke hain.

Mufassarin ke mutabiq 'Sultan e Mobin' se Hazrat Moosa (as) ka 'Asa' murad hai aur 'Ayaat' se wo 9 Ayaat (Nishaniyan) murad hai jo Allah ne unhe ata ki thi:

(1) Yad e Baiza (Glowing Hand) (2) Tufaan (3) Tiddi dal (Locust) (4) Juin (Lice) (5) Medak (Frog) (6) Khoon (7) Samarat (Fruits) wa Nufoos ki kami (8) Badalon ka saaya (9) Darya (River) ka phat jana.

Sultan Badshah ko bhi kehte hain yaani mazbooti aur Daleel ya Certificate ko kehte hain.

Firaun Rushd o Hidayat se koso door tha kyonki woh Badbakht Daherya (Atheist) afraad nazarye ka haamil tha, kisi Khaliq (Creator) aur Ma'ad (Resurrection) ka qael nahi tha. Aur woh ye kehta tha ke Kaynat ka koi Ma'bood nahi hai. Har ilaaqe ke logon ko chahiye ke woh apne Sultan ki Ita'at karen.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as)

se ek shakhs ne puchha ke, "Janabe Moosa (as) Jaadugaro'n ke muqable mein ghabra gaye the, jab ke Janabe Ibrahim (as) to Aag se bhi na ghabraye?" Imam (as) ne jawaab diya, "Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Sulb mein Muhammad (saww) aur Aal e Muhammad (as) ke Anwaar the."

(Tafseer e Anwaar e Najaf, v15, p14)

🤲🏻

.......یَا مُصْطَفِیَ مُوْسٰی بِالْكَلِمَاتِ..........یَا مَنِ اتَّخَذَ مُوْسٰی كَلِیْمًا......

(Dua-e-Mashlool - Mafateeh)

   20th November 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ HAZRAT MOOSA (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1572)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

یَقۡدُمُ قَوۡمَهُۥ یَوۡمَ ٱلۡقِیَـٰمَةِ فَأَوۡرَدَهُمُ ٱلنَّارَۖ وَبِئۡسَ ٱلۡوِرۡدُ ٱلۡمَوۡرُودُ *  وَأُتۡبِعُوا۟ فِی هَـٰذِهِۦ لَعۡنَةࣰ وَیَوۡمَ ٱلۡقِیَـٰمَةِۚ بِئۡسَ ٱلرِّفۡدُ ٱلۡمَرۡفُودُ

"Qayamat ke Din woh (Firaun) apni Qaum ki qayadat (lead) kar raha hoga aur unhe Dozakh ki taraf le jayega. Wo utarne ki bahut buri jagah hai. Unke peechhe is Duniya aur Akherat mein La'anat ko laga diya gaya. Ye kisi ko milne wala kaisa bura silah hai."

(Surah Hud: 98 - 99)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Qaum e Musa (as) wa Firaun ka Tazkara jaari hai.

👑

Ayat ka maqsad ye hai jis tarah se Firaun Duniya mein apni Qaum ka Qaed (Leader) tha usi tarah se Akherat ke Din bhi apni Qaum ka Qaed hoga, ye aur baat hai ke uski Qayadat ne Qaum ko barbaadi ke siwa kuchh nahi diya. Jab usne Duniya mein apni Qaum ki qayadat ki thi to unhe Samandar mein gharq karake dam liya tha aur jab woh Akherat mein Qaum ki qayadat karega to woh unhe Dozakh mein le jayega. Khuda aur Uske Farishte aur Anbiya aur unki Ummaten Duniya o Akherat mein Firaun aur Aale Firaun par La'anat karte rahenge.

Isi tarah ka matlab Ayat Surah Baqarah: 166-167 mein bayan kiya gaya hai jiski tafseel pesh kar chuke hain. Qayamat ke Din jab Ummat apne Farzi Leader ko saza paate dekhegi to bahut mayoos hogi aur chahegi ke in par Tabarrah karen. Lekin us waqt malamat se koi fayda na hoga.

(To be Cont'd......)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Yaqeenan tum mein se badtareen log woh hain jo is baat ko pasand karte hain ke log unke peechhe chalein. Yaqeenan aise log ya to jhoote hote hain ya unki raai kamzor hoti hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p41)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّي صَلَّيْتُ هٰذِهِ الصَّلٰوةَ ابْتِغَاۤءَ مَرْضَاتِكَ وَ طَلَبَ نَاۤئِلِكَ وَ رَجَاۤءَ رِفْدِكَ وَ جَوَاۤئِزِكَ فَصَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.....

(Dua in Aamaal e Masjid e Sehla - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

     ♦ QASASUL ANBIYA (as) ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1573)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ مِنۡ أَنۢبَاۤءِ ٱلۡقُرَىٰ نَقُصُّهُۥ عَلَیۡكَۖ مِنۡهَا قَاۤىِٕمࣱ وَحَصِیدࣱ *  وَمَا ظَلَمۡنَـٰهُمۡ وَلَـٰكِن ظَلَمُوۤا۟ أَنفُسَهُمۡۖ فَمَاۤ أَغۡنَتۡ عَنۡهُمۡ ءَالِهَتُهُمُ ٱلَّتِی یَدۡعُونَ مِن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ مِن شَیۡءࣲ لَّمَّا جَاۤءَ أَمۡرُ رَبِّكَۖ وَمَا زَادُوهُمۡ غَیۡرَ تَتۡبِیبࣲ *  وَكَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ أَخۡذُ رَبِّكَ إِذَاۤ أَخَذَ ٱلۡقُرَىٰ وَهِیَ ظَـٰلِمَةٌۚ إِنَّ أَخۡذَهُۥۤ أَلِیمࣱ شَدِیدٌ.

"Ye Chand Bastiyon ki sarguzisht jo Ham aap se bayan kar rahe hain. Un mein se kuchh abhi khadi hain aur kuchh ki Fasal kat chuki hai."

"Hamne un par Zulm nahi kiya. Unhone apne aap par khud hi Zulm tha aur jab tere Rab ka Hukm aa gaya to unke woh Ma'bood unke kuchh kaam na aaye jinhe woh Khuda pukara karte the. Unhone halakat o barbadi ke siwa un mein kuchh izaafa nahi kiya. Aur tera Rab jab kisi Basti ko pakadta hai to Uski Pakad aisi hua karti hai. Yaqeenan Khuda ki Pakad Sakht, Dardnak hoti hai."

(Surah Hud: 100 - 102)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Surah e Mubarakah mein Allah Ta'ala ne 7 Anbiya aur unki Aqwaam ki Dastaan bayan ki hai aur farmaya hai ke ye Zalim Bastiyon ki sarguzisht hai, jin par Hamne Zulm nahi kiya tha. Unhone khud hi apne upar Zulm kiya tha aur jab Hamara Azaab nazil hua to unke khud sakhta (Fabricated, Fake) Ma'bood (Deity) unki koi madad na kar sake the.

Iske peechhe do Hikmaten hain:

1. Khalis Aqli Daleel Insaane Kamil ke liye mufeed hoti hai, aam afraad ke liye kuchh faydemand nahi hoti. Dalail (Proofs) bayan karne ke baad agar gawah wa mushahede ke taur par isse mutalliq kuchh waqeaat o Qasas (Stories) bayan kiye jayen to baat mein asar paida hota hai.

2. Qurani Qisse (Stories) sirf Dastaan sarai (story telling, folk tale) tak mehdood nahi hai. In mein Anbiya aur unki Ummaton ki guftugu ki tafseel bhi maujood hai aur Kuffar ke tamam etrazat ke jawab bhi bayan kiye gaye hain. Isliye Qurani Qisse shukook o shubhaat (doubts) ka azala (clear) karte hain aur Ahle Dil ko Nasihat faraham karte hain.

Jin Bastiyon par Khuda ka Azaab aaya un mein se kuchh aisi hain jinke nishan Duniya mein aaj tak baqi hain aur wo aane wali Naslon je liye baes e ibrat ban chuki hain jabke baaz Azaab shuda Bastiyan aisi bhi hain jinke naam o nishan tak Duniya se mit chuke hain.

Khuda Adil hai, kisi par Zulm nahi karta. Punishment aur Oppression mein difference hai, Saza aur Zulm aur hain. Saza dena Zulm nahi kehlata.

Kuffar ye aqeeda rakhte the ke jinko woh Poojte hain, woh unko bacha lenge. Lekin Jin ko woh maante the koi bachane nahi aaya.

Waqea mashoor hai jab Kashti doob rahi thi, to musafiron ne pehle ko, doosre wa teesre ko apne apne hisaab se pukara jab koi nahi aaya to sab Aliwale ki taraf rukh kiya aur usne Ya Ali Madad keh kar naara lagaya to Kadhti bhanwar se nikal gayi. Isliye Haq ka daaman chhod kar idhar udhar bhatkenge to Khasaare ke alawa kuchh na milega.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Zulm karte waqt apne baare mein Khuda ke Adl ko yaad rakho aur taaqat o qudrat ke waqt ye yaad rakho ke tum Khuda ki Qudrat se baahar nahi ho."

(Gorar ul Hakam, v2, p33)

🤲🏻

Imam Sajjad (as):

"Aye Ma'bood! Beshak Tu ne Apni Kitaab mein ye Hukm naazil kiya hai jo hum par zulm kare use Ma'af kar de. Zaroor humne apne Nafso'n par zulm kiya, Tu humen Ma'af farma."

(Dua e Abu Hamza Shimaali)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         6th Rabiul Akhir 1442

  22nd November 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ YAUMUL HASHR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1574)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

إِنَّ فِی ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ لَـَٔایَةࣰ لِّمَنۡ خَافَ عَذَابَ ٱلۡـَٔاخِرَةِۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ یَوۡمࣱ مَّجۡمُوعࣱ لَّهُ ٱلنَّاسُ وَذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ یَوۡمࣱ مَّشۡهُودࣱ *  وَمَا نُؤَخِّرُهُۥۤ إِلَّا لِأَجَلࣲ مَّعۡدُودࣲ *  یَوۡمَ یَأۡتِ لَا تَكَلَّمُ نَفۡسٌ إِلَّا بِإِذۡنِهِۦۚ فَمِنۡهُمۡ شَقِیࣱّ وَسَعِیدࣱ.

"Azaab e Akherat se darne wale ke liye is mein Nishani (Ayat) hai. Wo ek aisa Din hoga jis mein sab log jama kiye jatenge aur ye aisa Din hoga jiski Gawahi di jayegi. Ham us Din ke laane mein gini hui muddat tak hi takheer kar rahe hain. Jab wo Din aayega to Khuda ki ijazat ke baghair kisi baat karne ki majal na hogi. Us Din kuchh afraad Bad-bakht honge aur kuchh Nek-bakht honge."

(Surah Hud: 103 - 105)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Roze Akherat ke Allah ne do Ausaaf (features) bayan kiye hain:

1. Us Din tamam log jama kiye jayenge. (Yaume Hashr)

2. Us Din tamam log Bargahe Ahdiyyat (Khuda) mein hazir honge.

Khuda ki taraf se Ayyam e Duniya (Period of World) ki ginti muqarrar ho chuki hai aur jo bhi Din guzarta hai uske guzarne ke saath Qayamat qareeb ho rahi hai aur jo cheez shumar (ginti) mein aa jaye wo ahista ahista khatm ho jati hai.

👉🏻

Ab is Ayat mein jo kaha gaya hai ke koi Qayamat ke Din Hukme Khuda ke baghair bol nahi payega. Jabke ek Ayat mein ye hai

"Har Nafs apni zat ka difa kar raha hoga." (16:111)

Ya jhooti Qasmen kha kar kahenge "Mein Mushrik nahi hun." (6:23) "Unhe roko unse sawal kiya jayega." (37:24) "Ye woh Din hai jis mein woh kuchh na bolenge aur na unhe mauqa diya jayega ......" (77:35-36) "Unke Munh par Mohr laga di jayegi." (36:65)

In Ayaat mein koi Tazaad (Difference) nahi hai. Asl baat ye hai ke wo intihai taweel Din hoga. Is mein bahut se Moqif (Stops) honge. Kuchh Moqif par woh apna difa karenge, to kuchh Moqif par Kalam band hoga. Kuchh par ijazat hogi jabke kuchh par unke Zabano par Mohr laga di jayegi aur sirf doosre aazaa jaise Haath Paon hi gawahi denge.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Roz e Qayamat Khuda logo'n ko ek zameen mein jamaa  karega aur Meezan rakhi jayegi aur Shahido'n ke khoon ko Ulema ke qalam se wazn kiya jayega aur Ulema ke qalam ki syaahi (ink) Shohda ke khoon se zyada wazni (heavy) hogi."

(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p166)

🤲🏻

صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَّ عَلٰى اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَّاجْعَلْنِىْ مِنْ اَتْبَاعِهٖ وَ شِيْعَتِهٖ وَاحْشُرْنِىْ فِىْ زُمْرَتِهٖ وَ وَفِّقْنِىْ لِاَدَاۤءِ فَرْضِ الْجُمُعَاتِ وَ مَا اَوْجَبْتَ عَلَىَّ فِيْهَا مِنَ الطَّاعَاتِ وَ قَسَمْتَ لِاَهْلِهَا مِنَ الْعَطَاۤءِ فِىْ يَوْمِ الْجَزَاۤءِ اِنَّكَ اَنْتَ الْعَزِيْزُ الْحَكِيْمُ۔

(Dua e Roze Juma - Mafateeh)

  23rd November 2020, Monday

          ♦ SHAQI & SAEED ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1575)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 ...فَمِنۡهُمۡ شَقِیࣱّ وَسَعِیدࣱ *  فَأَمَّا ٱلَّذِینَ شَقُوا۟ فَفِی ٱلنَّارِ لَهُمۡ فِیهَا زَفِیرࣱ وَشَهِیقٌ *  خَـٰلِدِینَ فِیهَا مَا دَامَتِ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تُ وَٱلۡأَرۡضُ إِلَّا مَا شَاۤءَ رَبُّكَۚ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ فَعَّالࣱ لِّمَا یُرِیدُ.

"Us Din kuchh afraad Bad-bakht honge aur kuchh Nek-bakht honge. Jo Bad-bakht honge woh Dozakh mein jayenge jahan unki Aahen aur Cheekhen buland hongi. Jab tak Zameen o Aasmaan qaem hain woh usi haalat mein rahenge. Haan, tera Rab Chaahe to uska maamla juda hai. Beshak tera Rab jo Chahta use baja lata hai."

(Surah Hud: 105 - 107)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Yahan jo do group ka tazkara kiya gaya hai ye woh log hain jinhe Hisaab dena hai.

Rasoole Khuda (saww) se is silsile mein sawal kiye gaye to Aap (saww) ne farmaya:

"Khuda baghair Daleel o Burhaan ke kisi ko Azaab nahi deta. Baqi woh Mushrekin ke Bachche jo bachpan mein hi mar gaye ye hai ke, jab Qayamat ka Din hoga to tamam Makhlooq Bargahe Khuda wandi mein Hisaab ke liye pesh hogi aur Mushrekin ki Aulad bhi us mein shamil hogi. Allah Ta'ala farmayega: Aye mere Bandon aur meri Kaneezon! Tumhara Rab kaun hai? Aur Tumhara Deen kya hai aur tumhare Aamal kaise hain?"

Us waqt woh arz karenge: "Tu ne hamen paida kiya aur phir hame mar diya tha. Hamare paas bolne wali Zabaan na thi aur sunne wale Kaan nahi the. Hamne na to koi Kitab padhi thi aur na hi hamen kisi Rasool ki pairavi ka mauqa mila tha. Hame to kuchh Ilm nahi hai siwai iske jo Tu ne ata kiya hai."

Us waqt Nida e Qudrat buland hogi: "Aye mere Bandon aur Kaneezon! Agar Mein tumhe koi Hukm dun to kya tum us par Amal karoge?" Woh kahenge 'Ji haan.'

Us waqt Khuda ke Hukm se Dozakh ke darmiyan se "Falaq - *فلق* " naami Aag baramad hogi jo ke intihai Siyah (black) hogi aur Malaika use Zanjeeron se jakde hue honge. Woh Aag Saans legi aur uske Saans ki tapish se Aasmaan gir padega, Sitaare be-Noor ho jayenge aur Samandar munjamid (solidify) ho jayenge aur Haamla Janwaron ke Hamal gir padenge aur iski dehshat se Bachche Budhe honge. Us waqt Allah Ta'ala Aulad e Mushrekin se kahega ke tum is mein chale jao. Un mein se jo Ilm e Ilahi ke tehte Sa'adat mand honge woh be khatar Aag mein kood padenge. Aag unke liye Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki tarah se thandak aur Salamti ban jayegi aur jo Khuda ke Ilm ke tehet Babakht honge woh us Aag mein jaane se inkar kar dengen. Dozakh ki Aag unhe Arsa e Mehshar se utha legi aur woh apne Abaa o Ajdaad ke saath Dozakh mein chale jayenge aur is baat ko Allah Ta'ala ne is Ayat (11:105-108) mein bayan kiya hai."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Hasan (as):

"Log 4 qism ke hain:

(1) Nek Akhlaaq hain magar Daulatmand nahi hain,

(2) Daulatmand hain magar Nek Akhlaaq nahi,

(3) Jo na Nek Akhlaaq hai na Daulatmand. Ye tamam Aadmiyo'n se zyada bad-bakht hai,

(4) Nek Akhlaaq bhi hai aur Daulatmand bhi hai. Ye log tamam logo'n se achche hain."

(Khisaal, p127)

🤲🏻

يَا مَوْلَايَ شَقِيَ مَنْ خَالَفَكُمْ وَ سَعِدَ مَنْ اَطَاعَكُمْ....

"Ay mere Maula! Shaqi woh hai jisne Aapki Mukhalefat ki, Saeed (Khushnaseeb) woh hai jisne Aapki Ita'at ki..."

(Ziyarat e Aale Yasin - Mafateeh)

SHIA CHANNEL CELEBRATES WILADAT OF IMAM HASAN ASKARI (as)

🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹

         8th Rabius Sani 1442

  24th November 2020, Tuesday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

Hadis e Lauh mein Imam Askari (as) ka zikr:

*"ابو محمد الحسن بن على(ع) الرفيق، أمه جاريه، إسمها سمانة، تكني بٱم الحسن، الْخَازِنَ لِعِلْمِی  وَ أُکمِلُ ذَلِک بِابْنِهِ محمد رَحْمَةً لِلْعَالَمِینَ عَلَیهِ کمَالُ مُوسَی وَ بَهَاءُ عِیسَی وَ صَبْرُ أَیوبَ فَیذَلُّ أَوْلِیائِی فِی زَمَانِهِ وَ تُتَهَادَی رُءُوسُهُمْ."*

"Abu Mohd Al Hasan bin Ali (as), Al Rafeeq, unki madaregrami Kaneez Samana, unki Kunniyat Ummul Hasan, Ilm ka Khazana, unke bete Muhammad par (Imamat) ki takmeel hui."

(Kamaluddin, Vol 1, P-308)

🌷 Biography of Imam Askari (as), Click:

https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hasan_al-Askari

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ SHAQI & SAEED ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1576)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 ...فَمِنۡهُمۡ شَقِیࣱّ وَسَعِیدࣱ *.......وَأَمَّا ٱلَّذِینَ سُعِدُوا۟ فَفِی ٱلۡجَنَّةِ خَـٰلِدِینَ فِیهَا مَا دَامَتِ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تُ وَٱلۡأَرۡضُ إِلَّا مَا شَاۤءَ رَبُّكَۖ عَطَاۤءً غَیۡرَ مَجۡذُوذࣲ.

"Us Din kuchh afraad Bad-bakht honge aur kuchh Nek-bakht honge........."

"Woh log jo Nek-bakht (Saeed) honge woh Jannat mein jayenge aur jab tak Zameen o Aasmaan qaem hain woh us mein hamesha rahenge. Siwai iske tera Rab kuchh aur chahe. Unhe aisi Bakhshish milegi jiska silsila muqata (cut) na hoga."

(Surah Hud: 108)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah ne Makhlooq paida karne se qabl Khush-Naseebi aur Bad-Naseebi ko paida kiya jise Khuda ne Khush-Naseeb bana kar bheja hai woh kisi se kabhi Bughz na rakhega aur agar woh bura kaam bhi karega to us bure kaam se nafrat karega, lekin kaam karne wale se kabhi nafrar na karega. Aur jisko Shaqi bana kar paida kiya hai to usse kabhi Muhabbat nahi karega. Agar woh koi Nek Amal karega to uske Amal se Muhabbat karega, lekin Amal karne wale se phir bhi nafrat karega. Jab Allah kisi se Muhabbat karta hai to kabhi usse nafrat nahi karta aur jab kisi se Bughz rakhta hai to usse kabhi Muhabbat nahi karta."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Baaz auqaat ek Khush-Naseeb fard Bad-Naseeb afraad ke raaste par chalta hai. Log ye kehte hain ke ye to Bad-bakht afraad ke mushabeh (similar) hai, balke ye unka hi ek fard hai. Phir Qudrat ki taraf se Sa'adat o Khush-Bakhshi use hasil ho jati hai. Aur baaz auqaat ek Bad-bakht shakhs Khush-Naseeb afraad ke raaste par chalta hai. Uske tarz e amal ko dekh kar log ye kehte hain ke ye shakhs Khush-Naseeb afraad mein kitna hi mushabeh hai, balke ye to unki Jamat ka hi ek fard hai. Phir achanak uski Bad-bakhti use apni lapet mein le leti hai jise Khuda ne Khush-Naseeb likha hua ho. Agar uski tamam Umr bhi Bad-bakhti ke raaste mein basar hui aur uski Umr khatm hone mein itna time ho jis mein Oontni ko dooha ja sakta ho to bhi uska anjaam Sa'adat aur Khush-Naseebi hoga."

(Noorus Saqlain)

⚜️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Allah apne Bande ko Shaqawat se nikal kar Sa'adat par to le aata hai, magar kisi ko Sa'adat se Shaqawat ki taraf muntaqil nahi karta."

(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as):

"Rehm e Maadar (Womb) mein Nutfa 40 Din tak Nutfe ke hi shakl mein rehta hai. Jo koi Bete Beti ke liye Dua karta ho to woh ineqaad Nutfa ke ibtedai 40 Dino (initial stage) mein hi Dua maange. Iske baad Allah us Farishte ko bhejta hai jo Ihaam par moakkal hai woh use Khuda ke Huzoor le jata hai, jab tak Khuda chahta hai woh khada rehta hai. Phir woh kehta hai: Khudaya! Ise Nar banana hai ya Maada (Male or Female)? Allah jo Chahta hai use uska Hukm deta hai. Hukme Khuda wandi ko Farishta likh leta hai. Iske baad woh arz karta hai ke: Khudaya! Ye Shaqi hai ya Saeed? Allah jo chahta hai uski taraf Wahy kar deta hai aur Farishta use likh leta hai."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

وَ سَوَّلَتْ لِيْ نَفْسِيْ، وَ غَلَبَنِيْ هَوَايَ، وَ اَعَانَنِيْ عَلَيْهَا شِقْوَتِيْ،۔۔۔۔

(Dua-e-Hamza Somali - Mafateeh)

25th November 2020, Wednesday

          ♦ SHAQI & SAEED ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1577)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 ...فَمِنۡهُمۡ شَقِیࣱّ وَسَعِیدࣱ *.......فَأَمَّا ٱلَّذِینَ شَقُوا۟ فَفِی ٱلنَّارِ لَهُمۡ فِیهَا زَفِیرࣱ وَشَهِیقٌ *  خَـٰلِدِینَ فِیهَا مَا دَامَتِ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تُ وَٱلۡأَرۡضُ إِلَّا مَا شَاۤءَ رَبُّكَۚ إِنَّ رَبَّكَ فَعَّالࣱ لِّمَا یُرِیدُ * وَأَمَّا ٱلَّذِینَ سُعِدُوا۟ فَفِی ٱلۡجَنَّةِ خَـٰلِدِینَ فِیهَا مَا دَامَتِ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تُ وَٱلۡأَرۡضُ إِلَّا مَا شَاۤءَ رَبُّكَۖ عَطَاۤءً غَیۡرَ مَجۡذُوذࣲ.

"Us Din kuchh afraad Bad-bakht honge aur kuchh Nek-bakht honge........."

"Woh log jo Nek-bakht (Saeed) honge woh Jannat mein jayenge aur jab tak Zameen o Aasmaan qaem hain woh us mein hamesha rahenge. Siwai iske tera Rab kuchh aur chahe. Unhe aisi Bakhshish milegi jiska silsila muqata (cut) na hoga."

(Surah Hud: 106 - 108)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:  (Cont'd)

Hazrat Ali (as):

"Sa'adat ki Haqeeqat ye hai ke kisi ka Anjaam Khush-Naseebi par Muntij (result) ho, aur Shaqawat ki Haqeeqat bhi yehi hai ke kisi ka Anjaam Bad-bakhti par Muntij ho."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) se 'Maut ki Haqeeqat' ke bare mein sawal hua, to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Maut 3 mein se ek Haalat ki mazhar zaroor hoti hai. Maut ya to Abadi Ne'maat (Eternal Blessings) ki Bashaarat le kar aati hai ye phir Abadi Azaab (Eternal Chastisement) ka Paigham le kar aati hai ya phir Khauf aur Mubham (Ambiguous) halaat le kar warid hoti hai aur marne wale ke anjam ke mutalliq koi Ilm nahi hota ke iska talluq do fariqon mein se kis ke saath hai."

"Hamare Dost aur hamare Ahkam ki Ita'at karnewale ke liye Maut Abadi Ne'maat ka Paigham le kar aati hai. Aur hamare Dushman aur Mukhalif ke liye Abadi Azaab ka Paigham le kar aati hai. Aur woh shakhs jiski haalat Mubham hoti hai to ye us Momin ki haalat hai jo apne Nafs par tajawuz karnewala hota hai. Iske liye Maut Mubham aur Ghamgeen kaifiyat le kar aati hai, lekin yaad rakho hamare us Gunahgar Dost se Allah hamare Dushman jaisa sulook nahi karta. Khuda hamari Shafa'at ki wajah se use Dozakh se nikalega. Lehaza tum Amal karo aur Ita'at karo aur Khudayi Saza ko haqeer na samjho. Kuchh aise israaf karne wale bhi honge ke 3 Lakh Saal Azaab sehne ke baad unhe hamari Shafa'at naseeb hogi."

(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜️

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

"Ankhon ka khushk hona, Dil ki sakhti, Talab e Rizq ki shadeed Hirs aur Gunahon par israar ka talluq Bad-Naseebi ki Alamat se hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

...يَا مَوْلَايَ شَقِيَ مَنْ خَالَفَكُمْ وَ سَعِدَ مَنْ اَطَاعَكُمْ......

"Aye mere Maula! Shaqi (Bad-bakht) woh hai jisne Aapki Mukhalefat ki, Saeed  (Khush-Naseeb) woh hai jisne Aapki Ita'at ki....."

(Ziyarat-e-Aale Yasin - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ BAAZ NA AANE WALE LOG ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1578)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 فَلَا تَكُ فِی مِرۡیَةࣲ مِّمَّا یَعۡبُدُ هَـٰۤؤُلَاۤءِۚ مَا یَعۡبُدُونَ إِلَّا كَمَا یَعۡبُدُ ءَابَاۤؤُهُم مِّن قَبۡلُۚ وَإِنَّا لَمُوَفُّوهُمۡ نَصِیبَهُمۡ غَیۡرَ مَنقُوصࣲ.

"Aye Nabi! Aap in Ma'boodon ki taraf se kisi Shak mein na rahen jinki woh Ibaadat kar rahe hain. Ye log apne Aba o Ajdaad (Forefathers) ki tarah se Buton ki Pooja pat kar rahe hain. Ham inhe unka bhar poor hissa denge jis mein kisi tarah kami nahi ki jayegi."

(Surah Hud: 109)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ye Ayat Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko dilasa wa diljoi kar rahi hai. Kyonki guzishta Qaumon ke halaat ko dekha, unki harkaton ki wajah se kaise kaise Azaab aaye. Aap (saww) ne bhi Kuffar ko Buton ki pooja karte dekha to unki halaat dekh kar ranjeeda hae. Woh Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Nasihaton ke bawajood wohi unke Dada-pardada ki rawish par chal rahe the, baaz na aaye. Allah ne kaha ke unko unka poora Ajr milega. Yani Khuda ki Mukhalefat ka poora silah Azaab ki surat mein unhe milega. Lekin Allah mohlat deta hai, ke upni poori Umr ke darmiyan kabhi to Raahe Raast par aa jayen. Bahut se But-Parast kuchh Dunyavi Nek kaam bhi karte hain, jaise kisi par Ehsaan karna, ghareebon ki madad karna, khairaat karna etc. Allah unka Ajr is Duniya mein hi de deta hai aur Akhirat mein khali haath jata hai. Sab se pehle Aqeeda par sawal hoga, uske Amaal baad mein dekhe jayenge.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Khuda ne jis Bande se kisi achche kaam karne par Ajr o Sawaab ka waada farmaya hai, Wo use zaroor poora kar ke rahega. Aur jis Bande ko kisi bure kaam karne par Saza dene ki dhamki di hai, usme Use ikhtiyaar hai." (ke Saza de ya Ma'af kar de kyunki Uska Saza dena Adl hai aur Ma'af karna Fazl hai).

(Wasaail ush Shia, v1, p80)

⚜️

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Yaqeenan Akherat ki Niyyat se Duniya ka jo kaam karoge uska Ajr (Sawaab) Duniya mein milega lekin Duniya ki Niyyat se jo Akherat ka kaam karoge, Allah uska Ajr hargiz nahi dega."

(Hadiyat ush Shia, p36)

🤲🏻

......ثُمَّ جَعَلْتَ اَجْرَ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَوَاتُكَ عَلَیْهِ وَ اٰلِهٖ مَوَدَّتَھُمْ فِیْ كِتَابِكَ فَقُلْتَ قُلْ لَاۤ اَسْئَلُكُمْ عَلَیْهِ اَجْرًا اِلَّا الْمَوَدَّۃَ فِی الْقُرْبٰی وَ قُلْتَ مَا سَئَلْتُكُمْ مِنْ اَجْرٍ فَھُوَ لَكُمْ وَ قُلْتَ مَاۤ اَسْئَلُكُمْ عَلَیْهِ مِنْ اَجْرٍ اِلَّا مَنْ شَاۤءَاَنْ یَّتَّخِذَ اِلٰی رَبِّهٖ سَبِیْلًا فَكَانُوْا ھُمُ السَّبِیْلَ اِلَیْكَ وَ الْمَسْلَكَ اِلٰی رِضْوَانِكَ....

(Dua-e-Nudba - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
