⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ MASHKOOK AFRAAD ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1578)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

 وَلَقَدۡ ءَاتَیۡنَا مُوسَى ٱلۡكِتَـٰبَ فَٱخۡتُلِفَ فِیهِۚ وَلَوۡلَا كَلِمَةࣱ سَبَقَتۡ مِن رَّبِّكَ لَقُضِیَ بَیۡنَهُمۡۚ وَإِنَّهُمۡ لَفِی شَكࣲّ مِّنۡهُ مُرِیبࣲ *  وَإِنَّ كُلࣰّا لَّمَّا لَیُوَفِّیَنَّهُمۡ رَبُّكَ أَعۡمَـٰلَهُمۡۚ إِنَّهُۥ بِمَا یَعۡمَلُونَ خَبِیرࣱ * فَٱسۡتَقِمۡ كَمَاۤ أُمِرۡتَ وَمَن تَابَ مَعَكَ وَلَا تَطۡغَوۡا۟ۚ إِنَّهُۥ بِمَا تَعۡمَلُونَ بَصِیرࣱ.

"Yaqeenan Hamne Moosa (as) ko Kitab ata ki. Is mein Ikhtelaf kiya gaya hai. Agar tere Rab ki taraf se ek baat pehle se tai shudah na hoti to ikhtelaf karne walon ke darmiyan faisla chuka diya gaya hota. Ye log Uski taraf se khiljaan (Staunch Doubt) paida karane wale Shak mein mubtila hain. Yaqeenan tera Rab un sab ko unke Aamaal ka badla de kar rahega. Woh unke Aamaal se poori tarah ba-Khabar hai."

"Aye Nabi! Jaisa tumhe Hukm diya gaya hai usi tarah se Isteqamat ikhtiyar karo aur Aapke woh saathi bhi Isteqamat ikhtiyar karen jo Haq ki taraf palat aaye hain aur tajawuz na karo. Beshak jo kuchh tum Amal kar rahe ho unhe Khuda dekh raha hai."

(Surah Hud: 110 - 112)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Allah ne pichhli Ummaton ka Zikr karke bata diya ke jisko Imaan nahi lana hai woh nahi layega, ghabrane ki koi zaroorat nahi hai. Unko uski jaza milege. Jab Yahoodiyon ne Hazrat Moosa (as) ki Torah ko change kar diya aur asl aasmani Kitab ko nahi maana to ye aaj ke Kuffar kya maanenge, chahe ham kitne hi Qur'an ke Mojize bayan karte rahen. Woh doubt mein hi rahenge. Hamari zimmedari hai Hidayat karna, ab koi maane ya na maane. Jo Shaqi tha woh Shaqi rahega, jo Saeed hai woh Saeed.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Ali (as):

"Tajjub hai aur mujhe kaise tajjub na ho un Giroho'n ki khataao'n par jinhone apne Deen ki hujjato'n mein ikhtelaf paida kar rakhe hain. Jo na Nabi ke naqsh e qadam par chalte hain, na Wasi ke amal ki pairavi karte hain, na Ghaib par Imaan laate hain, na Aib se daaman bachate hain. Maskook (Doubtful) cheezo'n par amal karte hain aur apni khwaisho'n (ki Duniya) mein chalte phirte hain. Unke nazdeek bus wohi cheez achchi hai jisko wo achcha samajhte hain aur wohi cheez buri hai jisko wo bura jaante hain. Mushkil gutthiyo'n ko suljhaane ke liye unhone apne Nafso'n par etemaad kar liya hai aur mushtaba (Ambiguous) cheezo'n mein apni Raai par bharosa kar liya hai, goya un mein se har shakhs apna Imam hai aur usne apni jagah jo faisla apni Raai se kar liya hai uske baare mein ye khayal karta hai ke ise qaabil e itminaan zariyo'n se haasil kiya hai."

(Nahjul Balagah, Sermon 88 (About the division of the community into factions (causes of people’s destruction)), Ghorarul Hakam, v2, p494, Nahjul Balagah, Khutba 88 (Jisme logo'n Ki Halaakat ke Asbaab bayan kiye gaye hain)

🤲🏻

اَنَّكَ حُجَّةُ اللّٰهِ، اَنْتُمْ الْاَوَّلُ وَ الْاٰخِرُ وَ اَنَّ رَجْعَتَكُمْ حَقٌّ لَا رَيْبَ فِيْهَا يَوْمَ لَا يَنْفَعُ نَفْسًا اِيْمَانُهَا لَمْ تَكُنْ اٰمَنَتْ مِنْ قَبْلُ اَوْ كَسَبَتْ فِيۤ اِيْمَانِهَا خَيْرًا وَ اَنَّ الْمَوْتَ حَقٌّ وَ اَنَّ نَاكِرًا وَ نَكِيْرًا حَقٌّ.......

(Ziyarat-e-Aale Yasin - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         12th Rabiul Akhir 1442

  28th November 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ♦ ZALIM KI TARAF JHUKAO ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1579)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَا تَرۡكَنُوۤا۟ إِلَى ٱلَّذِینَ ظَلَمُوا۟ فَتَمَسَّكُمُ ٱلنَّارُ وَمَا لَكُم مِّن دُونِ ٱللَّهِ مِنۡ أَوۡلِیَاۤءَ ثُمَّ لَا تُنصَرُونَ.

"Zalimon ki taraf bilkul na jhukna warna tum log bhi Dozakh ki lapet mein aa jaoge aur tumhe Khuda ke alawa koi Madadgar nahi milega. Phir tumhari Madad na ki jayegi."

(Surah Hud: 113)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Kazim (as) ke ek Mukhlis Sahabi the, Safwan Jammal. Unhone apne Oont Khalifa Haroon Rashid ko kiraye par diye jo Hajj par ja raha tha. Imam (as) ki Safwan se mulaqat hui to Aap (as) ne Safwan se farmaya: Safwan, tumhare sab kam achhe hain, lekin ek ghalti ki. Oont ko kiraye par de kar. Safwan ne kaha: 'Maula! meine to Nek kaam ke liye diye. Woh Hajj par ja raha hai.' Imam (as) ne farmaya: 'Ab tum dua karoge ke jab tak tumhara Kiraya na mil jaye tab tak woh Zinda rahe. Is tarah tum ek Zalim ke liye uski Baqa ke liye Dua karoge.' (Yani jab tak tumhara jhukao, dhayan, tawajjoh us Zalim ki taraf rahega.) Safwan ne is baat ki tasdeeq ki, ji haan aisa hi hai. Safwan ko Imam (as) ki ye baat dil mein utar gayi aur unhone apne sare Oont bech diye, taake Zalim ke dabao se bach jayen.

Itna sa Zalim ki taraf jhukna Imam (as) pasand nahi to unka kya hoga jo Zalim Hukumat ki Chaplosi, chamchagiri mein lage rehte hain. Ye log Daulat, Shohrat, Hukumat ke khatir apna Imaan bech dete hain.

⚜️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jo kisi Zalim ki baqa ke liye itni der ki khwahish kare ke woh apna haath Jeb mein dal kar use kuchh Sikke pakdaye to amali taur par (practically) woh Zalimon ki taraf jhukao ke jurm mein sharik hai."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜️

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Zalim ki taraf jhukao se Insaan abadi (Eternal) Dozakh ka Haqdar nahi banta, albatta Dozakh mas (touch) zaroor karegi, isliye Zalimon ki taraf jhukao na rakho."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasoole Akram (saww):

"Zalim ki taraf jhukao na rakhna, agarche woh tumhara qareebi Dost hi kyon na ho."

(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Zainul Abedin (as):

"Duniya ki taraf jhukao na rakho, kyonki Allah Ta'ala ne Musalmano se kaha hai ke Zalimon ki taraf kabhi jhokao na rakho, warna tum bhi Dozakh ki lapet mein aa jaoge."

(Roza e Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Hasan (as):

"Behtareen maaldaari Qana'at hai aur bad-tareen faqeeri (daulat-mando'n ke saamne) sar jhukaana hai."

(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p85)

🕌

Imam Hasan (as)

se puchha gaya ke Buzdili kya hai? Aap ne farmaya: “Dost par Jari (needar / audacious) hona aur Dushman ke saamne Jhuk jaana."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p58)

🤲🏻

صَلِّ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ اٰلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَاَعِنِّىْ عَلٰى بَوَاۤئِقِ الدُّهُوْرِ وَصُرُوْفِ اللَّیَالِىْ وَالْاَیَّامِ وَنَجِّنِىْ مِنْ اَهْوَالِ الدُّنْیَا وَكُرُبَاتِ الْاٰ خِرَۃِ وَاكْفِنِىْ شَرَّ مَا یَعْمَلُ الظَّالِمُوْنَ فِى الْاَرْضِ .......

(Dua-e-Arafa - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU

         13th Rabius Sani 1442

  29th November 2020, Sunday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ NAKI BURAYI KO DHO DETI HAI. ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1580)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ طَرَفَیِ ٱلنَّهَارِ وَزُلَفࣰا مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِۚ *إِنَّ ٱلۡحَسَنَـٰتِ یُذۡهِبۡنَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ ذِكۡرَىٰ لِلذَّ ٰ⁠كِرِینَ *  وَٱصۡبِرۡ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا یُضِیعُ أَجۡرَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ.*

"Aur Namaz qaem karo Din ke dono siron par aur kuchh Raat guzarne par. *Dar haqeeqat Nekiyan Buraiyyon ko door kar deti hain.* Ye Khuda ko yaad rakhne walon ke liye yaad dahani hai. Sabr karo, yaqeenan Allah Neki karnewalon ka Ajr (Reward) zaaye (waste) nahi karta."

(Surah Hud: 114 - 115)

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Imam Ali (as):

"Allah Ta'ala har Neki ki wajah se ek na ek Burayi khatm kar deta hai, kyonki Allah Ta'ala ka Farman hai (11:114)"

(Amaali Shaikh Tusi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Rasoole Akram (as):

"Jab koi Banda Neki ka iraada kar ke us par Amal karta hai to uske Naama e Aamaal mein poori Neki ka Sawab likha jata hai aur usje Naama e Aamaal mein Das Nekiyan likhi jati hain aur agar koi shakhs Neki ki Niyyat ke baad Neki na baja la sake to uski Sachchi Niyyat ki wajah se uske Naama e Aamaal mein ek Neki likhi jati hai."

"Aur jab koi shakhs Burayi ka iraada karta hai aur kisi wajah se Burayi nahi karta to uske Naama e Aamaal mein koi Gunah nahi likha jata aur agar woh Burayi kar le to phir Khuda ki taraf se use 7 ghante ki mohlat di jati hai. Dayen taraf wala Farishta jo ke Nekiyan likhta hai woh Bayen taraf wale Farishte se jo ke Buraiyyan likhta hai ye kehta hai ke jaldi na karo mumkin hai ke ye shakhs us Burayi ke baad koi aisi Bhalayi kare jo us Burayi ko mita de, kyonki Allah Ta'ala ka Farman hai: 'Yaqeenan Nekiyan Buraiyyon ko mita deti hain."

"Agar Gunah karne ke baad Banda in Alfaaz se Isteghfar kare to uski Burayi nahi likhi jati:

استغفر الله الذي لا إله إلا هو عالم الغيب والشهادة العزيز الحكيم الغفور الرحيم ذاالجلال و الأكرم و اتوب اليه.

"Agar Gunah ke baad 7 ghante guzar jayen aur Insaan is dauran koi Neki na kare aur Isteghfar na kare to phir Neki wala Farishta Burayi likhne wale Farishte se kehta hai: 'Ab is mehroom Bad-bakht ki Burayi likh lo."

(Usoole Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Ghalti aur Khata Insaan ke anjaam ke liye intihai nuqsaandeh aur sharmindgi ka sabab hai aur Ghalti ki talaafi ke liye Neki se badh kar aur koi cheez nahi hai. Neki Insaan ki aisi purani Ghaltiyon ki bhi talaafi kar deti hai jo Naama e Aamaal mein record ho chuki hoti hain, kyonki Allah Ta'ala ka Farman hai (11:114)"

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal hua ke ek Officer apni Najaez kamai (Corruption) se Sadqa deta hai aur Rishtedaron ki madad karta hai aur Hajj karta hai aur kehta hai (11:114)?

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Burayi, Burayi ko khatm nahi karti. Burayi ko hamesha Neki se hi door kiya ja sakta hai. Haan albatta agar uske Maal e Halaal ki Maal e Haraam se aamezish (mix) ho gayi ho aur ye Ilm na ho ke Halaal kitna hai aur Haraam kitna to phir koi mazaeqa (harj) nahi hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَنَّ بِوِلَايَتِكَ تُقْبَلُ الْاَعْمَالُ وَ تُزَكَّى الْاَفْعَالُ وَ تُضَاعَفُ الْحَسَنَاتُ وَ تُمْحَى السَّيِّئَاتُ فَمَنْ جَاۤءَ بِوِلَايَتِكَ وَ اعْتَرَفَ بِاِمَامَتِكَ قُبِلَتْ اَعْمَالُهُ وَ صُدِّقَتْ اَقْوَالُهُ وَ تَضَاعَفَتْ حَسَنَاتُهُ وَ مُحِيَتْ سَيِّئَاتُهُ وَ مَنْ عَدَلَ عَنْ وِلَايَتِكَ وَ جَهِلَ مَعْرِفْتَكَ .......

(Ziyarat Sahebe Amr (atfs) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU

**********************************

         14th Rabiul Akhir 1442

  30th November 2020, Monday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

♦ NAMAZ BURAYI KO DHO DALTI HAI. ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1580)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَأَقِمِ ٱلصَّلَوٰةَ طَرَفَیِ ٱلنَّهَارِ وَزُلَفࣰا مِّنَ ٱلَّیۡلِۚ إِنَّ ٱلۡحَسَنَـٰتِ یُذۡهِبۡنَ ٱلسَّیِّـَٔاتِۚ ذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ ذِكۡرَىٰ لِلذَّ ٰ⁠كِرِینَ *  وَٱصۡبِرۡ فَإِنَّ ٱللَّهَ لَا یُضِیعُ أَجۡرَ ٱلۡمُحۡسِنِینَ.

"Aur Namaz qaem karo Din ke dono siron par aur kuchh Raat guzarne par. Dar haqeeqat Nekiyan Buraiyyon ko door kar deti hain. Ye Khuda ko yaad rakhne walon ke liye yaad dahani hai. Sabr karo, yaqeenan Allah Neki karnewalon ka Ajr (Reward) zaaye (waste) nahi karta."

(Surah Hud: 114 - 115)

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer: (Cont'd)

Imam Baqir (as):

"Din ke do hisson se Maghrib aur Subah ki Namaz murad hai aur 'Kuchh Raat guzarne' se Namaz e Isha murad hai."

(Tehzeebul Ahkam, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Momin jab Raat ke waqt Namaz padhta hai to usse Din ke Gunah mit jate hain."

(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Rasoole Akram (saww):

"Ya Ali! Mujhe Us Zaat ki Qasam Jisne mujhe Haq ke saath Basheer o Nazir bana kar bheja hai, jab tum mein se koi shakhs Wuzu karta hai to uske Aaza ke Gunah jhad jate hain aur jab woh apne Chehre aur Dil ko Khuda ke Huzoor (Namaz mein) le jata hai to jaise hi woh Namaz se farigh hota hai to uske Gunag khatm ho chuke hote hain aur woh Gunahon se yun Paak ho jata hai jaisa abhi Shikm e Maadar se paida hua ho."

'Agar do Namazon ke darmiyan Gunah karta hai to baad wali Namaz uske Gunahon ko khatm kar deti hai."_

"Ya Ali (as)! Namaz e Panchgana ki misal us Naher ki si hai ji kisi ke Darwaze par beh rahi ho, woh shakhs rozana us Naher mein Panch martaba Ghusl kare to kya uske Badan par bhi koi Mail kuchail baqi rahega? Meri Ummat ke liye Namaz e Panchgana (Daily Prayers) bhi isi tarah se hai."

(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Jab Momin Namaz e Shab padhta hai to uske us Din ke Gunah zayel ho (dhul) jate hain.'

(Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Sadiq (as):

"Logon ki baaton se dhoke mein mubtila na ho jana. Tumhare Faraiz tum se hi makhsoos hain aur apna Din idhar udhar ki baaton mein zaaye (waste) na karna, kyonki Farishte tumhari baaten likh rahe hain. Meine Neki se badh kar aur kisi cheez ko nahi dekha jo purane Gunah ko mita dene wali ho. Neki ko kabhi haqeer (negligent) na samajhna. Neki tujhe us maqam par zaroor dikhayi degi jahan use dekh kar tujhe khushi mehsoos hogi aur Burayi ko kabhi haqeer na samajhna, kyonki Burayi tumhe wahan dikhayi degi jahan tujhe intihai pareshani hogi. Allah Ta'ala ka Farman hai (11:114)"

(Kitab Sawabul Amaal, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

.....اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنِّيْ اَسْاَلُكَ بَعْدَ الصَّلٰوةِ وَ التَّسْلِيْمِ اَنْ تُصَلِّيَ عَلٰى مُحَمَّدٍ وَ عَلِيٍّ وَ فَاطِمَةَ وَ الْحَسَنِ وَ الْحُسَيْنِ وَ عَلِيٍّ وَ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ جَعْفَرٍ وَ مُوْسٰى وَ عَلِيٍّ وَ مُحَمَّدٍ وَ عَلِيٍّ وَ الْحَسَنِ وَ الْحُجَّةِ.......

(Zikre Wida Ziyarat Ameerul Momeneen (as) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦ MA'ASHRA - SOCIETY ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1581)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

فَلَوۡلَا كَانَ مِنَ ٱلۡقُرُونِ مِن قَبۡلِكُمۡ أُو۟لُوا۟ بَقِیَّةࣲ یَنۡهَوۡنَ عَنِ ٱلۡفَسَادِ فِی ٱلۡأَرۡضِ إِلَّا قَلِیلࣰا مِّمَّنۡ أَنجَیۡنَا مِنۡهُمۡۗ وَٱتَّبَعَ ٱلَّذِینَ ظَلَمُوا۟ مَاۤ أُتۡرِفُوا۟ فِیهِ وَكَانُوا۟ مُجۡرِمِینَ *  وَمَا كَانَ رَبُّكَ لِیُهۡلِكَ ٱلۡقُرَىٰ بِظُلۡمࣲ وَأَهۡلُهَا مُصۡلِحُونَ.

"Phir kyon na in Qaumo mein jo tum se pehle guzar chuki hain aise Ahle Khair maujood rahe jo logon ko Zameen mein Fasaad barpa karne se rokte? Aise log bahut kam nikle jin ko Hamne in Qaumo mein se bacha liya. Zalim log un cheezon ke maze udate rahe jo unhe farawani ke saath di gayi thin aur woh mujrim the. Tere Rab ka ye dastoor nahi hai ke woh Bastiyon ko Na-Haq karde jab ke unke Bashinde Islah karne wale hain."

(Surah Hud: 116 - 117)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Guzishta Qaumon ka Zikr kar ke Allah ne hame ye sabaq diya ke Woh yun hi Qaumon ko tabah nahi karta. Allah ka Azaab Mujrimon par aata hai, Musleh (Reformers) afraad par nahi.

Ek healthy Society ke liye uske members ka bhi Saleh wa Nek hona zaroori hai warna us mein Fasaad barpa hoga. Society ke bhi ek head/chief hota hai, sabko unka order manna padta hai. Jo follow nahi karta usko Punish kiya jata hai. Agar ek Society mein ye nizam dirhm barham ho jaye aur apne Chief ki baat na maani jaye to Society mein Ikhtelaf hoga aur woh society toot jati hai aur log tabah wa barbad ho jate hain.

Guzishta Qaumen bhi ek Society thi. Allah ne jisko us Society ka chief banaya tha, woh unko follow nahi kar rahe the. Akhir kar Hukumat to Allah ki hai. Woh Uske Azaab se nahi bach sake. Allah ke Numainde ne chaha ke ek Civilised Society Usool o Zabte se chale. Lekin jab aksariyat qanoon todne lagi to woh uncivilised ho gayi aur usko khatm karna zaroori tha taake uske bure asaraat doosri Nek Qaumon par na paden.

👉🏻

Rasoole Khuda (saww):

'Jis Ma'ashre mein Adl o Insaaf ho to Allah us Ma'ashre ko kabhi barbaad nahi karta."

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Agar Qaum e Musa (as) mein Ek giroh aisa hai jo Haq ki Hidayat karta hai aur Haq ke saath insaaf karta hai to Allah ne meri Ummat mein bhi aisa giroh paida kiya hai jaisa ke Usne irshaad farmaya hai, "Hamari Makhlooq mein ek Giroh aisa bhi hai jo Haq ke saath hidayat karta hai aur Haq ke saath insaaf karta hai" (7:181)."

(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain, v3, p477)

🤲🏻

...صَلِّ عَلَيْهِ صَلَاةً نَامِيَةً مُنِيْفَةً زَاكِيَةً تُوْجِبُ لَهُ بِهَا شَفَاعَةَ اُمَمٍ مِنْ خَلْقِكَ وَ قُرُوْنٍ مِنْ بَرَايَاكَ وَ بَلِّغْهُ عَنَّا تَحِيَّةً وَ سَلَامًا.....

(Salwat Imam Musa Kazim (as) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 2nd December 2020, Wednesday

      ♦ EXAM - IMTIHAN ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1582)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلَوۡ شَاۤءَ رَبُّكَ لَجَعَلَ ٱلنَّاسَ أُمَّةࣰ وَ ٰ⁠حِدَةࣰۖ وَلَا یَزَالُونَ مُخۡتَلِفِینَ *  إِلَّا مَن رَّحِمَ رَبُّكَۚ وَلِذَ ٰ⁠لِكَ خَلَقَهُمۡۗ وَتَمَّتۡ كَلِمَةُ رَبِّكَ لَأَمۡلَأَنَّ جَهَنَّمَ مِنَ ٱلۡجِنَّةِ وَٱلنَّاسِ أَجۡمَعِینَ.

"Agar tera Rab chahta to tamam logon ko ek Giroh (Group) bana sakta tha magar woh hamesha Ikhtelaf karte rahenge. In be-Raah Raviyyon se wohi bachenge jin par tere Rab ne Rahem kiya ho aur isi Imtihan o Azmayish ke liye hi to Khuda ne unhe paida kiya hai. Tere Rab ki baat poori ho gayi ke Mein Jahannum ko Jinnat aur Insaano se bhar dunga."

(Surah Hud: 118 - 119)

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇 📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Is Sawal ka jawab ham pehle bhi de chuke hain ke jab Allah ko iska Ilm hi hai to ke log kaisa Amal karenge to phir Duniya mein ye sab naatak kyon? Aisa hi sawal Anbiya aur Aimma (as) ke Ilm e Ghaib aur unki Musibat par hota hai.

In sab ka ek hi jawab hai ke Duniya Examination Hall hai.

👉🏻

Imam Sadiq (as) se is Ayat ke bare sawal kiya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Log Ummat e Waheda (One Nation) the, Allah ne itmaam e Hujjat ke liye Anbiya bheje."

(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

🕌

Imam Baqir (as) se sawal hua ke إِلَّا مَن رَّحِمَ رَبُّكَۚ se murad kaun hain?

Imam (as) ne farmaya:

"Isse hamare Shia murad hain. Allah ne unhe Apni Rehmat ke liye paida kiya hai aur Allah ne apni wus'at ke mutalliq farmaya: 'Ke Meri Rehmat har cheez par Wasee hai.' Jis tarah se Khuda ki Rehmat har cheez se Wasee hai usi tarah se Imam ka Ilm bhi logon ke Ilm par Muheet hai."

Ayat وَلَا یَزَالُونَ مُخۡتَلِفِینَ ke bare mein farmaya:

"Iska mafhoom ye hai ke log Deen mein Ikhtelaf karte rahen albatta woh log isse mustashna (exception) hain jin par Allah ne Rehmat ki hai aur jinhe Rehmat ke liye paida kiya hai. Isse Aale Muhammad (as) aur unke Pairokar murad hain. Allah ne unhe apni Rehmat ke liye paida kiya hai aur woh Deen mein Ikhtelaf nahi karte."

(Usoole Kaafi, Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim Qummi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

Imam Zainul Abedin se bhi same hadis hai, aur farmate hain:

".... Allah ne inhe Pakeeza Teenat se paida kiya hai. Kya tumne Ibrahim (as) ki ye Dua nahi padhi:

"Parwardigar! Is Shaher ko Aman ka Shaher bana aur is mein rehne walon se jo Allah par Imaan laaye use Phalon ka Rizq ata farma:" (2:126)

"Is Dua ka Samar (Phal) ham aur hamare Shia hain."

"Allah ne farmaya:

"Aur jo koi inkaar karega to Mein use chand Din fayda dunga phir Mein use Dozakh ke Azaab ke liye majboor kar dunga." (2:126)

"Isse woh afraad muraad hain Jinhone Nabi ke Wasi ka inkaar kiya hai."

(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكِ يَا مُمْتَحَنَةُ امْتَحَنَكِ الَّذِيْ خَلَقَكِ قَبْلَ اَنْ يَخْلُقَكِ وَ كُنْتِ لِمَا امْتَحَنَكِ بِهِ صَابِرَةً وَ نَحْنُ لَكِ اَوْلِيَاۤءُ مُصَدِّقُوْنَ وَ لِكُلِّ مَا اَتٰى بِهِ اَبُوْكِ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَ اٰلِهِ وَ سَلَّمَ وَ اَتٰى بِهِ....

(Ziyarat-e-Janab e Zehra (sa) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    3rd December 2020, Thursday

♦ LESSONS FROM HISTORY ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1583)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَكُلࣰّا نَّقُصُّ عَلَیۡكَ مِنۡ أَنۢبَاۤءِ ٱلرُّسُلِ مَا نُثَبِّتُ بِهِۦ فُؤَادَكَۚ وَجَاۤءَكَ فِی هَـٰذِهِ ٱلۡحَقُّ وَمَوۡعِظَةࣱ وَذِكۡرَىٰ لِلۡمُؤۡمِنِینَ

"Paighambaron ke ye Qisse Ham Aapko isliye suna rahe hain ke isse Ham tere Dil ko mazboot karen. Inke andar tumko Haqeeqat ka Ilm mila aur Imaan laane walon ko Nasihat aur Bedaari (Awakening) naseeb hui."

(Surah Hud: 120)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Surah ke akher mein Allah Ta'ala is Ayat mein khulasa kiya hai. Chunke is Surah mein Anbiya ke Qisse bayan kiye gaye, Allah Ta'ala ne inke sunane ka maqsad bayan kiya. Ye Qisse koi entertainment ke liye ya Bachcho ko liye farzi kahaniya nahi the, balke ye Haqeeqat par mabni the jinse hamse Sabaq/Lesson liya ja sakta hai. In Qisson ka maqsad tha taak hamara Aqeeda mazboot ho. Yani hamara Aqeeda Haqeeqat par mabni hai, yaha Jhoot fareb ki koi jagah nahi. Ye Qisse sun kar Imaan qawi hota hai, Nasihaten milti hain, soyi hui fitrat jagti hai. Gunahon ki parten hatti hai, Dil Roshan hota hai. Ambiguity, mubham baton ki wazahat ho jati hai, shukook o shubhaat door ho jate hain. Ye Tarikhi waqeaat hain. Mashoor hai History repeats itself. Tarikh dohrati rehti hai. Guzishta Tarikh dekh kar bhi agar ham wohi ghalti karte rahen to ye sarasar bewaqoofi hogi. Hame tarikh se use musbat +ve pehlu ko lena hoga aur - ve aspect se door rehna hoga, ye Aqalmandi hogi.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Rasule Khuda (saww):

"Logo'n mein sabse zyada ghaafil (negligent) wo hai jo Duniya ke badalte haalaat se sabak (lesson) nahi leta."

(Nahjul Fasaha)

🕌

Imam Ali (as):

"Momin duniya ko ibrat (lesson) ki Nigah se dekhta hai aur utni hi ghiza haasil karta hai jiske liye shikam ki zaroorat use majboor karti hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p53)

🤲🏻

اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ وَ عَلٰى اُمِّكَ وَ اَخِيْكَ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ وَ عَلَى الْاَئِمَّةِ مِنْ ذُرِّيَّتِكَ وَ بَنِيْكَ اَشْهَدُ لَقَدْ طَيَّبَ اللّٰهُ بِكَ التُّرَابَ وَ اَوْضَحَ بِكَ الْكِتَابَ وَ جَعَلَكَ وَ اَبَاكَ وَ جَدَّكَ وَ اَخَاكَ وَ بَنِيْكَ عِبْرَةً لِاُوْلِي الْاَلْبَابِ

(Ziyarat Mutlaqa Ameerul Mo'meneen (as) - Mafateeh)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

         18th Rabiul Akhir 1442

     4th December 2020, Friday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ INTEZAAR ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1584)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَقُل لِّلَّذِینَ لَا یُؤۡمِنُونَ ٱعۡمَلُوا۟ عَلَىٰ مَكَانَتِكُمۡ إِنَّا عَـٰمِلُونَ *  وَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنَّا مُنتَظِرُونَ.

"Woh log jo Imaan nahi laate Aap unse keh den ke tum apni jagah reh kar kaam kiye jao ham bhi kaam kar rahe hain. Aur tum Intezaar karo Ham bhi Intezaar kar rahe hain."

(Surah Hud: 121 - 122)

وَیَـٰقَوۡمِ ٱعۡمَلُوا۟ عَلَىٰ مَكَانَتِكُمۡ إِنِّی عَـٰمِلࣱۖ سَوۡفَ تَعۡلَمُونَ مَن یَأۡتِیهِ عَذَابࣱ یُخۡزِیهِ وَمَنۡ هُوَ كَـٰذِبࣱۖ وَٱرۡتَقِبُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُمۡ رَقِیبࣱ

"Aye meri Qaum! Tum apni jagah kaam kiye jao mein bhi amal kar raha hun tum anqareeb jaan loge ke kis par Zillat ka Azaab aata hai aur kaun jhootha hai. Tum bhi intezar karo, mein bhi tumhare saath Intezaar kar raha hun."

(Surah Hud: 93)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

17th Nov 2020 ko hamne (11:93) ki Tafseer post ki thi usi ko wapas repeat kar rahe hain.

Allah Ta'ala ne akhir mein Surah ke akhir mein khulase ke taur par phir se Hazrat Shu'aib (as) ka qaul Aap (saww) se dohraya.

Maqsad ye hai ke Munkarin ko kab Azaab milega aur Azaab kis ke zariye takmeel hoga, iska hame Intezaar hai. Aap (saww) ko is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne dilasa diya aur yehi Khitab Mo'meneen ke liye bhi hai ke Sabr ke saath Intezar karen, wo waqt zaroor aayega jab Allah ki Akhiri Hujjat is sar Zameen par zahoor karegi aur Munkarin o Munafiqin se Ilahi Inteqaam legi.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

Repeat:

Jab Qaume Shu'aib (as) ne apni zor zabardasti dikhayi aur apni baat par ade rahe to Aap (as) ne bhi unko aisa hi jawab diya. Yani ab jo tumhe karna hai karo, tumhe jitni apni taqat lagani hai laga lo. Idhar ham bhi intezaar mein hain, ab dekhte jao kya hota hai. Ye log muqabila kar rahe the Usse jo Maut o Hayat ka Malik hai. Yani ye ek tarah ka Mubahela tha ke dekhte hain Jhoota kaun hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Christian se Mubahela kiya tha ke Jhooton par Allah ki La'anat Barsegi. Lekin un logon ne Panjetan e Paak (as) ko dekh kar hi Mubahela radd kar diya aur Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki baat maan li.

Lekin Qaum-e-Shu'aib (as) par koi asar na hua aur ye challenge qabool kiya.

Ab Aap (as) ko us waqt ka Intezaar tha ke kab ye Azaab in par aayega.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Reza (as) se Sawaal kiya ke kushaysh (Faraj) kab hogi?Aap (as) ne farmaya:

"Kya tum nahi jaante ke Kushayesh ka Intezaar bhi Kushayesh ka ek hissa hai. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ.

"Sabr aur Kushayesh ka Intezaar behtareen cheez hai. Kya tu ne Allah ka ye farman nahi suna:

وَٱرۡتَقِبُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُمۡ رَقِیبࣱ (Hud: 93)

فَٱنتَظِرُوۤا۟ إِنِّی مَعَكُم مِّنَ ٱلۡمُنتَظِرِینَ. (7: 71)

"Lehaza tumhe Sabr se kaam lena chahiye. Hamesha Mayusi ke Waqt hi Kushayesh utarti hai. (Kyonki Shab e Siyah ka khatema hamesha Subah par hua karta hai.)Tumse pehle log tumse bade Sabir the."

& (11:122)

(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)

🤲🏻

اَللّٰهُمَّ اِنْ حَالَ بَيْنِيْ وَ بَيْنَهُ الْمَوْتُ الَّذِيْ جَعَلْتَهُ عَلٰى عِبَادِكَ حَتْمًا مَقْضِيًّا، فَاَخْرِجْنِيْ مِنْ قَبْرِيْ مُؤْتَزِرًا كَفَنِيْ شَاهِرًا سَيْفِيْ مُجَرِّدًا قَنَاتِيْ

(Dua-e-Ahad)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU

**********************************

           19th Rabius Sani 1442

    5th December 2020, Saturday

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             ♦ ILM-E-GHAIB ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (1585)

بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

وَلِلَّهِ غَیۡبُ ٱلسَّمَـٰوَ ٰ⁠تِ وَٱلۡأَرۡضِ وَإِلَیۡهِ یُرۡجَعُ ٱلۡأَمۡرُ كُلُّهُۥ فَٱعۡبُدۡهُ وَتَوَكَّلۡ عَلَیۡهِۚ وَمَا رَبُّكَ بِغَـٰفِلٍ عَمَّا تَعۡمَلُونَ.

"Woh log jo Imaan nahi laate Aap unse keh den ke tum apni jagah reh kar kaam kiye jao ham bhi kaam kar rahe hain. Aur tum Intezaar karo Ham bhi Intezaar kar rahe hain."

(Surah Hud: 123)

📚📖

👉 Tafseer:

Ilm-e-Ghaib Khuda ke paas hai aur Aalim-e-Ghaib bhi wohi hai. Albatta Allah Ta'ala Anbiya o Mursaleen ko jitna Chahta hai utna Ilm-e-Ghaib ata kar deta hai. Makhlooq mein se koi bhi Allah ke Ilm ka ahata nahi kar sakta. Allah ka Ilm Zaati hai aur Hadiyaan e Deen ka Ilm Uska ata kardah hai (bestowed). Isi liye "Aalimul Ghaib" ki Sifat Khuda se makhsoos hai jabke Hadiyaan e Deen "Matlah alal Ghaib" (Informed) hain.

Allah Ta'ala ne Paighambar e Akram (saww) ko Ghaib ke bahut se umoor ki ittela di thi aur Habib e Khuda (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ko ye khabar di aur Hazrat Ali (as) ne apni Aulad ko in ki taleem di. Yehi wajah hai ke Hazrat Ali (as) ne aur unke baad Aimma e Huda (as) ne aane wale waqeaat ki peshingoyi farmayi jo ke harf ba harf sachchi sabit hui.

Maslan:

(1) Hazrat Ali (as) ne Sahebe Zanj ke Fitne ki taraf ishara kiya tha. Ye waqea 255 AH mein Nehre Furat par waqe hua.

(2) Hazrat Ali (as) ne farmaya Marwan ki Hukumat itne der ki hogi jitni der Kutta Paani chaatta hai. Uski hukumat sirf 9 mahine ki thi.

(3) Imam Sadiq (as) ke paas kuchh Aulad e Ali (as) wa Ibne Abbas jama hue aur Mohd bin Abdullah ko Khalifa ke liye propose kiya aur Imam (as) se kaha inki Bai'at karo. Imam (as) ne farmaya:  'Hukumat Ibne Abbas ko milegi aur tumhare dono bete mare jayenge. Baad mein ye sab aisa hi hua.

(4) Imam Reza (as) ne farmaya:' Toos ki Qabr aur Baghdad ki do Qabron par Khuda ki barkat ho.'

Baad mein ye bhi sach hua, Toos mein Aap (as) ki khud ki Qabr aur Baghdad mein unke farzandon ki Qabr.

(5) Raavi ka bayan hai ke mein Kufa se Marv ja raha tha to meri beti ne ek Kapda diya aur kaha ise bech kar mere liye Firoza le aana. Lekin jab ye wahan pahuncha to kharid farokht mein wo kapda bhool gaya. Hazrat Imam Reza (as) ki ziyarat ko pahuncha. Chalte waqt Imam (as) ne usse farmaya us Baste mein wo kapda maujood hai usse Firoza kharid lena. Ye sun kar usne Imam (as) ke hathon ka bosa liya aur farmaya: "Beshak Aap Imam e Barhaq hain."

Ye kuchh waqeaat the jinse pata chalta hain ke Imam (as) Ilm-e-Ghaib rakhte the. Aur bahut se waqeat Kitabon mein darj hain refer karen.

(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!

🙇

Imam Baqir (as):

"Allah Ta'ala ka Ism e Aazam 73 Harfo'n mein hai. Hamare Ahlebait (as) ke paas uske 72 Huroof hain aur ek harf Allah Ta'ala ke paas hai jiski bina par Ilm e Ghaib ko Usne Apni Zaat ke liye pasand farmaya aur Apne hi paas rakha hai. Pas, har qism ki Quwwat o Taaqat bas Usi ke paas hai."

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p916)

🤲🏻

...وَ اَسْاَلُكَ بِاسْمِكَ الْمَخْزُوْنِ فِيْ خَزَاۤئِنِكَ الَّذِيْ اسْتَأْثَرْتَ بِهِ فِيْ عِلْمِ الْغَيْبِ عِنْدَكَ لَمْ يَظْهَرْ عَلَيْهِ اَحَدٌ مِنْ خَلْقِكَ...

(Dua Amal e Shabe Arafa - Mafateeh)
